84//-------------------------------------------------------------------------
85// [SECTION] STB libraries implementation (for stb_truetype and stb_rect_pack)
86//-------------------------------------------------------------------------
87
88// Compile time options:
89//#define IMGUI_STB_NAMESPACE ImStb
90//#define IMGUI_STB_TRUETYPE_FILENAME "my_folder/stb_truetype.h"
91//#define IMGUI_STB_RECT_PACK_FILENAME "my_folder/stb_rect_pack.h"
92//#define IMGUI_DISABLE_STB_TRUETYPE_IMPLEMENTATION
93//#define IMGUI_DISABLE_STB_RECT_PACK_IMPLEMENTATION
94
95#ifdef IMGUI_STB_NAMESPACE
96namespace IMGUI_STB_NAMESPACE
97{
98#endif
99
100#ifdef _MSC_VER
101#pragma warning (push)
102#pragma warning (disable: 4456) // declaration of 'xx' hides previous local declaration
103#pragma warning (disable: 6011) // (stb_rectpack) Dereferencing NULL pointer 'cur->next'.
104#pragma warning (disable: 6385) // (stb_truetype) Reading invalid data from 'buffer': the readable size is '_Old_3`kernel_width' bytes, but '3' bytes may be read.
105#pragma warning (disable: 28182) // (stb_rectpack) Dereferencing NULL pointer. 'cur' contains the same NULL value as 'cur->next' did.
106#endif
107
108#if defined(__clang__)
109#pragma clang diagnostic push
110#pragma clang diagnostic ignored "-Wunused-function" // warning: 'xxxx' defined but not used
111#pragma clang diagnostic ignored "-Wmissing-prototypes"
112#pragma clang diagnostic ignored "-Wimplicit-fallthrough"
113#endif
114
115#if defined(__GNUC__)
116#pragma GCC diagnostic push
117#pragma GCC diagnostic ignored "-Wtype-limits" // warning: comparison is always true due to limited range of data type [-Wtype-limits]
118#pragma GCC diagnostic ignored "-Wimplicit-fallthrough" // warning: this statement may fall through
119#endif
120
121#ifndef STB_RECT_PACK_IMPLEMENTATION // in case the user already have an implementation in the _same_ compilation unit (e.g. unity builds)
122#ifndef IMGUI_DISABLE_STB_RECT_PACK_IMPLEMENTATION // in case the user already have an implementation in another compilation unit
123#define STBRP_STATIC
124#define STBRP_ASSERT(x) do { IM_ASSERT(x); } while (0)
125#define STBRP_SORT ImQsort
126#define STB_RECT_PACK_IMPLEMENTATION
127#endif
128#ifdef IMGUI_STB_RECT_PACK_FILENAME
129#include IMGUI_STB_RECT_PACK_FILENAME
130#else
131#include "imstb_rectpack.h"
132#endif
133#endif
134
135#ifdef IMGUI_ENABLE_STB_TRUETYPE
136#ifndef STB_TRUETYPE_IMPLEMENTATION // in case the user already have an implementation in the _same_ compilation unit (e.g. unity builds)
137#ifndef IMGUI_DISABLE_STB_TRUETYPE_IMPLEMENTATION // in case the user already have an implementation in another compilation unit
138#define STBTT_malloc(x,u) ((void)(u), IM_ALLOC(x))
139#define STBTT_free(x,u) ((void)(u), IM_FREE(x))
140#define STBTT_assert(x) do { IM_ASSERT(x); } while(0)
141#define STBTT_fmod(x,y) ImFmod(x,y)
142#define STBTT_sqrt(x) ImSqrt(x)
143#define STBTT_pow(x,y) ImPow(x,y)
144#define STBTT_fabs(x) ImFabs(x)
145#define STBTT_ifloor(x) ((int)ImFloor(x))
146#define STBTT_iceil(x) ((int)ImCeil(x))
147#define STBTT_strlen(x) ImStrlen(x)
148#define STBTT_STATIC
149#define STB_TRUETYPE_IMPLEMENTATION
150#else
151#define STBTT_DEF extern
152#endif
153#ifdef IMGUI_STB_TRUETYPE_FILENAME
154#include IMGUI_STB_TRUETYPE_FILENAME
155#else
156#include "imstb_truetype.h"
157#endif
158#endif
159#endif // IMGUI_ENABLE_STB_TRUETYPE

163#endif

167#endif

314// Those light colors are better suited with a thicker font than the default one + FrameBorder
315void ImGui::StyleColorsLight(ImGuiStyle* dst)
316{
317 ImGuiStyle* style = dst ? dst : &ImGui::GetStyle();
318 ImVec4* colors = style->Colors;
319
320 colors[ImGuiCol_Text] = ImVec4(0.00f, 0.00f, 0.00f, 1.00f);
321 colors[ImGuiCol_TextDisabled] = ImVec4(0.60f, 0.60f, 0.60f, 1.00f);
322 colors[ImGuiCol_WindowBg] = ImVec4(0.94f, 0.94f, 0.94f, 1.00f);
323 colors[ImGuiCol_ChildBg] = ImVec4(0.00f, 0.00f, 0.00f, 0.00f);
324 colors[ImGuiCol_PopupBg] = ImVec4(1.00f, 1.00f, 1.00f, 0.98f);
325 colors[ImGuiCol_Border] = ImVec4(0.00f, 0.00f, 0.00f, 0.30f);
326 colors[ImGuiCol_BorderShadow] = ImVec4(0.00f, 0.00f, 0.00f, 0.00f);
327 colors[ImGuiCol_FrameBg] = ImVec4(1.00f, 1.00f, 1.00f, 1.00f);
328 colors[ImGuiCol_FrameBgHovered] = ImVec4(0.26f, 0.59f, 0.98f, 0.40f);
329 colors[ImGuiCol_FrameBgActive] = ImVec4(0.26f, 0.59f, 0.98f, 0.67f);
330 colors[ImGuiCol_TitleBg] = ImVec4(0.96f, 0.96f, 0.96f, 1.00f);

381//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
382// [SECTION] ImDrawList
383//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
384
385ImDrawListSharedData::ImDrawListSharedData()
386{
387 memset(this, 0, sizeof(*this));
388 InitialFringeScale = 1.0f;
389 for (int i = 0; i < IM_ARRAYSIZE(ArcFastVtx); i++)
390 {
391 const float a = ((float)i * 2 * IM_PI) / (float)IM_ARRAYSIZE(ArcFastVtx);
392 ArcFastVtx[i] = ImVec2(ImCos(a), ImSin(a));
393 }
394 ArcFastRadiusCutoff = IM_DRAWLIST_CIRCLE_AUTO_SEGMENT_CALC_R(IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX, CircleSegmentMaxError);
395}
396
397void ImDrawListSharedData::SetCircleTessellationMaxError(float max_error)
398{
399 if (CircleSegmentMaxError == max_error)
400 return;
401
402 IM_ASSERT(max_error > 0.0f);
403 CircleSegmentMaxError = max_error;
404 for (int i = 0; i < IM_ARRAYSIZE(CircleSegmentCounts); i++)
405 {
406 const float radius = (float)i;
407 CircleSegmentCounts[i] = (ImU8)((i > 0) ? IM_DRAWLIST_CIRCLE_AUTO_SEGMENT_CALC(radius, CircleSegmentMaxError) : IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX);
408 }
409 ArcFastRadiusCutoff = IM_DRAWLIST_CIRCLE_AUTO_SEGMENT_CALC_R(IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX, CircleSegmentMaxError);
410}
411
412ImDrawList::ImDrawList(ImDrawListSharedData* shared_data)
413{
414 memset(this, 0, sizeof(*this));
415 _Data = shared_data;
416}
417
418ImDrawList::~ImDrawList()
419{
420 _ClearFreeMemory();
421}
422
423// Initialize before use in a new frame. We always have a command ready in the buffer.
424// In the majority of cases, you would want to call PushClipRect() and PushTextureID() after this.
425void ImDrawList::_ResetForNewFrame()
426{
427 // Verify that the ImDrawCmd fields we want to memcmp() are contiguous in memory.
428 IM_STATIC_ASSERT(offsetof(ImDrawCmd, ClipRect) == 0);
429 IM_STATIC_ASSERT(offsetof(ImDrawCmd, TextureId) == sizeof(ImVec4));
430 IM_STATIC_ASSERT(offsetof(ImDrawCmd, VtxOffset) == sizeof(ImVec4) + sizeof(ImTextureID));
431 if (_Splitter._Count > 1)
432 _Splitter.Merge(this);
433
434 CmdBuffer.resize(0);
435 IdxBuffer.resize(0);
436 VtxBuffer.resize(0);
437 Flags = _Data->InitialFlags;
438 memset(&_CmdHeader, 0, sizeof(_CmdHeader));
439 _VtxCurrentIdx = 0;
440 _VtxWritePtr = NULL;
441 _IdxWritePtr = NULL;
442 _ClipRectStack.resize(0);
443 _TextureIdStack.resize(0);
444 _CallbacksDataBuf.resize(0);
445 _Path.resize(0);
446 _Splitter.Clear();
447 CmdBuffer.push_back(ImDrawCmd());
448 _FringeScale = _Data->InitialFringeScale;
449}
450
451void ImDrawList::_ClearFreeMemory()
452{
453 CmdBuffer.clear();
454 IdxBuffer.clear();
455 VtxBuffer.clear();
456 Flags = ImDrawListFlags_None;
457 _VtxCurrentIdx = 0;
458 _VtxWritePtr = NULL;
459 _IdxWritePtr = NULL;
460 _ClipRectStack.clear();
461 _TextureIdStack.clear();
462 _CallbacksDataBuf.clear();
463 _Path.clear();
464 _Splitter.ClearFreeMemory();
465}
466
467ImDrawList* ImDrawList::CloneOutput() const
468{
469 ImDrawList* dst = IM_NEW(ImDrawList(_Data));
470 dst->CmdBuffer = CmdBuffer;
471 dst->IdxBuffer = IdxBuffer;
472 dst->VtxBuffer = VtxBuffer;
473 dst->Flags = Flags;
474 return dst;
475}
476
477void ImDrawList::AddDrawCmd()
478{
479 ImDrawCmd draw_cmd;
480 draw_cmd.ClipRect = _CmdHeader.ClipRect; // Same as calling ImDrawCmd_HeaderCopy()
481 draw_cmd.TextureId = _CmdHeader.TextureId;
482 draw_cmd.VtxOffset = _CmdHeader.VtxOffset;
483 draw_cmd.IdxOffset = IdxBuffer.Size;
484
485 IM_ASSERT(draw_cmd.ClipRect.x <= draw_cmd.ClipRect.z && draw_cmd.ClipRect.y <= draw_cmd.ClipRect.w);
486 CmdBuffer.push_back(draw_cmd);
487}
488
489// Pop trailing draw command (used before merging or presenting to user)
490// Note that this leaves the ImDrawList in a state unfit for further commands, as most code assume that CmdBuffer.Size > 0 && CmdBuffer.back().UserCallback == NULL
491void ImDrawList::_PopUnusedDrawCmd()
492{
493 while (CmdBuffer.Size > 0)
494 {
495 ImDrawCmd* curr_cmd = &CmdBuffer.Data[CmdBuffer.Size - 1];
496 if (curr_cmd->ElemCount != 0 || curr_cmd->UserCallback != NULL)
497 return;// break;
498 CmdBuffer.pop_back();
499 }
500}
501
502void ImDrawList::AddCallback(ImDrawCallback callback, void* userdata, size_t userdata_size)
503{
504 IM_ASSERT_PARANOID(CmdBuffer.Size > 0);
505 ImDrawCmd* curr_cmd = &CmdBuffer.Data[CmdBuffer.Size - 1];
506 IM_ASSERT(curr_cmd->UserCallback == NULL);
507 if (curr_cmd->ElemCount != 0)
508 {
509 AddDrawCmd();
510 curr_cmd = &CmdBuffer.Data[CmdBuffer.Size - 1];
511 }
512
513 curr_cmd->UserCallback = callback;
514 if (userdata_size == 0)
515 {
516 // Store user data directly in command (no indirection)
517 curr_cmd->UserCallbackData = userdata;
518 curr_cmd->UserCallbackDataSize = 0;
519 curr_cmd->UserCallbackDataOffset = -1;
520 }
521 else
522 {
523 // Copy and store user data in a buffer
524 IM_ASSERT(userdata != NULL);
525 IM_ASSERT(userdata_size < (1u << 31));
526 curr_cmd->UserCallbackData = NULL; // Will be resolved during Render()
527 curr_cmd->UserCallbackDataSize = (int)userdata_size;
528 curr_cmd->UserCallbackDataOffset = _CallbacksDataBuf.Size;
529 _CallbacksDataBuf.resize(_CallbacksDataBuf.Size + (int)userdata_size);
530 memcpy(_CallbacksDataBuf.Data + (size_t)curr_cmd->UserCallbackDataOffset, userdata, userdata_size);
531 }
532
533 AddDrawCmd(); // Force a new command after us (see comment below)
534}
535
536// Compare ClipRect, TextureId and VtxOffset with a single memcmp()
537#define ImDrawCmd_HeaderSize (offsetof(ImDrawCmd, VtxOffset) + sizeof(unsigned int))
538#define ImDrawCmd_HeaderCompare(CMD_LHS, CMD_RHS) (memcmp(CMD_LHS, CMD_RHS, ImDrawCmd_HeaderSize)) // Compare ClipRect, TextureId, VtxOffset
539#define ImDrawCmd_HeaderCopy(CMD_DST, CMD_SRC) (memcpy(CMD_DST, CMD_SRC, ImDrawCmd_HeaderSize)) // Copy ClipRect, TextureId, VtxOffset
540#define ImDrawCmd_AreSequentialIdxOffset(CMD_0, CMD_1) (CMD_0->IdxOffset + CMD_0->ElemCount == CMD_1->IdxOffset)
541
542// Try to merge two last draw commands
543void ImDrawList::_TryMergeDrawCmds()
544{
545 IM_ASSERT_PARANOID(CmdBuffer.Size > 0);
546 ImDrawCmd* curr_cmd = &CmdBuffer.Data[CmdBuffer.Size - 1];
547 ImDrawCmd* prev_cmd = curr_cmd - 1;
548 if (ImDrawCmd_HeaderCompare(curr_cmd, prev_cmd) == 0 && ImDrawCmd_AreSequentialIdxOffset(prev_cmd, curr_cmd) && curr_cmd->UserCallback == NULL && prev_cmd->UserCallback == NULL)
549 {
550 prev_cmd->ElemCount += curr_cmd->ElemCount;
551 CmdBuffer.pop_back();
552 }
553}
554
555// Our scheme may appears a bit unusual, basically we want the most-common calls AddLine AddRect etc. to not have to perform any check so we always have a command ready in the stack.
556// The cost of figuring out if a new command has to be added or if we can merge is paid in those Update** functions only.
557void ImDrawList::_OnChangedClipRect()
558{
559 // If current command is used with different settings we need to add a new command
560 IM_ASSERT_PARANOID(CmdBuffer.Size > 0);
561 ImDrawCmd* curr_cmd = &CmdBuffer.Data[CmdBuffer.Size - 1];
562 if (curr_cmd->ElemCount != 0 && memcmp(&curr_cmd->ClipRect, &_CmdHeader.ClipRect, sizeof(ImVec4)) != 0)
563 {
564 AddDrawCmd();
565 return;
566 }
567 IM_ASSERT(curr_cmd->UserCallback == NULL);
568
569 // Try to merge with previous command if it matches, else use current command
570 ImDrawCmd* prev_cmd = curr_cmd - 1;
571 if (curr_cmd->ElemCount == 0 && CmdBuffer.Size > 1 && ImDrawCmd_HeaderCompare(&_CmdHeader, prev_cmd) == 0 && ImDrawCmd_AreSequentialIdxOffset(prev_cmd, curr_cmd) && prev_cmd->UserCallback == NULL)
572 {
573 CmdBuffer.pop_back();
574 return;
575 }
576 curr_cmd->ClipRect = _CmdHeader.ClipRect;
577}
578
579void ImDrawList::_OnChangedTextureID()
580{
581 // If current command is used with different settings we need to add a new command
582 IM_ASSERT_PARANOID(CmdBuffer.Size > 0);
583 ImDrawCmd* curr_cmd = &CmdBuffer.Data[CmdBuffer.Size - 1];
584 if (curr_cmd->ElemCount != 0 && curr_cmd->TextureId != _CmdHeader.TextureId)
585 {
586 AddDrawCmd();
587 return;
588 }
589 IM_ASSERT(curr_cmd->UserCallback == NULL);
590
591 // Try to merge with previous command if it matches, else use current command
592 ImDrawCmd* prev_cmd = curr_cmd - 1;
593 if (curr_cmd->ElemCount == 0 && CmdBuffer.Size > 1 && ImDrawCmd_HeaderCompare(&_CmdHeader, prev_cmd) == 0 && ImDrawCmd_AreSequentialIdxOffset(prev_cmd, curr_cmd) && prev_cmd->UserCallback == NULL)
594 {
595 CmdBuffer.pop_back();
596 return;
597 }
598 curr_cmd->TextureId = _CmdHeader.TextureId;
599}
600
601void ImDrawList::_OnChangedVtxOffset()
602{
603 // We don't need to compare curr_cmd->VtxOffset != _CmdHeader.VtxOffset because we know it'll be different at the time we call this.
604 _VtxCurrentIdx = 0;
605 IM_ASSERT_PARANOID(CmdBuffer.Size > 0);
606 ImDrawCmd* curr_cmd = &CmdBuffer.Data[CmdBuffer.Size - 1];
607 //IM_ASSERT(curr_cmd->VtxOffset != _CmdHeader.VtxOffset); // See #3349
608 if (curr_cmd->ElemCount != 0)
609 {
610 AddDrawCmd();
611 return;
612 }
613 IM_ASSERT(curr_cmd->UserCallback == NULL);
614 curr_cmd->VtxOffset = _CmdHeader.VtxOffset;
615}
616
617int ImDrawList::_CalcCircleAutoSegmentCount(float radius) const
618{
619 // Automatic segment count
620 const int radius_idx = (int)(radius + 0.999999f); // ceil to never reduce accuracy
621 if (radius_idx >= 0 && radius_idx < IM_ARRAYSIZE(_Data->CircleSegmentCounts))
622 return _Data->CircleSegmentCounts[radius_idx]; // Use cached value
623 else
624 return IM_DRAWLIST_CIRCLE_AUTO_SEGMENT_CALC(radius, _Data->CircleSegmentMaxError);
625}
626
627// Render-level scissoring. This is passed down to your render function but not used for CPU-side coarse clipping. Prefer using higher-level ImGui::PushClipRect() to affect logic (hit-testing and widget culling)
628void ImDrawList::PushClipRect(const ImVec2& cr_min, const ImVec2& cr_max, bool intersect_with_current_clip_rect)
629{
630 ImVec4 cr(cr_min.x, cr_min.y, cr_max.x, cr_max.y);
631 if (intersect_with_current_clip_rect)
632 {
633 ImVec4 current = _CmdHeader.ClipRect;
634 if (cr.x < current.x) cr.x = current.x;
635 if (cr.y < current.y) cr.y = current.y;
636 if (cr.z > current.z) cr.z = current.z;
637 if (cr.w > current.w) cr.w = current.w;
638 }
639 cr.z = ImMax(cr.x, cr.z);
640 cr.w = ImMax(cr.y, cr.w);
641
642 _ClipRectStack.push_back(cr);
643 _CmdHeader.ClipRect = cr;
644 _OnChangedClipRect();
645}
646
647void ImDrawList::PushClipRectFullScreen()
648{
649 PushClipRect(ImVec2(_Data->ClipRectFullscreen.x, _Data->ClipRectFullscreen.y), ImVec2(_Data->ClipRectFullscreen.z, _Data->ClipRectFullscreen.w));
650}
651
652void ImDrawList::PopClipRect()
653{
654 _ClipRectStack.pop_back();
655 _CmdHeader.ClipRect = (_ClipRectStack.Size == 0) ? _Data->ClipRectFullscreen : _ClipRectStack.Data[_ClipRectStack.Size - 1];
656 _OnChangedClipRect();
657}
658
659void ImDrawList::PushTextureID(ImTextureID texture_id)
660{
661 _TextureIdStack.push_back(texture_id);
662 _CmdHeader.TextureId = texture_id;
663 _OnChangedTextureID();
664}
665
666void ImDrawList::PopTextureID()
667{
668 _TextureIdStack.pop_back();
669 _CmdHeader.TextureId = (_TextureIdStack.Size == 0) ? (ImTextureID)NULL : _TextureIdStack.Data[_TextureIdStack.Size - 1];
670 _OnChangedTextureID();
671}
672
673// This is used by ImGui::PushFont()/PopFont(). It works because we never use _TextureIdStack[] elsewhere than in PushTextureID()/PopTextureID().
674void ImDrawList::_SetTextureID(ImTextureID texture_id)
675{
676 if (_CmdHeader.TextureId == texture_id)
677 return;
678 _CmdHeader.TextureId = texture_id;
679 _OnChangedTextureID();
680}
681
682// Reserve space for a number of vertices and indices.
683// You must finish filling your reserved data before calling PrimReserve() again, as it may reallocate or
684// submit the intermediate results. PrimUnreserve() can be used to release unused allocations.
685void ImDrawList::PrimReserve(int idx_count, int vtx_count)
686{
687 // Large mesh support (when enabled)
688 IM_ASSERT_PARANOID(idx_count >= 0 && vtx_count >= 0);
689 if (sizeof(ImDrawIdx) == 2 && (_VtxCurrentIdx + vtx_count >= (1 << 16)) && (Flags & ImDrawListFlags_AllowVtxOffset))
690 {
691 // FIXME: In theory we should be testing that vtx_count <64k here.
692 // In practice, RenderText() relies on reserving ahead for a worst case scenario so it is currently useful for us
693 // to not make that check until we rework the text functions to handle clipping and large horizontal lines better.
694 _CmdHeader.VtxOffset = VtxBuffer.Size;
695 _OnChangedVtxOffset();
696 }
697
698 ImDrawCmd* draw_cmd = &CmdBuffer.Data[CmdBuffer.Size - 1];
699 draw_cmd->ElemCount += idx_count;
700
701 int vtx_buffer_old_size = VtxBuffer.Size;
702 VtxBuffer.resize(vtx_buffer_old_size + vtx_count);
703 _VtxWritePtr = VtxBuffer.Data + vtx_buffer_old_size;
704
705 int idx_buffer_old_size = IdxBuffer.Size;
706 IdxBuffer.resize(idx_buffer_old_size + idx_count);
707 _IdxWritePtr = IdxBuffer.Data + idx_buffer_old_size;
708}
709
710// Release the number of reserved vertices/indices from the end of the last reservation made with PrimReserve().
711void ImDrawList::PrimUnreserve(int idx_count, int vtx_count)
712{
713 IM_ASSERT_PARANOID(idx_count >= 0 && vtx_count >= 0);
714
715 ImDrawCmd* draw_cmd = &CmdBuffer.Data[CmdBuffer.Size - 1];
716 draw_cmd->ElemCount -= idx_count;
717 VtxBuffer.shrink(VtxBuffer.Size - vtx_count);
718 IdxBuffer.shrink(IdxBuffer.Size - idx_count);
719}
720
721// Fully unrolled with inline call to keep our debug builds decently fast.
722void ImDrawList::PrimRect(const ImVec2& a, const ImVec2& c, ImU32 col)
723{
724 ImVec2 b(c.x, a.y), d(a.x, c.y), uv(_Data->TexUvWhitePixel);
725 ImDrawIdx idx = (ImDrawIdx)_VtxCurrentIdx;
726 _IdxWritePtr[0] = idx; _IdxWritePtr[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx+1); _IdxWritePtr[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx+2);
727 _IdxWritePtr[3] = idx; _IdxWritePtr[4] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx+2); _IdxWritePtr[5] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx+3);
728 _VtxWritePtr[0].pos = a; _VtxWritePtr[0].uv = uv; _VtxWritePtr[0].col = col;
729 _VtxWritePtr[1].pos = b; _VtxWritePtr[1].uv = uv; _VtxWritePtr[1].col = col;
730 _VtxWritePtr[2].pos = c; _VtxWritePtr[2].uv = uv; _VtxWritePtr[2].col = col;
731 _VtxWritePtr[3].pos = d; _VtxWritePtr[3].uv = uv; _VtxWritePtr[3].col = col;
732 _VtxWritePtr += 4;
733 _VtxCurrentIdx += 4;
734 _IdxWritePtr += 6;
735}
736
737void ImDrawList::PrimRectUV(const ImVec2& a, const ImVec2& c, const ImVec2& uv_a, const ImVec2& uv_c, ImU32 col)
738{
739 ImVec2 b(c.x, a.y), d(a.x, c.y), uv_b(uv_c.x, uv_a.y), uv_d(uv_a.x, uv_c.y);
740 ImDrawIdx idx = (ImDrawIdx)_VtxCurrentIdx;
741 _IdxWritePtr[0] = idx; _IdxWritePtr[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx+1); _IdxWritePtr[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx+2);
742 _IdxWritePtr[3] = idx; _IdxWritePtr[4] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx+2); _IdxWritePtr[5] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx+3);
743 _VtxWritePtr[0].pos = a; _VtxWritePtr[0].uv = uv_a; _VtxWritePtr[0].col = col;
744 _VtxWritePtr[1].pos = b; _VtxWritePtr[1].uv = uv_b; _VtxWritePtr[1].col = col;
745 _VtxWritePtr[2].pos = c; _VtxWritePtr[2].uv = uv_c; _VtxWritePtr[2].col = col;
746 _VtxWritePtr[3].pos = d; _VtxWritePtr[3].uv = uv_d; _VtxWritePtr[3].col = col;
747 _VtxWritePtr += 4;
748 _VtxCurrentIdx += 4;
749 _IdxWritePtr += 6;
750}
751
752void ImDrawList::PrimQuadUV(const ImVec2& a, const ImVec2& b, const ImVec2& c, const ImVec2& d, const ImVec2& uv_a, const ImVec2& uv_b, const ImVec2& uv_c, const ImVec2& uv_d, ImU32 col)
753{
754 ImDrawIdx idx = (ImDrawIdx)_VtxCurrentIdx;
755 _IdxWritePtr[0] = idx; _IdxWritePtr[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx+1); _IdxWritePtr[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx+2);
756 _IdxWritePtr[3] = idx; _IdxWritePtr[4] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx+2); _IdxWritePtr[5] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx+3);
757 _VtxWritePtr[0].pos = a; _VtxWritePtr[0].uv = uv_a; _VtxWritePtr[0].col = col;
758 _VtxWritePtr[1].pos = b; _VtxWritePtr[1].uv = uv_b; _VtxWritePtr[1].col = col;
759 _VtxWritePtr[2].pos = c; _VtxWritePtr[2].uv = uv_c; _VtxWritePtr[2].col = col;
760 _VtxWritePtr[3].pos = d; _VtxWritePtr[3].uv = uv_d; _VtxWritePtr[3].col = col;
761 _VtxWritePtr += 4;
762 _VtxCurrentIdx += 4;
763 _IdxWritePtr += 6;
764}
765
766// On AddPolyline() and AddConvexPolyFilled() we intentionally avoid using ImVec2 and superfluous function calls to optimize debug/non-inlined builds.
767// - Those macros expects l-values and need to be used as their own statement.
768// - Those macros are intentionally not surrounded by the 'do {} while (0)' idiom because even that translates to runtime with debug compilers.
769#define IM_NORMALIZE2F_OVER_ZERO(VX,VY) { float d2 = VX*VX + VY*VY; if (d2 > 0.0f) { float inv_len = ImRsqrt(d2); VX *= inv_len; VY *= inv_len; } } (void)0
770#define IM_FIXNORMAL2F_MAX_INVLEN2 100.0f // 500.0f (see #4053, #3366)
771#define IM_FIXNORMAL2F(VX,VY) { float d2 = VX*VX + VY*VY; if (d2 > 0.000001f) { float inv_len2 = 1.0f / d2; if (inv_len2 > IM_FIXNORMAL2F_MAX_INVLEN2) inv_len2 = IM_FIXNORMAL2F_MAX_INVLEN2; VX *= inv_len2; VY *= inv_len2; } } (void)0
772
773// TODO: Thickness anti-aliased lines cap are missing their AA fringe.
774// We avoid using the ImVec2 math operators here to reduce cost to a minimum for debug/non-inlined builds.
775void ImDrawList::AddPolyline(const ImVec2* points, const int points_count, ImU32 col, ImDrawFlags flags, float thickness)
776{
777 if (points_count < 2 || (col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0)
778 return;
779
780 const bool closed = (flags & ImDrawFlags_Closed) != 0;
781 const ImVec2 opaque_uv = _Data->TexUvWhitePixel;
782 const int count = closed ? points_count : points_count - 1; // The number of line segments we need to draw
783 const bool thick_line = (thickness > _FringeScale);
784
785 if (Flags & ImDrawListFlags_AntiAliasedLines)
786 {
787 // Anti-aliased stroke
788 const float AA_SIZE = _FringeScale;
789 const ImU32 col_trans = col & ~IM_COL32_A_MASK;
790
791 // Thicknesses <1.0 should behave like thickness 1.0
792 thickness = ImMax(thickness, 1.0f);
793 const int integer_thickness = (int)thickness;
794 const float fractional_thickness = thickness - integer_thickness;
795
796 // Do we want to draw this line using a texture?
797 // - For now, only draw integer-width lines using textures to avoid issues with the way scaling occurs, could be improved.
798 // - If AA_SIZE is not 1.0f we cannot use the texture path.
799 const bool use_texture = (Flags & ImDrawListFlags_AntiAliasedLinesUseTex) && (integer_thickness < IM_DRAWLIST_TEX_LINES_WIDTH_MAX) && (fractional_thickness <= 0.00001f) && (AA_SIZE == 1.0f);
800
801 // We should never hit this, because NewFrame() doesn't set ImDrawListFlags_AntiAliasedLinesUseTex unless ImFontAtlasFlags_NoBakedLines is off
802 IM_ASSERT_PARANOID(!use_texture || !(_Data->Font->ContainerAtlas->Flags & ImFontAtlasFlags_NoBakedLines));
803
804 const int idx_count = use_texture ? (count * 6) : (thick_line ? count * 18 : count * 12);
805 const int vtx_count = use_texture ? (points_count * 2) : (thick_line ? points_count * 4 : points_count * 3);
806 PrimReserve(idx_count, vtx_count);
807
808 // Temporary buffer
809 // The first <points_count> items are normals at each line point, then after that there are either 2 or 4 temp points for each line point
810 _Data->TempBuffer.reserve_discard(points_count * ((use_texture || !thick_line) ? 3 : 5));
811 ImVec2* temp_normals = _Data->TempBuffer.Data;
812 ImVec2* temp_points = temp_normals + points_count;
813
814 // Calculate normals (tangents) for each line segment
815 for (int i1 = 0; i1 < count; i1++)
816 {
817 const int i2 = (i1 + 1) == points_count ? 0 : i1 + 1;
818 float dx = points[i2].x - points[i1].x;
819 float dy = points[i2].y - points[i1].y;
820 IM_NORMALIZE2F_OVER_ZERO(dx, dy);
821 temp_normals[i1].x = dy;
822 temp_normals[i1].y = -dx;
823 }
824 if (!closed)
825 temp_normals[points_count - 1] = temp_normals[points_count - 2];
826
827 // If we are drawing a one-pixel-wide line without a texture, or a textured line of any width, we only need 2 or 3 vertices per point
828 if (use_texture || !thick_line)
829 {
830 // [PATH 1] Texture-based lines (thick or non-thick)
831 // [PATH 2] Non texture-based lines (non-thick)
832
833 // The width of the geometry we need to draw - this is essentially <thickness> pixels for the line itself, plus "one pixel" for AA.
834 // - In the texture-based path, we don't use AA_SIZE here because the +1 is tied to the generated texture
835 // (see ImFontAtlasBuildRenderLinesTexData() function), and so alternate values won't work without changes to that code.
836 // - In the non texture-based paths, we would allow AA_SIZE to potentially be != 1.0f with a patch (e.g. fringe_scale patch to
837 // allow scaling geometry while preserving one-screen-pixel AA fringe).
838 const float half_draw_size = use_texture ? ((thickness * 0.5f) + 1) : AA_SIZE;
839
840 // If line is not closed, the first and last points need to be generated differently as there are no normals to blend
841 if (!closed)
842 {
843 temp_points[0] = points[0] + temp_normals[0] * half_draw_size;
844 temp_points[1] = points[0] - temp_normals[0] * half_draw_size;
845 temp_points[(points_count-1)*2+0] = points[points_count-1] + temp_normals[points_count-1] * half_draw_size;
846 temp_points[(points_count-1)*2+1] = points[points_count-1] - temp_normals[points_count-1] * half_draw_size;
847 }
848
849 // Generate the indices to form a number of triangles for each line segment, and the vertices for the line edges
850 // This takes points n and n+1 and writes into n+1, with the first point in a closed line being generated from the final one (as n+1 wraps)
851 // FIXME-OPT: Merge the different loops, possibly remove the temporary buffer.
852 unsigned int idx1 = _VtxCurrentIdx; // Vertex index for start of line segment
853 for (int i1 = 0; i1 < count; i1++) // i1 is the first point of the line segment
854 {
855 const int i2 = (i1 + 1) == points_count ? 0 : i1 + 1; // i2 is the second point of the line segment
856 const unsigned int idx2 = ((i1 + 1) == points_count) ? _VtxCurrentIdx : (idx1 + (use_texture ? 2 : 3)); // Vertex index for end of segment
857
858 // Average normals
859 float dm_x = (temp_normals[i1].x + temp_normals[i2].x) * 0.5f;
860 float dm_y = (temp_normals[i1].y + temp_normals[i2].y) * 0.5f;
861 IM_FIXNORMAL2F(dm_x, dm_y);
862 dm_x *= half_draw_size; // dm_x, dm_y are offset to the outer edge of the AA area
863 dm_y *= half_draw_size;
864
865 // Add temporary vertices for the outer edges
866 ImVec2* out_vtx = &temp_points[i2 * 2];
867 out_vtx[0].x = points[i2].x + dm_x;
868 out_vtx[0].y = points[i2].y + dm_y;
869 out_vtx[1].x = points[i2].x - dm_x;
870 out_vtx[1].y = points[i2].y - dm_y;
871
872 if (use_texture)
873 {
874 // Add indices for two triangles
875 _IdxWritePtr[0] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 0); _IdxWritePtr[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 0); _IdxWritePtr[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 1); // Right tri
876 _IdxWritePtr[3] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 1); _IdxWritePtr[4] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 1); _IdxWritePtr[5] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 0); // Left tri
877 _IdxWritePtr += 6;
878 }
879 else
880 {
881 // Add indexes for four triangles
882 _IdxWritePtr[0] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 0); _IdxWritePtr[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 0); _IdxWritePtr[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 2); // Right tri 1
883 _IdxWritePtr[3] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 2); _IdxWritePtr[4] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 2); _IdxWritePtr[5] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 0); // Right tri 2
884 _IdxWritePtr[6] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 1); _IdxWritePtr[7] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 1); _IdxWritePtr[8] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 0); // Left tri 1
885 _IdxWritePtr[9] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 0); _IdxWritePtr[10] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 0); _IdxWritePtr[11] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 1); // Left tri 2
886 _IdxWritePtr += 12;
887 }
888
889 idx1 = idx2;
890 }
891
892 // Add vertices for each point on the line
893 if (use_texture)
894 {
895 // If we're using textures we only need to emit the left/right edge vertices
896 ImVec4 tex_uvs = _Data->TexUvLines[integer_thickness];
897 /*if (fractional_thickness != 0.0f) // Currently always zero when use_texture==false!
898 {
899 const ImVec4 tex_uvs_1 = _Data->TexUvLines[integer_thickness + 1];
900 tex_uvs.x = tex_uvs.x + (tex_uvs_1.x - tex_uvs.x) * fractional_thickness; // inlined ImLerp()
901 tex_uvs.y = tex_uvs.y + (tex_uvs_1.y - tex_uvs.y) * fractional_thickness;
902 tex_uvs.z = tex_uvs.z + (tex_uvs_1.z - tex_uvs.z) * fractional_thickness;
903 tex_uvs.w = tex_uvs.w + (tex_uvs_1.w - tex_uvs.w) * fractional_thickness;
904 }*/
905 ImVec2 tex_uv0(tex_uvs.x, tex_uvs.y);
906 ImVec2 tex_uv1(tex_uvs.z, tex_uvs.w);
907 for (int i = 0; i < points_count; i++)
908 {
909 _VtxWritePtr[0].pos = temp_points[i * 2 + 0]; _VtxWritePtr[0].uv = tex_uv0; _VtxWritePtr[0].col = col; // Left-side outer edge
910 _VtxWritePtr[1].pos = temp_points[i * 2 + 1]; _VtxWritePtr[1].uv = tex_uv1; _VtxWritePtr[1].col = col; // Right-side outer edge
911 _VtxWritePtr += 2;
912 }
913 }
914 else
915 {
916 // If we're not using a texture, we need the center vertex as well
917 for (int i = 0; i < points_count; i++)
918 {
919 _VtxWritePtr[0].pos = points[i]; _VtxWritePtr[0].uv = opaque_uv; _VtxWritePtr[0].col = col; // Center of line
920 _VtxWritePtr[1].pos = temp_points[i * 2 + 0]; _VtxWritePtr[1].uv = opaque_uv; _VtxWritePtr[1].col = col_trans; // Left-side outer edge
921 _VtxWritePtr[2].pos = temp_points[i * 2 + 1]; _VtxWritePtr[2].uv = opaque_uv; _VtxWritePtr[2].col = col_trans; // Right-side outer edge
922 _VtxWritePtr += 3;
923 }
924 }
925 }
926 else
927 {
928 // [PATH 2] Non texture-based lines (thick): we need to draw the solid line core and thus require four vertices per point
929 const float half_inner_thickness = (thickness - AA_SIZE) * 0.5f;
930
931 // If line is not closed, the first and last points need to be generated differently as there are no normals to blend
932 if (!closed)
933 {
934 const int points_last = points_count - 1;
935 temp_points[0] = points[0] + temp_normals[0] * (half_inner_thickness + AA_SIZE);
936 temp_points[1] = points[0] + temp_normals[0] * (half_inner_thickness);
937 temp_points[2] = points[0] - temp_normals[0] * (half_inner_thickness);
938 temp_points[3] = points[0] - temp_normals[0] * (half_inner_thickness + AA_SIZE);
939 temp_points[points_last * 4 + 0] = points[points_last] + temp_normals[points_last] * (half_inner_thickness + AA_SIZE);
940 temp_points[points_last * 4 + 1] = points[points_last] + temp_normals[points_last] * (half_inner_thickness);
941 temp_points[points_last * 4 + 2] = points[points_last] - temp_normals[points_last] * (half_inner_thickness);
942 temp_points[points_last * 4 + 3] = points[points_last] - temp_normals[points_last] * (half_inner_thickness + AA_SIZE);
943 }
944
945 // Generate the indices to form a number of triangles for each line segment, and the vertices for the line edges
946 // This takes points n and n+1 and writes into n+1, with the first point in a closed line being generated from the final one (as n+1 wraps)
947 // FIXME-OPT: Merge the different loops, possibly remove the temporary buffer.
948 unsigned int idx1 = _VtxCurrentIdx; // Vertex index for start of line segment
949 for (int i1 = 0; i1 < count; i1++) // i1 is the first point of the line segment
950 {
951 const int i2 = (i1 + 1) == points_count ? 0 : (i1 + 1); // i2 is the second point of the line segment
952 const unsigned int idx2 = (i1 + 1) == points_count ? _VtxCurrentIdx : (idx1 + 4); // Vertex index for end of segment
953
954 // Average normals
955 float dm_x = (temp_normals[i1].x + temp_normals[i2].x) * 0.5f;
956 float dm_y = (temp_normals[i1].y + temp_normals[i2].y) * 0.5f;
957 IM_FIXNORMAL2F(dm_x, dm_y);
958 float dm_out_x = dm_x * (half_inner_thickness + AA_SIZE);
959 float dm_out_y = dm_y * (half_inner_thickness + AA_SIZE);
960 float dm_in_x = dm_x * half_inner_thickness;
961 float dm_in_y = dm_y * half_inner_thickness;
962
963 // Add temporary vertices
964 ImVec2* out_vtx = &temp_points[i2 * 4];
965 out_vtx[0].x = points[i2].x + dm_out_x;
966 out_vtx[0].y = points[i2].y + dm_out_y;
967 out_vtx[1].x = points[i2].x + dm_in_x;
968 out_vtx[1].y = points[i2].y + dm_in_y;
969 out_vtx[2].x = points[i2].x - dm_in_x;
970 out_vtx[2].y = points[i2].y - dm_in_y;
971 out_vtx[3].x = points[i2].x - dm_out_x;
972 out_vtx[3].y = points[i2].y - dm_out_y;
973
974 // Add indexes
975 _IdxWritePtr[0] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 1); _IdxWritePtr[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 1); _IdxWritePtr[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 2);
976 _IdxWritePtr[3] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 2); _IdxWritePtr[4] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 2); _IdxWritePtr[5] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 1);
977 _IdxWritePtr[6] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 1); _IdxWritePtr[7] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 1); _IdxWritePtr[8] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 0);
978 _IdxWritePtr[9] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 0); _IdxWritePtr[10] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 0); _IdxWritePtr[11] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 1);
979 _IdxWritePtr[12] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 2); _IdxWritePtr[13] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 2); _IdxWritePtr[14] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 3);
980 _IdxWritePtr[15] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 3); _IdxWritePtr[16] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 3); _IdxWritePtr[17] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 2);
981 _IdxWritePtr += 18;
982
983 idx1 = idx2;
984 }
985
986 // Add vertices
987 for (int i = 0; i < points_count; i++)
988 {
989 _VtxWritePtr[0].pos = temp_points[i * 4 + 0]; _VtxWritePtr[0].uv = opaque_uv; _VtxWritePtr[0].col = col_trans;
990 _VtxWritePtr[1].pos = temp_points[i * 4 + 1]; _VtxWritePtr[1].uv = opaque_uv; _VtxWritePtr[1].col = col;
991 _VtxWritePtr[2].pos = temp_points[i * 4 + 2]; _VtxWritePtr[2].uv = opaque_uv; _VtxWritePtr[2].col = col;
992 _VtxWritePtr[3].pos = temp_points[i * 4 + 3]; _VtxWritePtr[3].uv = opaque_uv; _VtxWritePtr[3].col = col_trans;
993 _VtxWritePtr += 4;
994 }
995 }
996 _VtxCurrentIdx += (ImDrawIdx)vtx_count;
997 }
998 else
999 {
1000 // [PATH 4] Non texture-based, Non anti-aliased lines
1001 const int idx_count = count * 6;
1002 const int vtx_count = count * 4; // FIXME-OPT: Not sharing edges
1003 PrimReserve(idx_count, vtx_count);
1004
1005 for (int i1 = 0; i1 < count; i1++)
1006 {
1007 const int i2 = (i1 + 1) == points_count ? 0 : i1 + 1;
1008 const ImVec2& p1 = points[i1];
1009 const ImVec2& p2 = points[i2];
1010
1011 float dx = p2.x - p1.x;
1012 float dy = p2.y - p1.y;
1013 IM_NORMALIZE2F_OVER_ZERO(dx, dy);
1014 dx *= (thickness * 0.5f);
1015 dy *= (thickness * 0.5f);
1016
1017 _VtxWritePtr[0].pos.x = p1.x + dy; _VtxWritePtr[0].pos.y = p1.y - dx; _VtxWritePtr[0].uv = opaque_uv; _VtxWritePtr[0].col = col;
1018 _VtxWritePtr[1].pos.x = p2.x + dy; _VtxWritePtr[1].pos.y = p2.y - dx; _VtxWritePtr[1].uv = opaque_uv; _VtxWritePtr[1].col = col;
1019 _VtxWritePtr[2].pos.x = p2.x - dy; _VtxWritePtr[2].pos.y = p2.y + dx; _VtxWritePtr[2].uv = opaque_uv; _VtxWritePtr[2].col = col;
1020 _VtxWritePtr[3].pos.x = p1.x - dy; _VtxWritePtr[3].pos.y = p1.y + dx; _VtxWritePtr[3].uv = opaque_uv; _VtxWritePtr[3].col = col;
1021 _VtxWritePtr += 4;
1022
1023 _IdxWritePtr[0] = (ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx); _IdxWritePtr[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx + 1); _IdxWritePtr[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx + 2);
1024 _IdxWritePtr[3] = (ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx); _IdxWritePtr[4] = (ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx + 2); _IdxWritePtr[5] = (ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx + 3);
1025 _IdxWritePtr += 6;
1026 _VtxCurrentIdx += 4;
1027 }
1028 }
1029}
1030
1031// - We intentionally avoid using ImVec2 and its math operators here to reduce cost to a minimum for debug/non-inlined builds.
1032// - Filled shapes must always use clockwise winding order. The anti-aliasing fringe depends on it. Counter-clockwise shapes will have "inward" anti-aliasing.
1033void ImDrawList::AddConvexPolyFilled(const ImVec2* points, const int points_count, ImU32 col)
1034{
1035 if (points_count < 3 || (col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0)
1036 return;
1037
1038 const ImVec2 uv = _Data->TexUvWhitePixel;
1039
1040 if (Flags & ImDrawListFlags_AntiAliasedFill)
1041 {
1042 // Anti-aliased Fill
1043 const float AA_SIZE = _FringeScale;
1044 const ImU32 col_trans = col & ~IM_COL32_A_MASK;
1045 const int idx_count = (points_count - 2)*3 + points_count * 6;
1046 const int vtx_count = (points_count * 2);
1047 PrimReserve(idx_count, vtx_count);
1048
1049 // Add indexes for fill
1050 unsigned int vtx_inner_idx = _VtxCurrentIdx;
1051 unsigned int vtx_outer_idx = _VtxCurrentIdx + 1;
1052 for (int i = 2; i < points_count; i++)
1053 {
1054 _IdxWritePtr[0] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_inner_idx); _IdxWritePtr[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_inner_idx + ((i - 1) << 1)); _IdxWritePtr[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_inner_idx + (i << 1));
1055 _IdxWritePtr += 3;
1056 }
1057
1058 // Compute normals
1059 _Data->TempBuffer.reserve_discard(points_count);
1060 ImVec2* temp_normals = _Data->TempBuffer.Data;
1061 for (int i0 = points_count - 1, i1 = 0; i1 < points_count; i0 = i1++)
1062 {
1063 const ImVec2& p0 = points[i0];
1064 const ImVec2& p1 = points[i1];
1065 float dx = p1.x - p0.x;
1066 float dy = p1.y - p0.y;
1067 IM_NORMALIZE2F_OVER_ZERO(dx, dy);
1068 temp_normals[i0].x = dy;
1069 temp_normals[i0].y = -dx;
1070 }
1071
1072 for (int i0 = points_count - 1, i1 = 0; i1 < points_count; i0 = i1++)
1073 {
1074 // Average normals
1075 const ImVec2& n0 = temp_normals[i0];
1076 const ImVec2& n1 = temp_normals[i1];
1077 float dm_x = (n0.x + n1.x) * 0.5f;
1078 float dm_y = (n0.y + n1.y) * 0.5f;
1079 IM_FIXNORMAL2F(dm_x, dm_y);
1080 dm_x *= AA_SIZE * 0.5f;
1081 dm_y *= AA_SIZE * 0.5f;
1082
1083 // Add vertices
1084 _VtxWritePtr[0].pos.x = (points[i1].x - dm_x); _VtxWritePtr[0].pos.y = (points[i1].y - dm_y); _VtxWritePtr[0].uv = uv; _VtxWritePtr[0].col = col; // Inner
1085 _VtxWritePtr[1].pos.x = (points[i1].x + dm_x); _VtxWritePtr[1].pos.y = (points[i1].y + dm_y); _VtxWritePtr[1].uv = uv; _VtxWritePtr[1].col = col_trans; // Outer
1086 _VtxWritePtr += 2;
1087
1088 // Add indexes for fringes
1089 _IdxWritePtr[0] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_inner_idx + (i1 << 1)); _IdxWritePtr[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_inner_idx + (i0 << 1)); _IdxWritePtr[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_outer_idx + (i0 << 1));
1090 _IdxWritePtr[3] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_outer_idx + (i0 << 1)); _IdxWritePtr[4] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_outer_idx + (i1 << 1)); _IdxWritePtr[5] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_inner_idx + (i1 << 1));
1091 _IdxWritePtr += 6;
1092 }
1093 _VtxCurrentIdx += (ImDrawIdx)vtx_count;
1094 }
1095 else
1096 {
1097 // Non Anti-aliased Fill
1098 const int idx_count = (points_count - 2)*3;
1099 const int vtx_count = points_count;
1100 PrimReserve(idx_count, vtx_count);
1101 for (int i = 0; i < vtx_count; i++)
1102 {
1103 _VtxWritePtr[0].pos = points[i]; _VtxWritePtr[0].uv = uv; _VtxWritePtr[0].col = col;
1104 _VtxWritePtr++;
1105 }
1106 for (int i = 2; i < points_count; i++)
1107 {
1108 _IdxWritePtr[0] = (ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx); _IdxWritePtr[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx + i - 1); _IdxWritePtr[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx + i);
1109 _IdxWritePtr += 3;
1110 }
1111 _VtxCurrentIdx += (ImDrawIdx)vtx_count;
1112 }
1113}
1114
1115void ImDrawList::_PathArcToFastEx(const ImVec2& center, float radius, int a_min_sample, int a_max_sample, int a_step)
1116{
1117 if (radius < 0.5f)
1118 {
1119 _Path.push_back(center);
1120 return;
1121 }
1122
1123 // Calculate arc auto segment step size
1124 if (a_step <= 0)
1125 a_step = IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX / _CalcCircleAutoSegmentCount(radius);
1126
1127 // Make sure we never do steps larger than one quarter of the circle
1128 a_step = ImClamp(a_step, 1, IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_TABLE_SIZE / 4);
1129
1130 const int sample_range = ImAbs(a_max_sample - a_min_sample);
1131 const int a_next_step = a_step;
1132
1133 int samples = sample_range + 1;
1134 bool extra_max_sample = false;
1135 if (a_step > 1)
1136 {
1137 samples = sample_range / a_step + 1;
1138 const int overstep = sample_range % a_step;
1139
1140 if (overstep > 0)
1141 {
1142 extra_max_sample = true;
1143 samples++;
1144
1145 // When we have overstep to avoid awkwardly looking one long line and one tiny one at the end,
1146 // distribute first step range evenly between them by reducing first step size.
1147 if (sample_range > 0)
1148 a_step -= (a_step - overstep) / 2;
1149 }
1150 }
1151
1152 _Path.resize(_Path.Size + samples);
1153 ImVec2* out_ptr = _Path.Data + (_Path.Size - samples);
1154
1155 int sample_index = a_min_sample;
1156 if (sample_index < 0 || sample_index >= IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX)
1157 {
1158 sample_index = sample_index % IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX;
1159 if (sample_index < 0)
1160 sample_index += IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX;
1161 }
1162
1163 if (a_max_sample >= a_min_sample)
1164 {
1165 for (int a = a_min_sample; a <= a_max_sample; a += a_step, sample_index += a_step, a_step = a_next_step)
1166 {
1167 // a_step is clamped to IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX, so we have guaranteed that it will not wrap over range twice or more
1168 if (sample_index >= IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX)
1169 sample_index -= IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX;
1170
1171 const ImVec2 s = _Data->ArcFastVtx[sample_index];
1172 out_ptr->x = center.x + s.x * radius;
1173 out_ptr->y = center.y + s.y * radius;
1174 out_ptr++;
1175 }
1176 }
1177 else
1178 {
1179 for (int a = a_min_sample; a >= a_max_sample; a -= a_step, sample_index -= a_step, a_step = a_next_step)
1180 {
1181 // a_step is clamped to IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX, so we have guaranteed that it will not wrap over range twice or more
1182 if (sample_index < 0)
1183 sample_index += IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX;
1184
1185 const ImVec2 s = _Data->ArcFastVtx[sample_index];
1186 out_ptr->x = center.x + s.x * radius;
1187 out_ptr->y = center.y + s.y * radius;
1188 out_ptr++;
1189 }
1190 }
1191
1192 if (extra_max_sample)
1193 {
1194 int normalized_max_sample = a_max_sample % IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX;
1195 if (normalized_max_sample < 0)
1196 normalized_max_sample += IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX;
1197
1198 const ImVec2 s = _Data->ArcFastVtx[normalized_max_sample];
1199 out_ptr->x = center.x + s.x * radius;
1200 out_ptr->y = center.y + s.y * radius;
1201 out_ptr++;
1202 }
1203
1204 IM_ASSERT_PARANOID(_Path.Data + _Path.Size == out_ptr);
1205}
1206
1207void ImDrawList::_PathArcToN(const ImVec2& center, float radius, float a_min, float a_max, int num_segments)
1208{
1209 if (radius < 0.5f)
1210 {
1211 _Path.push_back(center);
1212 return;
1213 }
1214
1215 // Note that we are adding a point at both a_min and a_max.
1216 // If you are trying to draw a full closed circle you don't want the overlapping points!
1217 _Path.reserve(_Path.Size + (num_segments + 1));
1218 for (int i = 0; i <= num_segments; i++)
1219 {
1220 const float a = a_min + ((float)i / (float)num_segments) * (a_max - a_min);
1221 _Path.push_back(ImVec2(center.x + ImCos(a) * radius, center.y + ImSin(a) * radius));
1222 }
1223}
1224
1225// 0: East, 3: South, 6: West, 9: North, 12: East
1226void ImDrawList::PathArcToFast(const ImVec2& center, float radius, int a_min_of_12, int a_max_of_12)
1227{
1228 if (radius < 0.5f)
1229 {
1230 _Path.push_back(center);
1231 return;
1232 }
1233 _PathArcToFastEx(center, radius, a_min_of_12 * IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX / 12, a_max_of_12 * IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX / 12, 0);
1234}
1235
1236void ImDrawList::PathArcTo(const ImVec2& center, float radius, float a_min, float a_max, int num_segments)
1237{
1238 if (radius < 0.5f)
1239 {
1240 _Path.push_back(center);
1241 return;
1242 }
1243
1244 if (num_segments > 0)
1245 {
1246 _PathArcToN(center, radius, a_min, a_max, num_segments);
1247 return;
1248 }
1249
1250 // Automatic segment count
1251 if (radius <= _Data->ArcFastRadiusCutoff)
1252 {
1253 const bool a_is_reverse = a_max < a_min;
1254
1255 // We are going to use precomputed values for mid samples.
1256 // Determine first and last sample in lookup table that belong to the arc.
1257 const float a_min_sample_f = IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX * a_min / (IM_PI * 2.0f);
1258 const float a_max_sample_f = IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX * a_max / (IM_PI * 2.0f);
1259
1260 const int a_min_sample = a_is_reverse ? (int)ImFloor(a_min_sample_f) : (int)ImCeil(a_min_sample_f);
1261 const int a_max_sample = a_is_reverse ? (int)ImCeil(a_max_sample_f) : (int)ImFloor(a_max_sample_f);
1262 const int a_mid_samples = a_is_reverse ? ImMax(a_min_sample - a_max_sample, 0) : ImMax(a_max_sample - a_min_sample, 0);
1263
1264 const float a_min_segment_angle = a_min_sample * IM_PI * 2.0f / IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX;
1265 const float a_max_segment_angle = a_max_sample * IM_PI * 2.0f / IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX;
1266 const bool a_emit_start = ImAbs(a_min_segment_angle - a_min) >= 1e-5f;
1267 const bool a_emit_end = ImAbs(a_max - a_max_segment_angle) >= 1e-5f;
1268
1269 _Path.reserve(_Path.Size + (a_mid_samples + 1 + (a_emit_start ? 1 : 0) + (a_emit_end ? 1 : 0)));
1270 if (a_emit_start)
1271 _Path.push_back(ImVec2(center.x + ImCos(a_min) * radius, center.y + ImSin(a_min) * radius));
1272 if (a_mid_samples > 0)
1273 _PathArcToFastEx(center, radius, a_min_sample, a_max_sample, 0);
1274 if (a_emit_end)
1275 _Path.push_back(ImVec2(center.x + ImCos(a_max) * radius, center.y + ImSin(a_max) * radius));
1276 }
1277 else
1278 {
1279 const float arc_length = ImAbs(a_max - a_min);
1280 const int circle_segment_count = _CalcCircleAutoSegmentCount(radius);
1281 const int arc_segment_count = ImMax((int)ImCeil(circle_segment_count * arc_length / (IM_PI * 2.0f)), (int)(2.0f * IM_PI / arc_length));
1282 _PathArcToN(center, radius, a_min, a_max, arc_segment_count);
1283 }
1284}
1285
1286void ImDrawList::PathEllipticalArcTo(const ImVec2& center, const ImVec2& radius, float rot, float a_min, float a_max, int num_segments)
1287{
1288 if (num_segments <= 0)
1289 num_segments = _CalcCircleAutoSegmentCount(ImMax(radius.x, radius.y)); // A bit pessimistic, maybe there's a better computation to do here.
1290
1291 _Path.reserve(_Path.Size + (num_segments + 1));
1292
1293 const float cos_rot = ImCos(rot);
1294 const float sin_rot = ImSin(rot);
1295 for (int i = 0; i <= num_segments; i++)
1296 {
1297 const float a = a_min + ((float)i / (float)num_segments) * (a_max - a_min);
1298 ImVec2 point(ImCos(a) * radius.x, ImSin(a) * radius.y);
1299 const ImVec2 rel((point.x * cos_rot) - (point.y * sin_rot), (point.x * sin_rot) + (point.y * cos_rot));
1300 point.x = rel.x + center.x;
1301 point.y = rel.y + center.y;
1302 _Path.push_back(point);
1303 }
1304}
1305
1306ImVec2 ImBezierCubicCalc(const ImVec2& p1, const ImVec2& p2, const ImVec2& p3, const ImVec2& p4, float t)
1307{
1308 float u = 1.0f - t;
1309 float w1 = u * u * u;
1310 float w2 = 3 * u * u * t;
1311 float w3 = 3 * u * t * t;
1312 float w4 = t * t * t;
1313 return ImVec2(w1 * p1.x + w2 * p2.x + w3 * p3.x + w4 * p4.x, w1 * p1.y + w2 * p2.y + w3 * p3.y + w4 * p4.y);
1314}
1315
1316ImVec2 ImBezierQuadraticCalc(const ImVec2& p1, const ImVec2& p2, const ImVec2& p3, float t)
1317{
1318 float u = 1.0f - t;
1319 float w1 = u * u;
1320 float w2 = 2 * u * t;
1321 float w3 = t * t;
1322 return ImVec2(w1 * p1.x + w2 * p2.x + w3 * p3.x, w1 * p1.y + w2 * p2.y + w3 * p3.y);
1323}
1324
1325// Closely mimics ImBezierCubicClosestPointCasteljau() in imgui.cpp
1326static void PathBezierCubicCurveToCasteljau(ImVector<ImVec2>* path, float x1, float y1, float x2, float y2, float x3, float y3, float x4, float y4, float tess_tol, int level)
1327{
1328 float dx = x4 - x1;
1329 float dy = y4 - y1;
1330 float d2 = (x2 - x4) * dy - (y2 - y4) * dx;
1331 float d3 = (x3 - x4) * dy - (y3 - y4) * dx;
1332 d2 = (d2 >= 0) ? d2 : -d2;
1333 d3 = (d3 >= 0) ? d3 : -d3;
1334 if ((d2 + d3) * (d2 + d3) < tess_tol * (dx * dx + dy * dy))
1335 {
1336 path->push_back(ImVec2(x4, y4));
1337 }
1338 else if (level < 10)
1339 {
1340 float x12 = (x1 + x2) * 0.5f, y12 = (y1 + y2) * 0.5f;
1341 float x23 = (x2 + x3) * 0.5f, y23 = (y2 + y3) * 0.5f;
1342 float x34 = (x3 + x4) * 0.5f, y34 = (y3 + y4) * 0.5f;
1343 float x123 = (x12 + x23) * 0.5f, y123 = (y12 + y23) * 0.5f;
1344 float x234 = (x23 + x34) * 0.5f, y234 = (y23 + y34) * 0.5f;
1345 float x1234 = (x123 + x234) * 0.5f, y1234 = (y123 + y234) * 0.5f;
1346 PathBezierCubicCurveToCasteljau(path, x1, y1, x12, y12, x123, y123, x1234, y1234, tess_tol, level + 1);
1347 PathBezierCubicCurveToCasteljau(path, x1234, y1234, x234, y234, x34, y34, x4, y4, tess_tol, level + 1);
1348 }
1349}
1350
1351static void PathBezierQuadraticCurveToCasteljau(ImVector<ImVec2>* path, float x1, float y1, float x2, float y2, float x3, float y3, float tess_tol, int level)
1352{
1353 float dx = x3 - x1, dy = y3 - y1;
1354 float det = (x2 - x3) * dy - (y2 - y3) * dx;
1355 if (det * det * 4.0f < tess_tol * (dx * dx + dy * dy))
1356 {
1357 path->push_back(ImVec2(x3, y3));
1358 }
1359 else if (level < 10)
1360 {
1361 float x12 = (x1 + x2) * 0.5f, y12 = (y1 + y2) * 0.5f;
1362 float x23 = (x2 + x3) * 0.5f, y23 = (y2 + y3) * 0.5f;
1363 float x123 = (x12 + x23) * 0.5f, y123 = (y12 + y23) * 0.5f;
1364 PathBezierQuadraticCurveToCasteljau(path, x1, y1, x12, y12, x123, y123, tess_tol, level + 1);
1365 PathBezierQuadraticCurveToCasteljau(path, x123, y123, x23, y23, x3, y3, tess_tol, level + 1);
1366 }
1367}
1368
1369void ImDrawList::PathBezierCubicCurveTo(const ImVec2& p2, const ImVec2& p3, const ImVec2& p4, int num_segments)
1370{
1371 ImVec2 p1 = _Path.back();
1372 if (num_segments == 0)
1373 {
1374 IM_ASSERT(_Data->CurveTessellationTol > 0.0f);
1375 PathBezierCubicCurveToCasteljau(&_Path, p1.x, p1.y, p2.x, p2.y, p3.x, p3.y, p4.x, p4.y, _Data->CurveTessellationTol, 0); // Auto-tessellated
1376 }
1377 else
1378 {
1379 float t_step = 1.0f / (float)num_segments;
1380 for (int i_step = 1; i_step <= num_segments; i_step++)
1381 _Path.push_back(ImBezierCubicCalc(p1, p2, p3, p4, t_step * i_step));
1382 }
1383}
1384
1385void ImDrawList::PathBezierQuadraticCurveTo(const ImVec2& p2, const ImVec2& p3, int num_segments)
1386{
1387 ImVec2 p1 = _Path.back();
1388 if (num_segments == 0)
1389 {
1390 IM_ASSERT(_Data->CurveTessellationTol > 0.0f);
1391 PathBezierQuadraticCurveToCasteljau(&_Path, p1.x, p1.y, p2.x, p2.y, p3.x, p3.y, _Data->CurveTessellationTol, 0);// Auto-tessellated
1392 }
1393 else
1394 {
1395 float t_step = 1.0f / (float)num_segments;
1396 for (int i_step = 1; i_step <= num_segments; i_step++)
1397 _Path.push_back(ImBezierQuadraticCalc(p1, p2, p3, t_step * i_step));
1398 }
1399}
1400
1401static inline ImDrawFlags FixRectCornerFlags(ImDrawFlags flags)
1402{
1403 /*
1404 IM_STATIC_ASSERT(ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopLeft == (1 << 4));
1405#ifndef IMGUI_DISABLE_OBSOLETE_FUNCTIONS
1406 // Obsoleted in 1.82 (from February 2021). This code was stripped/simplified and mostly commented in 1.90 (from September 2023)
1407 // - Legacy Support for hard coded ~0 (used to be a suggested equivalent to ImDrawCornerFlags_All)
1408 if (flags == ~0) { return ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersAll; }
1409 // - Legacy Support for hard coded 0x01 to 0x0F (matching 15 out of 16 old flags combinations). Read details in older version of this code.
1410 if (flags >= 0x01 && flags <= 0x0F) { return (flags << 4); }
1411 // We cannot support hard coded 0x00 with 'float rounding > 0.0f' --> replace with ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersNone or use 'float rounding = 0.0f'
1412#endif
1413 */
1414 // If this assert triggers, please update your code replacing hardcoded values with new ImDrawFlags_RoundCorners* values.
1415 // Note that ImDrawFlags_Closed (== 0x01) is an invalid flag for AddRect(), AddRectFilled(), PathRect() etc. anyway.
1416 // See details in 1.82 Changelog as well as 2021/03/12 and 2023/09/08 entries in "API BREAKING CHANGES" section.
1417 IM_ASSERT((flags & 0x0F) == 0 && "Misuse of legacy hardcoded ImDrawCornerFlags values!");
1418
1419 if ((flags & ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersMask_) == 0)
1420 flags |= ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersAll;
1421
1422 return flags;
1423}
1424
1425void ImDrawList::PathRect(const ImVec2& a, const ImVec2& b, float rounding, ImDrawFlags flags)
1426{
1427 if (rounding >= 0.5f)
1428 {
1429 flags = FixRectCornerFlags(flags);
1430 rounding = ImMin(rounding, ImFabs(b.x - a.x) * (((flags & ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTop) == ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTop) || ((flags & ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBottom) == ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBottom) ? 0.5f : 1.0f) - 1.0f);
1431 rounding = ImMin(rounding, ImFabs(b.y - a.y) * (((flags & ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersLeft) == ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersLeft) || ((flags & ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersRight) == ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersRight) ? 0.5f : 1.0f) - 1.0f);
1432 }
1433 if (rounding < 0.5f || (flags & ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersMask_) == ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersNone)
1434 {
1435 PathLineTo(a);
1436 PathLineTo(ImVec2(b.x, a.y));
1437 PathLineTo(b);
1438 PathLineTo(ImVec2(a.x, b.y));
1439 }
1440 else
1441 {
1442 const float rounding_tl = (flags & ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopLeft) ? rounding : 0.0f;
1443 const float rounding_tr = (flags & ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopRight) ? rounding : 0.0f;
1444 const float rounding_br = (flags & ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBottomRight) ? rounding : 0.0f;
1445 const float rounding_bl = (flags & ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBottomLeft) ? rounding : 0.0f;
1446 PathArcToFast(ImVec2(a.x + rounding_tl, a.y + rounding_tl), rounding_tl, 6, 9);
1447 PathArcToFast(ImVec2(b.x - rounding_tr, a.y + rounding_tr), rounding_tr, 9, 12);
1448 PathArcToFast(ImVec2(b.x - rounding_br, b.y - rounding_br), rounding_br, 0, 3);
1449 PathArcToFast(ImVec2(a.x + rounding_bl, b.y - rounding_bl), rounding_bl, 3, 6);
1450 }
1451}
1452
1453void ImDrawList::AddLine(const ImVec2& p1, const ImVec2& p2, ImU32 col, float thickness)
1454{
1455 if ((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0)
1456 return;
1457 PathLineTo(p1 + ImVec2(0.5f, 0.5f));
1458 PathLineTo(p2 + ImVec2(0.5f, 0.5f));
1459 PathStroke(col, 0, thickness);
1460}
1461
1462// p_min = upper-left, p_max = lower-right
1463// Note we don't render 1 pixels sized rectangles properly.
1464void ImDrawList::AddRect(const ImVec2& p_min, const ImVec2& p_max, ImU32 col, float rounding, ImDrawFlags flags, float thickness)
1465{
1466 if ((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0)
1467 return;
1468 if (Flags & ImDrawListFlags_AntiAliasedLines)
1469 PathRect(p_min + ImVec2(0.50f, 0.50f), p_max - ImVec2(0.50f, 0.50f), rounding, flags);
1470 else
1471 PathRect(p_min + ImVec2(0.50f, 0.50f), p_max - ImVec2(0.49f, 0.49f), rounding, flags); // Better looking lower-right corner and rounded non-AA shapes.
1472 PathStroke(col, ImDrawFlags_Closed, thickness);
1473}
1474
1475void ImDrawList::AddRectFilled(const ImVec2& p_min, const ImVec2& p_max, ImU32 col, float rounding, ImDrawFlags flags)
1476{
1477 if ((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0)
1478 return;
1479 if (rounding < 0.5f || (flags & ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersMask_) == ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersNone)
1480 {
1481 PrimReserve(6, 4);
1482 PrimRect(p_min, p_max, col);
1483 }
1484 else
1485 {
1486 PathRect(p_min, p_max, rounding, flags);
1487 PathFillConvex(col);
1488 }
1489}
1490
1491// p_min = upper-left, p_max = lower-right
1492void ImDrawList::AddRectFilledMultiColor(const ImVec2& p_min, const ImVec2& p_max, ImU32 col_upr_left, ImU32 col_upr_right, ImU32 col_bot_right, ImU32 col_bot_left)
1493{
1494 if (((col_upr_left | col_upr_right | col_bot_right | col_bot_left) & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0)
1495 return;
1496
1497 const ImVec2 uv = _Data->TexUvWhitePixel;
1498 PrimReserve(6, 4);
1499 PrimWriteIdx((ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx)); PrimWriteIdx((ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx + 1)); PrimWriteIdx((ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx + 2));
1500 PrimWriteIdx((ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx)); PrimWriteIdx((ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx + 2)); PrimWriteIdx((ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx + 3));
1501 PrimWriteVtx(p_min, uv, col_upr_left);
1502 PrimWriteVtx(ImVec2(p_max.x, p_min.y), uv, col_upr_right);
1503 PrimWriteVtx(p_max, uv, col_bot_right);
1504 PrimWriteVtx(ImVec2(p_min.x, p_max.y), uv, col_bot_left);
1505}

1552
1553void ImDrawList::AddCircle(const ImVec2& center, float radius, ImU32 col, int num_segments, float thickness)
1554{
1555 if ((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0 || radius < 0.5f)
1556 return;
1557
1558 if (num_segments <= 0)
1559 {
1560 // Use arc with automatic segment count
1561 _PathArcToFastEx(center, radius - 0.5f, 0, IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX, 0);
1562 _Path.Size--;
1563 }
1564 else
1565 {
1566 // Explicit segment count (still clamp to avoid drawing insanely tessellated shapes)
1567 num_segments = ImClamp(num_segments, 3, IM_DRAWLIST_CIRCLE_AUTO_SEGMENT_MAX);
1568
1569 // Because we are filling a closed shape we remove 1 from the count of segments/points
1570 const float a_max = (IM_PI * 2.0f) * ((float)num_segments - 1.0f) / (float)num_segments;
1571 PathArcTo(center, radius - 0.5f, 0.0f, a_max, num_segments - 1);
1572 }
1573
1574 PathStroke(col, ImDrawFlags_Closed, thickness);
1575}
1576
1577void ImDrawList::AddCircleFilled(const ImVec2& center, float radius, ImU32 col, int num_segments)
1578{
1579 if ((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0 || radius < 0.5f)
1580 return;
1581
1582 if (num_segments <= 0)
1583 {
1584 // Use arc with automatic segment count
1585 _PathArcToFastEx(center, radius, 0, IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX, 0);
1586 _Path.Size--;
1587 }
1588 else
1589 {
1590 // Explicit segment count (still clamp to avoid drawing insanely tessellated shapes)
1591 num_segments = ImClamp(num_segments, 3, IM_DRAWLIST_CIRCLE_AUTO_SEGMENT_MAX);
1592
1593 // Because we are filling a closed shape we remove 1 from the count of segments/points
1594 const float a_max = (IM_PI * 2.0f) * ((float)num_segments - 1.0f) / (float)num_segments;
1595 PathArcTo(center, radius, 0.0f, a_max, num_segments - 1);
1596 }
1597
1598 PathFillConvex(col);
1599}
1600
1601// Guaranteed to honor 'num_segments'
1602void ImDrawList::AddNgon(const ImVec2& center, float radius, ImU32 col, int num_segments, float thickness)
1603{
1604 if ((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0 || num_segments <= 2)
1605 return;
1606
1607 // Because we are filling a closed shape we remove 1 from the count of segments/points
1608 const float a_max = (IM_PI * 2.0f) * ((float)num_segments - 1.0f) / (float)num_segments;
1609 PathArcTo(center, radius - 0.5f, 0.0f, a_max, num_segments - 1);
1610 PathStroke(col, ImDrawFlags_Closed, thickness);
1611}
1612
1613// Guaranteed to honor 'num_segments'
1614void ImDrawList::AddNgonFilled(const ImVec2& center, float radius, ImU32 col, int num_segments)
1615{
1616 if ((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0 || num_segments <= 2)
1617 return;
1618
1619 // Because we are filling a closed shape we remove 1 from the count of segments/points
1620 const float a_max = (IM_PI * 2.0f) * ((float)num_segments - 1.0f) / (float)num_segments;
1621 PathArcTo(center, radius, 0.0f, a_max, num_segments - 1);
1622 PathFillConvex(col);
1623}
1624
1625// Ellipse
1626void ImDrawList::AddEllipse(const ImVec2& center, const ImVec2& radius, ImU32 col, float rot, int num_segments, float thickness)
1627{
1628 if ((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0)
1629 return;
1630
1631 if (num_segments <= 0)
1632 num_segments = _CalcCircleAutoSegmentCount(ImMax(radius.x, radius.y)); // A bit pessimistic, maybe there's a better computation to do here.
1633
1634 // Because we are filling a closed shape we remove 1 from the count of segments/points
1635 const float a_max = IM_PI * 2.0f * ((float)num_segments - 1.0f) / (float)num_segments;
1636 PathEllipticalArcTo(center, radius, rot, 0.0f, a_max, num_segments - 1);
1637 PathStroke(col, true, thickness);
1638}
1639
1640void ImDrawList::AddEllipseFilled(const ImVec2& center, const ImVec2& radius, ImU32 col, float rot, int num_segments)
1641{
1642 if ((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0)
1643 return;
1644
1645 if (num_segments <= 0)
1646 num_segments = _CalcCircleAutoSegmentCount(ImMax(radius.x, radius.y)); // A bit pessimistic, maybe there's a better computation to do here.
1647
1648 // Because we are filling a closed shape we remove 1 from the count of segments/points
1649 const float a_max = IM_PI * 2.0f * ((float)num_segments - 1.0f) / (float)num_segments;
1650 PathEllipticalArcTo(center, radius, rot, 0.0f, a_max, num_segments - 1);
1651 PathFillConvex(col);
1652}
1653
1654// Cubic Bezier takes 4 controls points
1655void ImDrawList::AddBezierCubic(const ImVec2& p1, const ImVec2& p2, const ImVec2& p3, const ImVec2& p4, ImU32 col, float thickness, int num_segments)
1656{
1657 if ((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0)
1658 return;
1659
1660 PathLineTo(p1);
1661 PathBezierCubicCurveTo(p2, p3, p4, num_segments);
1662 PathStroke(col, 0, thickness);
1663}
1664
1665// Quadratic Bezier takes 3 controls points
1666void ImDrawList::AddBezierQuadratic(const ImVec2& p1, const ImVec2& p2, const ImVec2& p3, ImU32 col, float thickness, int num_segments)
1667{
1668 if ((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0)
1669 return;
1670
1671 PathLineTo(p1);
1672 PathBezierQuadraticCurveTo(p2, p3, num_segments);
1673 PathStroke(col, 0, thickness);
1674}
1675
1676void ImDrawList::AddText(ImFont* font, float font_size, const ImVec2& pos, ImU32 col, const char* text_begin, const char* text_end, float wrap_width, const ImVec4* cpu_fine_clip_rect)
1677{
1678 if ((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0)
1679 return;
1680
1681 // Accept null ranges
1682 if (text_begin == text_end || text_begin[0] == 0)
1683 return;
1684 // No need to strlen() here: font->RenderText() will do it and may early out.
1685
1686 // Pull default font/size from the shared ImDrawListSharedData instance
1687 if (font == NULL)
1688 font = _Data->Font;
1689 if (font_size == 0.0f)
1690 font_size = _Data->FontSize;
1691
1692 IM_ASSERT(font->ContainerAtlas->TexID == _CmdHeader.TextureId); // Use high-level ImGui::PushFont() or low-level ImDrawList::PushTextureId() to change font.
1693
1694 ImVec4 clip_rect = _CmdHeader.ClipRect;
1695 if (cpu_fine_clip_rect)
1696 {
1697 clip_rect.x = ImMax(clip_rect.x, cpu_fine_clip_rect->x);
1698 clip_rect.y = ImMax(clip_rect.y, cpu_fine_clip_rect->y);
1699 clip_rect.z = ImMin(clip_rect.z, cpu_fine_clip_rect->z);
1700 clip_rect.w = ImMin(clip_rect.w, cpu_fine_clip_rect->w);
1701 }
1702 font->RenderText(this, font_size, pos, col, clip_rect, text_begin, text_end, wrap_width, cpu_fine_clip_rect != NULL);
1703}
1704
1705void ImDrawList::AddText(const ImVec2& pos, ImU32 col, const char* text_begin, const char* text_end)
1706{
1707 AddText(_Data->Font, _Data->FontSize, pos, col, text_begin, text_end);
1708}
