1710void ImDrawList::AddImage(ImTextureID user_texture_id, const ImVec2& p_min, const ImVec2& p_max, const ImVec2& uv_min, const ImVec2& uv_max, ImU32 col)
1711{
1712 if ((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0)
1713 return;
1714
1715 const bool push_texture_id = user_texture_id != _CmdHeader.TextureId;
1716 if (push_texture_id)
1717 PushTextureID(user_texture_id);
1718
1719 PrimReserve(6, 4);
1720 PrimRectUV(p_min, p_max, uv_min, uv_max, col);
1721
1722 if (push_texture_id)
1723 PopTextureID();
1724}
1725
1726void ImDrawList::AddImageQuad(ImTextureID user_texture_id, const ImVec2& p1, const ImVec2& p2, const ImVec2& p3, const ImVec2& p4, const ImVec2& uv1, const ImVec2& uv2, const ImVec2& uv3, const ImVec2& uv4, ImU32 col)
1727{
1728 if ((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0)
1729 return;
1730
1731 const bool push_texture_id = user_texture_id != _CmdHeader.TextureId;
1732 if (push_texture_id)
1733 PushTextureID(user_texture_id);
1734
1735 PrimReserve(6, 4);
1736 PrimQuadUV(p1, p2, p3, p4, uv1, uv2, uv3, uv4, col);
1737
1738 if (push_texture_id)
1739 PopTextureID();
1740}
1741
1742void ImDrawList::AddImageRounded(ImTextureID user_texture_id, const ImVec2& p_min, const ImVec2& p_max, const ImVec2& uv_min, const ImVec2& uv_max, ImU32 col, float rounding, ImDrawFlags flags)
1743{
1744 if ((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0)
1745 return;
1746
1747 flags = FixRectCornerFlags(flags);
1748 if (rounding < 0.5f || (flags & ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersMask_) == ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersNone)
1749 {
1750 AddImage(user_texture_id, p_min, p_max, uv_min, uv_max, col);
1751 return;
1752 }
1753
1754 const bool push_texture_id = user_texture_id != _CmdHeader.TextureId;
1755 if (push_texture_id)
1756 PushTextureID(user_texture_id);
1757
1758 int vert_start_idx = VtxBuffer.Size;
1759 PathRect(p_min, p_max, rounding, flags);
1760 PathFillConvex(col);
1761 int vert_end_idx = VtxBuffer.Size;
1762 ImGui::ShadeVertsLinearUV(this, vert_start_idx, vert_end_idx, p_min, p_max, uv_min, uv_max, true);
1763
1764 if (push_texture_id)
1765 PopTextureID();
1766}
1767
1768//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
1769// [SECTION] ImTriangulator, ImDrawList concave polygon fill
1770//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
1771// Triangulate concave polygons. Based on "Triangulation by Ear Clipping" paper, O(N^2) complexity.
1772// Reference: https://www.geometrictools.com/Documentation/TriangulationByEarClipping.pdf
1773// Provided as a convenience for user but not used by main library.
1774//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
1775// - ImTriangulator [Internal]
1776// - AddConcavePolyFilled()
1777//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
1778
1779enum ImTriangulatorNodeType
1780{
1781 ImTriangulatorNodeType_Convex,
1782 ImTriangulatorNodeType_Ear,
1783 ImTriangulatorNodeType_Reflex
1784};
1785
1786struct ImTriangulatorNode
1787{
1788 ImTriangulatorNodeType Type;
1789 int Index;
1790 ImVec2 Pos;
1791 ImTriangulatorNode* Next;
1792 ImTriangulatorNode* Prev;
1793
1794 void Unlink() { Next->Prev = Prev; Prev->Next = Next; }
1795};
1796
1797struct ImTriangulatorNodeSpan
1798{
1799 ImTriangulatorNode** Data = NULL;
1800 int Size = 0;
1801
1802 void push_back(ImTriangulatorNode* node) { Data[Size++] = node; }
1803 void find_erase_unsorted(int idx) { for (int i = Size - 1; i >= 0; i--) if (Data[i]->Index == idx) { Data[i] = Data[Size - 1]; Size--; return; } }
1804};
1805
1806struct ImTriangulator
1807{
1808 static int EstimateTriangleCount(int points_count) { return (points_count < 3) ? 0 : points_count - 2; }
1809 static int EstimateScratchBufferSize(int points_count) { return sizeof(ImTriangulatorNode) * points_count + sizeof(ImTriangulatorNode*) * points_count * 2; }
1810
1811 void Init(const ImVec2* points, int points_count, void* scratch_buffer);
1812 void GetNextTriangle(unsigned int out_triangle[3]); // Return relative indexes for next triangle
1813
1814 // Internal functions
1815 void BuildNodes(const ImVec2* points, int points_count);
1816 void BuildReflexes();
1817 void BuildEars();
1818 void FlipNodeList();
1819 bool IsEar(int i0, int i1, int i2, const ImVec2& v0, const ImVec2& v1, const ImVec2& v2) const;
1820 void ReclassifyNode(ImTriangulatorNode* node);
1821
1822 // Internal members
1823 int _TrianglesLeft = 0;
1824 ImTriangulatorNode* _Nodes = NULL;
1825 ImTriangulatorNodeSpan _Ears;
1826 ImTriangulatorNodeSpan _Reflexes;
1827};
1828
1829// Distribute storage for nodes, ears and reflexes.
1830// FIXME-OPT: if everything is convex, we could report it to caller and let it switch to an convex renderer
1831// (this would require first building reflexes to bail to convex if empty, without even building nodes)
1832void ImTriangulator::Init(const ImVec2* points, int points_count, void* scratch_buffer)
1833{
1834 IM_ASSERT(scratch_buffer != NULL && points_count >= 3);
1835 _TrianglesLeft = EstimateTriangleCount(points_count);
1836 _Nodes = (ImTriangulatorNode*)scratch_buffer; // points_count x Node
1837 _Ears.Data = (ImTriangulatorNode**)(_Nodes + points_count); // points_count x Node*
1838 _Reflexes.Data = (ImTriangulatorNode**)(_Nodes + points_count) + points_count; // points_count x Node*
1839 BuildNodes(points, points_count);
1840 BuildReflexes();
1841 BuildEars();
1842}
1843
1844void ImTriangulator::BuildNodes(const ImVec2* points, int points_count)
1845{
1846 for (int i = 0; i < points_count; i++)
1847 {
1848 _Nodes[i].Type = ImTriangulatorNodeType_Convex;
1849 _Nodes[i].Index = i;
1850 _Nodes[i].Pos = points[i];
1851 _Nodes[i].Next = _Nodes + i + 1;
1852 _Nodes[i].Prev = _Nodes + i - 1;
1853 }
1854 _Nodes[0].Prev = _Nodes + points_count - 1;
1855 _Nodes[points_count - 1].Next = _Nodes;
1856}
1857
1858void ImTriangulator::BuildReflexes()
1859{
1860 ImTriangulatorNode* n1 = _Nodes;
1861 for (int i = _TrianglesLeft; i >= 0; i--, n1 = n1->Next)
1862 {
1863 if (ImTriangleIsClockwise(n1->Prev->Pos, n1->Pos, n1->Next->Pos))
1864 continue;
1865 n1->Type = ImTriangulatorNodeType_Reflex;
1866 _Reflexes.push_back(n1);
1867 }
1868}
1869
1870void ImTriangulator::BuildEars()
1871{
1872 ImTriangulatorNode* n1 = _Nodes;
1873 for (int i = _TrianglesLeft; i >= 0; i--, n1 = n1->Next)
1874 {
1875 if (n1->Type != ImTriangulatorNodeType_Convex)
1876 continue;
1877 if (!IsEar(n1->Prev->Index, n1->Index, n1->Next->Index, n1->Prev->Pos, n1->Pos, n1->Next->Pos))
1878 continue;
1879 n1->Type = ImTriangulatorNodeType_Ear;
1880 _Ears.push_back(n1);
1881 }
1882}
1883
1884void ImTriangulator::GetNextTriangle(unsigned int out_triangle[3])
1885{
1886 if (_Ears.Size == 0)
1887 {
1888 FlipNodeList();
1889
1890 ImTriangulatorNode* node = _Nodes;
1891 for (int i = _TrianglesLeft; i >= 0; i--, node = node->Next)
1892 node->Type = ImTriangulatorNodeType_Convex;
1893 _Reflexes.Size = 0;
1894 BuildReflexes();
1895 BuildEars();
1896
1897 // If we still don't have ears, it means geometry is degenerated.
1898 if (_Ears.Size == 0)
1899 {
1900 // Return first triangle available, mimicking the behavior of convex fill.
1901 IM_ASSERT(_TrianglesLeft > 0); // Geometry is degenerated
1902 _Ears.Data[0] = _Nodes;
1903 _Ears.Size = 1;
1904 }
1905 }
1906
1907 ImTriangulatorNode* ear = _Ears.Data[--_Ears.Size];
1908 out_triangle[0] = ear->Prev->Index;
1909 out_triangle[1] = ear->Index;
1910 out_triangle[2] = ear->Next->Index;
1911
1912 ear->Unlink();
1913 if (ear == _Nodes)
1914 _Nodes = ear->Next;
1915
1916 ReclassifyNode(ear->Prev);
1917 ReclassifyNode(ear->Next);
1918 _TrianglesLeft--;
1919}
1920
1921void ImTriangulator::FlipNodeList()
1922{
1923 ImTriangulatorNode* prev = _Nodes;
1924 ImTriangulatorNode* temp = _Nodes;
1925 ImTriangulatorNode* current = _Nodes->Next;
1926 prev->Next = prev;
1927 prev->Prev = prev;
1928 while (current != _Nodes)
1929 {
1930 temp = current->Next;
1931
1932 current->Next = prev;
1933 prev->Prev = current;
1934 _Nodes->Next = current;
1935 current->Prev = _Nodes;
1936
1937 prev = current;
1938 current = temp;
1939 }
1940 _Nodes = prev;
1941}
1942
1943// A triangle is an ear is no other vertex is inside it. We can test reflexes vertices only (see reference algorithm)
1944bool ImTriangulator::IsEar(int i0, int i1, int i2, const ImVec2& v0, const ImVec2& v1, const ImVec2& v2) const
1945{
1946 ImTriangulatorNode** p_end = _Reflexes.Data + _Reflexes.Size;
1947 for (ImTriangulatorNode** p = _Reflexes.Data; p < p_end; p++)
1948 {
1949 ImTriangulatorNode* reflex = *p;
1950 if (reflex->Index != i0 && reflex->Index != i1 && reflex->Index != i2)
1951 if (ImTriangleContainsPoint(v0, v1, v2, reflex->Pos))
1952 return false;
1953 }
1954 return true;
1955}
1956
1957void ImTriangulator::ReclassifyNode(ImTriangulatorNode* n1)
1958{
1959 // Classify node
1960 ImTriangulatorNodeType type;
1961 const ImTriangulatorNode* n0 = n1->Prev;
1962 const ImTriangulatorNode* n2 = n1->Next;
1963 if (!ImTriangleIsClockwise(n0->Pos, n1->Pos, n2->Pos))
1964 type = ImTriangulatorNodeType_Reflex;
1965 else if (IsEar(n0->Index, n1->Index, n2->Index, n0->Pos, n1->Pos, n2->Pos))
1966 type = ImTriangulatorNodeType_Ear;
1967 else
1968 type = ImTriangulatorNodeType_Convex;
1969
1970 // Update lists when a type changes
1971 if (type == n1->Type)
1972 return;
1973 if (n1->Type == ImTriangulatorNodeType_Reflex)
1974 _Reflexes.find_erase_unsorted(n1->Index);
1975 else if (n1->Type == ImTriangulatorNodeType_Ear)
1976 _Ears.find_erase_unsorted(n1->Index);
1977 if (type == ImTriangulatorNodeType_Reflex)
1978 _Reflexes.push_back(n1);
1979 else if (type == ImTriangulatorNodeType_Ear)
1980 _Ears.push_back(n1);
1981 n1->Type = type;
1982}
1983
1984// Use ear-clipping algorithm to triangulate a simple polygon (no self-interaction, no holes).
1985// (Reminder: we don't perform any coarse clipping/culling in ImDrawList layer!
1986// It is up to caller to ensure not making costly calls that will be outside of visible area.
1987// As concave fill is noticeably more expensive than other primitives, be mindful of this...
1988// Caller can build AABB of points, and avoid filling if 'draw_list->_CmdHeader.ClipRect.Overlays(points_bb) == false')
1989void ImDrawList::AddConcavePolyFilled(const ImVec2* points, const int points_count, ImU32 col)
1990{
1991 if (points_count < 3 || (col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0)
1992 return;
1993
1994 const ImVec2 uv = _Data->TexUvWhitePixel;
1995 ImTriangulator triangulator;
1996 unsigned int triangle[3];
1997 if (Flags & ImDrawListFlags_AntiAliasedFill)
1998 {
1999 // Anti-aliased Fill
2000 const float AA_SIZE = _FringeScale;
2001 const ImU32 col_trans = col & ~IM_COL32_A_MASK;
2002 const int idx_count = (points_count - 2) * 3 + points_count * 6;
2003 const int vtx_count = (points_count * 2);
2004 PrimReserve(idx_count, vtx_count);
2005
2006 // Add indexes for fill
2007 unsigned int vtx_inner_idx = _VtxCurrentIdx;
2008 unsigned int vtx_outer_idx = _VtxCurrentIdx + 1;
2009
2010 _Data->TempBuffer.reserve_discard((ImTriangulator::EstimateScratchBufferSize(points_count) + sizeof(ImVec2)) / sizeof(ImVec2));
2011 triangulator.Init(points, points_count, _Data->TempBuffer.Data);
2012 while (triangulator._TrianglesLeft > 0)
2013 {
2014 triangulator.GetNextTriangle(triangle);
2015 _IdxWritePtr[0] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_inner_idx + (triangle[0] << 1)); _IdxWritePtr[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_inner_idx + (triangle[1] << 1)); _IdxWritePtr[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_inner_idx + (triangle[2] << 1));
2016 _IdxWritePtr += 3;
2017 }
2018
2019 // Compute normals
2020 _Data->TempBuffer.reserve_discard(points_count);
2021 ImVec2* temp_normals = _Data->TempBuffer.Data;
2022 for (int i0 = points_count - 1, i1 = 0; i1 < points_count; i0 = i1++)
2023 {
2024 const ImVec2& p0 = points[i0];
2025 const ImVec2& p1 = points[i1];
2026 float dx = p1.x - p0.x;
2027 float dy = p1.y - p0.y;
2028 IM_NORMALIZE2F_OVER_ZERO(dx, dy);
2029 temp_normals[i0].x = dy;
2030 temp_normals[i0].y = -dx;
2031 }
2032
2033 for (int i0 = points_count - 1, i1 = 0; i1 < points_count; i0 = i1++)
2034 {
2035 // Average normals
2036 const ImVec2& n0 = temp_normals[i0];
2037 const ImVec2& n1 = temp_normals[i1];
2038 float dm_x = (n0.x + n1.x) * 0.5f;
2039 float dm_y = (n0.y + n1.y) * 0.5f;
2040 IM_FIXNORMAL2F(dm_x, dm_y);
2041 dm_x *= AA_SIZE * 0.5f;
2042 dm_y *= AA_SIZE * 0.5f;
2043
2044 // Add vertices
2045 _VtxWritePtr[0].pos.x = (points[i1].x - dm_x); _VtxWritePtr[0].pos.y = (points[i1].y - dm_y); _VtxWritePtr[0].uv = uv; _VtxWritePtr[0].col = col; // Inner
2046 _VtxWritePtr[1].pos.x = (points[i1].x + dm_x); _VtxWritePtr[1].pos.y = (points[i1].y + dm_y); _VtxWritePtr[1].uv = uv; _VtxWritePtr[1].col = col_trans; // Outer
2047 _VtxWritePtr += 2;
2048
2049 // Add indexes for fringes
2050 _IdxWritePtr[0] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_inner_idx + (i1 << 1)); _IdxWritePtr[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_inner_idx + (i0 << 1)); _IdxWritePtr[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_outer_idx + (i0 << 1));
2051 _IdxWritePtr[3] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_outer_idx + (i0 << 1)); _IdxWritePtr[4] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_outer_idx + (i1 << 1)); _IdxWritePtr[5] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_inner_idx + (i1 << 1));
2052 _IdxWritePtr += 6;
2053 }
2054 _VtxCurrentIdx += (ImDrawIdx)vtx_count;
2055 }
2056 else
2057 {
2058 // Non Anti-aliased Fill
2059 const int idx_count = (points_count - 2) * 3;
2060 const int vtx_count = points_count;
2061 PrimReserve(idx_count, vtx_count);
2062 for (int i = 0; i < vtx_count; i++)
2063 {
2064 _VtxWritePtr[0].pos = points[i]; _VtxWritePtr[0].uv = uv; _VtxWritePtr[0].col = col;
2065 _VtxWritePtr++;
2066 }
2067 _Data->TempBuffer.reserve_discard((ImTriangulator::EstimateScratchBufferSize(points_count) + sizeof(ImVec2)) / sizeof(ImVec2));
2068 triangulator.Init(points, points_count, _Data->TempBuffer.Data);
2069 while (triangulator._TrianglesLeft > 0)
2070 {
2071 triangulator.GetNextTriangle(triangle);
2072 _IdxWritePtr[0] = (ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx + triangle[0]); _IdxWritePtr[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx + triangle[1]); _IdxWritePtr[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx + triangle[2]);
2073 _IdxWritePtr += 3;
2074 }
2075 _VtxCurrentIdx += (ImDrawIdx)vtx_count;
2076 }
2077}
2078
2079//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
2080// [SECTION] ImDrawListSplitter
2081//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
2082// FIXME: This may be a little confusing, trying to be a little too low-level/optimal instead of just doing vector swap..
2083//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
2084
2085void ImDrawListSplitter::ClearFreeMemory()
2086{
2087 for (int i = 0; i < _Channels.Size; i++)
2088 {
2089 if (i == _Current)
2090 memset(&_Channels[i], 0, sizeof(_Channels[i])); // Current channel is a copy of CmdBuffer/IdxBuffer, don't destruct again
2091 _Channels[i]._CmdBuffer.clear();
2092 _Channels[i]._IdxBuffer.clear();
2093 }
2094 _Current = 0;
2095 _Count = 1;
2096 _Channels.clear();
2097}
2098
2099void ImDrawListSplitter::Split(ImDrawList* draw_list, int channels_count)
2100{
2101 IM_UNUSED(draw_list);
2102 IM_ASSERT(_Current == 0 && _Count <= 1 && "Nested channel splitting is not supported. Please use separate instances of ImDrawListSplitter.");
2103 int old_channels_count = _Channels.Size;
2104 if (old_channels_count < channels_count)
2105 {
2106 _Channels.reserve(channels_count); // Avoid over reserving since this is likely to stay stable
2107 _Channels.resize(channels_count);
2108 }
2109 _Count = channels_count;
2110
2111 // Channels[] (24/32 bytes each) hold storage that we'll swap with draw_list->_CmdBuffer/_IdxBuffer
2112 // The content of Channels[0] at this point doesn't matter. We clear it to make state tidy in a debugger but we don't strictly need to.
2113 // When we switch to the next channel, we'll copy draw_list->_CmdBuffer/_IdxBuffer into Channels[0] and then Channels[1] into draw_list->CmdBuffer/_IdxBuffer
2114 memset(&_Channels[0], 0, sizeof(ImDrawChannel));
2115 for (int i = 1; i < channels_count; i++)
2116 {
2117 if (i >= old_channels_count)
2118 {
2119 IM_PLACEMENT_NEW(&_Channels[i]) ImDrawChannel();
2120 }
2121 else
2122 {
2123 _Channels[i]._CmdBuffer.resize(0);
2124 _Channels[i]._IdxBuffer.resize(0);
2125 }
2126 }
2127}
2128
2129void ImDrawListSplitter::Merge(ImDrawList* draw_list)
2130{
2131 // Note that we never use or rely on _Channels.Size because it is merely a buffer that we never shrink back to 0 to keep all sub-buffers ready for use.
2132 if (_Count <= 1)
2133 return;
2134
2135 SetCurrentChannel(draw_list, 0);
2136 draw_list->_PopUnusedDrawCmd();
2137
2138 // Calculate our final buffer sizes. Also fix the incorrect IdxOffset values in each command.
2139 int new_cmd_buffer_count = 0;
2140 int new_idx_buffer_count = 0;
2141 ImDrawCmd* last_cmd = (_Count > 0 && draw_list->CmdBuffer.Size > 0) ? &draw_list->CmdBuffer.back() : NULL;
2142 int idx_offset = last_cmd ? last_cmd->IdxOffset + last_cmd->ElemCount : 0;
2143 for (int i = 1; i < _Count; i++)
2144 {
2145 ImDrawChannel& ch = _Channels[i];
2146 if (ch._CmdBuffer.Size > 0 && ch._CmdBuffer.back().ElemCount == 0 && ch._CmdBuffer.back().UserCallback == NULL) // Equivalent of PopUnusedDrawCmd()
2147 ch._CmdBuffer.pop_back();
2148
2149 if (ch._CmdBuffer.Size > 0 && last_cmd != NULL)
2150 {
2151 // Do not include ImDrawCmd_AreSequentialIdxOffset() in the compare as we rebuild IdxOffset values ourselves.
2152 // Manipulating IdxOffset (e.g. by reordering draw commands like done by RenderDimmedBackgroundBehindWindow()) is not supported within a splitter.
2153 ImDrawCmd* next_cmd = &ch._CmdBuffer[0];
2154 if (ImDrawCmd_HeaderCompare(last_cmd, next_cmd) == 0 && last_cmd->UserCallback == NULL && next_cmd->UserCallback == NULL)
2155 {
2156 // Merge previous channel last draw command with current channel first draw command if matching.
2157 last_cmd->ElemCount += next_cmd->ElemCount;
2158 idx_offset += next_cmd->ElemCount;
2159 ch._CmdBuffer.erase(ch._CmdBuffer.Data); // FIXME-OPT: Improve for multiple merges.
2160 }
2161 }
2162 if (ch._CmdBuffer.Size > 0)
2163 last_cmd = &ch._CmdBuffer.back();
2164 new_cmd_buffer_count += ch._CmdBuffer.Size;
2165 new_idx_buffer_count += ch._IdxBuffer.Size;
2166 for (int cmd_n = 0; cmd_n < ch._CmdBuffer.Size; cmd_n++)
2167 {
2168 ch._CmdBuffer.Data[cmd_n].IdxOffset = idx_offset;
2169 idx_offset += ch._CmdBuffer.Data[cmd_n].ElemCount;
2170 }
2171 }
2172 draw_list->CmdBuffer.resize(draw_list->CmdBuffer.Size + new_cmd_buffer_count);
2173 draw_list->IdxBuffer.resize(draw_list->IdxBuffer.Size + new_idx_buffer_count);
2174
2175 // Write commands and indices in order (they are fairly small structures, we don't copy vertices only indices)
2176 ImDrawCmd* cmd_write = draw_list->CmdBuffer.Data + draw_list->CmdBuffer.Size - new_cmd_buffer_count;
2177 ImDrawIdx* idx_write = draw_list->IdxBuffer.Data + draw_list->IdxBuffer.Size - new_idx_buffer_count;
2178 for (int i = 1; i < _Count; i++)
2179 {
2180 ImDrawChannel& ch = _Channels[i];
2181 if (int sz = ch._CmdBuffer.Size) { memcpy(cmd_write, ch._CmdBuffer.Data, sz * sizeof(ImDrawCmd)); cmd_write += sz; }
2182 if (int sz = ch._IdxBuffer.Size) { memcpy(idx_write, ch._IdxBuffer.Data, sz * sizeof(ImDrawIdx)); idx_write += sz; }
2183 }
2184 draw_list->_IdxWritePtr = idx_write;
2185
2186 // Ensure there's always a non-callback draw command trailing the command-buffer
2187 if (draw_list->CmdBuffer.Size == 0 || draw_list->CmdBuffer.back().UserCallback != NULL)
2188 draw_list->AddDrawCmd();
2189
2190 // If current command is used with different settings we need to add a new command
2191 ImDrawCmd* curr_cmd = &draw_list->CmdBuffer.Data[draw_list->CmdBuffer.Size - 1];
2192 if (curr_cmd->ElemCount == 0)
2193 ImDrawCmd_HeaderCopy(curr_cmd, &draw_list->_CmdHeader); // Copy ClipRect, TextureId, VtxOffset
2194 else if (ImDrawCmd_HeaderCompare(curr_cmd, &draw_list->_CmdHeader) != 0)
2195 draw_list->AddDrawCmd();
2196
2197 _Count = 1;
2198}
2199
2200void ImDrawListSplitter::SetCurrentChannel(ImDrawList* draw_list, int idx)
2201{
2202 IM_ASSERT(idx >= 0 && idx < _Count);
2203 if (_Current == idx)
2204 return;
2205
2206 // Overwrite ImVector (12/16 bytes), four times. This is merely a silly optimization instead of doing .swap()
2207 memcpy(&_Channels.Data[_Current]._CmdBuffer, &draw_list->CmdBuffer, sizeof(draw_list->CmdBuffer));
2208 memcpy(&_Channels.Data[_Current]._IdxBuffer, &draw_list->IdxBuffer, sizeof(draw_list->IdxBuffer));
2209 _Current = idx;
2210 memcpy(&draw_list->CmdBuffer, &_Channels.Data[idx]._CmdBuffer, sizeof(draw_list->CmdBuffer));
2211 memcpy(&draw_list->IdxBuffer, &_Channels.Data[idx]._IdxBuffer, sizeof(draw_list->IdxBuffer));
2212 draw_list->_IdxWritePtr = draw_list->IdxBuffer.Data + draw_list->IdxBuffer.Size;
2213
2214 // If current command is used with different settings we need to add a new command
2215 ImDrawCmd* curr_cmd = (draw_list->CmdBuffer.Size == 0) ? NULL : &draw_list->CmdBuffer.Data[draw_list->CmdBuffer.Size - 1];
2216 if (curr_cmd == NULL)
2217 draw_list->AddDrawCmd();
2218 else if (curr_cmd->ElemCount == 0)
2219 ImDrawCmd_HeaderCopy(curr_cmd, &draw_list->_CmdHeader); // Copy ClipRect, TextureId, VtxOffset
2220 else if (ImDrawCmd_HeaderCompare(curr_cmd, &draw_list->_CmdHeader) != 0)
2221 draw_list->AddDrawCmd();
2222}
2223
2224//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
2225// [SECTION] ImDrawData
2226//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
2227
2228void ImDrawData::Clear()
2229{
2230 Valid = false;
2231 CmdListsCount = TotalIdxCount = TotalVtxCount = 0;
2232 CmdLists.resize(0); // The ImDrawList are NOT owned by ImDrawData but e.g. by ImGuiContext, so we don't clear them.
2233 DisplayPos = DisplaySize = FramebufferScale = ImVec2(0.0f, 0.0f);
2234 OwnerViewport = NULL;
2235}
2236
2237// Important: 'out_list' is generally going to be draw_data->CmdLists, but may be another temporary list
2238// as long at it is expected that the result will be later merged into draw_data->CmdLists[].
2239void ImGui::AddDrawListToDrawDataEx(ImDrawData* draw_data, ImVector<ImDrawList*>* out_list, ImDrawList* draw_list)
2240{
2241 if (draw_list->CmdBuffer.Size == 0)
2242 return;
2243 if (draw_list->CmdBuffer.Size == 1 && draw_list->CmdBuffer[0].ElemCount == 0 && draw_list->CmdBuffer[0].UserCallback == NULL)
2244 return;
2245
2246 // Draw list sanity check. Detect mismatch between PrimReserve() calls and incrementing _VtxCurrentIdx, _VtxWritePtr etc.
2247 // May trigger for you if you are using PrimXXX functions incorrectly.
2248 IM_ASSERT(draw_list->VtxBuffer.Size == 0 || draw_list->_VtxWritePtr == draw_list->VtxBuffer.Data + draw_list->VtxBuffer.Size);
2249 IM_ASSERT(draw_list->IdxBuffer.Size == 0 || draw_list->_IdxWritePtr == draw_list->IdxBuffer.Data + draw_list->IdxBuffer.Size);
2250 if (!(draw_list->Flags & ImDrawListFlags_AllowVtxOffset))
2251 IM_ASSERT((int)draw_list->_VtxCurrentIdx == draw_list->VtxBuffer.Size);
2252
2253 // Check that draw_list doesn't use more vertices than indexable (default ImDrawIdx = unsigned short = 2 bytes = 64K vertices per ImDrawList = per window)
2254 // If this assert triggers because you are drawing lots of stuff manually:
2255 // - First, make sure you are coarse clipping yourself and not trying to draw many things outside visible bounds.
2256 // Be mindful that the lower-level ImDrawList API doesn't filter vertices. Use the Metrics/Debugger window to inspect draw list contents.
2257 // - If you want large meshes with more than 64K vertices, you can either:
2258 // (A) Handle the ImDrawCmd::VtxOffset value in your renderer backend, and set 'io.BackendFlags |= ImGuiBackendFlags_RendererHasVtxOffset'.
2259 // Most example backends already support this from 1.71. Pre-1.71 backends won't.
2260 // Some graphics API such as GL ES 1/2 don't have a way to offset the starting vertex so it is not supported for them.
2261 // (B) Or handle 32-bit indices in your renderer backend, and uncomment '#define ImDrawIdx unsigned int' line in imconfig.h.
2262 // Most example backends already support this. For example, the OpenGL example code detect index size at compile-time:
2263 // glDrawElements(GL_TRIANGLES, (GLsizei)pcmd->ElemCount, sizeof(ImDrawIdx) == 2 ? GL_UNSIGNED_SHORT : GL_UNSIGNED_INT, idx_buffer_offset);
2264 // Your own engine or render API may use different parameters or function calls to specify index sizes.
2265 // 2 and 4 bytes indices are generally supported by most graphics API.
2266 // - If for some reason neither of those solutions works for you, a workaround is to call BeginChild()/EndChild() before reaching
2267 // the 64K limit to split your draw commands in multiple draw lists.
2268 if (sizeof(ImDrawIdx) == 2)
2269 IM_ASSERT(draw_list->_VtxCurrentIdx < (1 << 16) && "Too many vertices in ImDrawList using 16-bit indices. Read comment above");
2270
2271 // Resolve callback data pointers
2272 if (draw_list->_CallbacksDataBuf.Size > 0)
2273 for (ImDrawCmd& cmd : draw_list->CmdBuffer)
2274 if (cmd.UserCallback != NULL && cmd.UserCallbackDataOffset != -1 && cmd.UserCallbackDataSize > 0)
2275 cmd.UserCallbackData = draw_list->_CallbacksDataBuf.Data + cmd.UserCallbackDataOffset;
2276
2277 // Add to output list + records state in ImDrawData
2278 out_list->push_back(draw_list);
2279 draw_data->CmdListsCount++;
2280 draw_data->TotalVtxCount += draw_list->VtxBuffer.Size;
2281 draw_data->TotalIdxCount += draw_list->IdxBuffer.Size;
2282}
2283
2284void ImDrawData::AddDrawList(ImDrawList* draw_list)
2285{
2286 IM_ASSERT(CmdLists.Size == CmdListsCount);
2287 draw_list->_PopUnusedDrawCmd();
2288 ImGui::AddDrawListToDrawDataEx(this, &CmdLists, draw_list);
2289}
2290
2291// For backward compatibility: convert all buffers from indexed to de-indexed, in case you cannot render indexed. Note: this is slow and most likely a waste of resources. Always prefer indexed rendering!
2292void ImDrawData::DeIndexAllBuffers()
2293{
2294 ImVector<ImDrawVert> new_vtx_buffer;
2295 TotalVtxCount = TotalIdxCount = 0;
2296 for (int i = 0; i < CmdListsCount; i++)
2297 {
2298 ImDrawList* cmd_list = CmdLists[i];
2299 if (cmd_list->IdxBuffer.empty())
2300 continue;
2301 new_vtx_buffer.resize(cmd_list->IdxBuffer.Size);
2302 for (int j = 0; j < cmd_list->IdxBuffer.Size; j++)
2303 new_vtx_buffer[j] = cmd_list->VtxBuffer[cmd_list->IdxBuffer[j]];
2304 cmd_list->VtxBuffer.swap(new_vtx_buffer);
2305 cmd_list->IdxBuffer.resize(0);
2306 TotalVtxCount += cmd_list->VtxBuffer.Size;
2307 }
2308}
2309
2310// Helper to scale the ClipRect field of each ImDrawCmd.
2311// Use if your final output buffer is at a different scale than draw_data->DisplaySize,
2312// or if there is a difference between your window resolution and framebuffer resolution.
2313void ImDrawData::ScaleClipRects(const ImVec2& fb_scale)
2314{
2315 for (ImDrawList* draw_list : CmdLists)
2316 for (ImDrawCmd& cmd : draw_list->CmdBuffer)
2317 cmd.ClipRect = ImVec4(cmd.ClipRect.x * fb_scale.x, cmd.ClipRect.y * fb_scale.y, cmd.ClipRect.z * fb_scale.x, cmd.ClipRect.w * fb_scale.y);
2318}
2319
2320//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
2321// [SECTION] Helpers ShadeVertsXXX functions
2322//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
2323
2324// Generic linear color gradient, write to RGB fields, leave A untouched.
2325void ImGui::ShadeVertsLinearColorGradientKeepAlpha(ImDrawList* draw_list, int vert_start_idx, int vert_end_idx, ImVec2 gradient_p0, ImVec2 gradient_p1, ImU32 col0, ImU32 col1)
2326{
2327 ImVec2 gradient_extent = gradient_p1 - gradient_p0;
2328 float gradient_inv_length2 = 1.0f / ImLengthSqr(gradient_extent);
2329 ImDrawVert* vert_start = draw_list->VtxBuffer.Data + vert_start_idx;
2330 ImDrawVert* vert_end = draw_list->VtxBuffer.Data + vert_end_idx;
2331 const int col0_r = (int)(col0 >> IM_COL32_R_SHIFT) & 0xFF;
2332 const int col0_g = (int)(col0 >> IM_COL32_G_SHIFT) & 0xFF;
2333 const int col0_b = (int)(col0 >> IM_COL32_B_SHIFT) & 0xFF;
2334 const int col_delta_r = ((int)(col1 >> IM_COL32_R_SHIFT) & 0xFF) - col0_r;
2335 const int col_delta_g = ((int)(col1 >> IM_COL32_G_SHIFT) & 0xFF) - col0_g;
2336 const int col_delta_b = ((int)(col1 >> IM_COL32_B_SHIFT) & 0xFF) - col0_b;
2337 for (ImDrawVert* vert = vert_start; vert < vert_end; vert++)
2338 {
2339 float d = ImDot(vert->pos - gradient_p0, gradient_extent);
2340 float t = ImClamp(d * gradient_inv_length2, 0.0f, 1.0f);
2341 int r = (int)(col0_r + col_delta_r * t);
2342 int g = (int)(col0_g + col_delta_g * t);
2343 int b = (int)(col0_b + col_delta_b * t);
2344 vert->col = (r << IM_COL32_R_SHIFT) | (g << IM_COL32_G_SHIFT) | (b << IM_COL32_B_SHIFT) | (vert->col & IM_COL32_A_MASK);
2345 }
2346}
2347
2348// Distribute UV over (a, b) rectangle
2349void ImGui::ShadeVertsLinearUV(ImDrawList* draw_list, int vert_start_idx, int vert_end_idx, const ImVec2& a, const ImVec2& b, const ImVec2& uv_a, const ImVec2& uv_b, bool clamp)
2350{
2351 const ImVec2 size = b - a;
2352 const ImVec2 uv_size = uv_b - uv_a;
2353 const ImVec2 scale = ImVec2(
2354 size.x != 0.0f ? (uv_size.x / size.x) : 0.0f,
2355 size.y != 0.0f ? (uv_size.y / size.y) : 0.0f);
2356
2357 ImDrawVert* vert_start = draw_list->VtxBuffer.Data + vert_start_idx;
2358 ImDrawVert* vert_end = draw_list->VtxBuffer.Data + vert_end_idx;
2359 if (clamp)
2360 {
2361 const ImVec2 min = ImMin(uv_a, uv_b);
2362 const ImVec2 max = ImMax(uv_a, uv_b);
2363 for (ImDrawVert* vertex = vert_start; vertex < vert_end; ++vertex)
2364 vertex->uv = ImClamp(uv_a + ImMul(ImVec2(vertex->pos.x, vertex->pos.y) - a, scale), min, max);
2365 }
2366 else
2367 {
2368 for (ImDrawVert* vertex = vert_start; vertex < vert_end; ++vertex)
2369 vertex->uv = uv_a + ImMul(ImVec2(vertex->pos.x, vertex->pos.y) - a, scale);
2370 }
2371}
2372
2373void ImGui::ShadeVertsTransformPos(ImDrawList* draw_list, int vert_start_idx, int vert_end_idx, const ImVec2& pivot_in, float cos_a, float sin_a, const ImVec2& pivot_out)
2374{
2375 ImDrawVert* vert_start = draw_list->VtxBuffer.Data + vert_start_idx;
2376 ImDrawVert* vert_end = draw_list->VtxBuffer.Data + vert_end_idx;
2377 for (ImDrawVert* vertex = vert_start; vertex < vert_end; ++vertex)
2378 vertex->pos = ImRotate(vertex->pos- pivot_in, cos_a, sin_a) + pivot_out;
2379}

2492ImFontAtlas::~ImFontAtlas()

2497
2498void ImFontAtlas::ClearInputData()
2499{
2500 IM_ASSERT(!Locked && "Cannot modify a locked ImFontAtlas between NewFrame() and EndFrame/Render()!");
2501 for (ImFontConfig& font_cfg : Sources)
2502 if (font_cfg.FontData && font_cfg.FontDataOwnedByAtlas)
2503 {
2504 IM_FREE(font_cfg.FontData);
2505 font_cfg.FontData = NULL;
2506 }
2507
2508 // When clearing this we lose access to the font name and other information used to build the font.
2509 for (ImFont* font : Fonts)
2510 if (font->Sources >= Sources.Data && font->Sources < Sources.Data + Sources.Size)
2511 {
2512 font->Sources = NULL;
2513 font->SourcesCount = 0;
2514 }
2515 Sources.clear();
2516 CustomRects.clear();
2517 PackIdMouseCursors = PackIdLines = -1;
2518 // Important: we leave TexReady untouched
2519}
2520
2521void ImFontAtlas::ClearTexData()
2522{
2523 IM_ASSERT(!Locked && "Cannot modify a locked ImFontAtlas between NewFrame() and EndFrame/Render()!");
2524 if (TexPixelsAlpha8)
2525 IM_FREE(TexPixelsAlpha8);
2526 if (TexPixelsRGBA32)
2527 IM_FREE(TexPixelsRGBA32);
2528 TexPixelsAlpha8 = NULL;
2529 TexPixelsRGBA32 = NULL;
2530 TexPixelsUseColors = false;
2531 // Important: we leave TexReady untouched
2532}
2533
2534void ImFontAtlas::ClearFonts()
2535{
2536 IM_ASSERT(!Locked && "Cannot modify a locked ImFontAtlas between NewFrame() and EndFrame/Render()!");
2537 ClearInputData();
2538 Fonts.clear_delete();
2539 TexReady = false;
2540}
2541
2542void ImFontAtlas::Clear()
2543{
2544 ClearInputData();
2545 ClearTexData();
2546 ClearFonts();
2547}
2548
2549void ImFontAtlas::GetTexDataAsAlpha8(unsigned char** out_pixels, int* out_width, int* out_height, int* out_bytes_per_pixel)
2550{
2551 // Build atlas on demand
2552 if (TexPixelsAlpha8 == NULL)
2553 Build();
2554
2555 *out_pixels = TexPixelsAlpha8;
2556 if (out_width) *out_width = TexWidth;
2557 if (out_height) *out_height = TexHeight;
2558 if (out_bytes_per_pixel) *out_bytes_per_pixel = 1;
2559}
2560
2561void ImFontAtlas::GetTexDataAsRGBA32(unsigned char** out_pixels, int* out_width, int* out_height, int* out_bytes_per_pixel)
2562{
2563 // Convert to RGBA32 format on demand
2564 // Although it is likely to be the most commonly used format, our font rendering is 1 channel / 8 bpp
2565 if (!TexPixelsRGBA32)
2566 {
2567 unsigned char* pixels = NULL;
2568 GetTexDataAsAlpha8(&pixels, NULL, NULL);
2569 if (pixels)
2570 {
2571 TexPixelsRGBA32 = (unsigned int*)IM_ALLOC((size_t)TexWidth * (size_t)TexHeight * 4);
2572 const unsigned char* src = pixels;
2573 unsigned int* dst = TexPixelsRGBA32;
2574 for (int n = TexWidth * TexHeight; n > 0; n--)
2575 *dst++ = IM_COL32(255, 255, 255, (unsigned int)(*src++));
2576 }
2577 }
2578
2579 *out_pixels = (unsigned char*)TexPixelsRGBA32;
2580 if (out_width) *out_width = TexWidth;
2581 if (out_height) *out_height = TexHeight;
2582 if (out_bytes_per_pixel) *out_bytes_per_pixel = 4;
2583}
2584
2585ImFont* ImFontAtlas::AddFont(const ImFontConfig* font_cfg)
2586{
2587 IM_ASSERT(!Locked && "Cannot modify a locked ImFontAtlas between NewFrame() and EndFrame/Render()!");
2588 IM_ASSERT(font_cfg->FontData != NULL && font_cfg->FontDataSize > 0);
2589 IM_ASSERT(font_cfg->SizePixels > 0.0f && "Is ImFontConfig struct correctly initialized?");
2590 IM_ASSERT(font_cfg->RasterizerDensity > 0.0f && "Is ImFontConfig struct correctly initialized?");
2591
2592 // Create new font
2593 if (!font_cfg->MergeMode)
2594 Fonts.push_back(IM_NEW(ImFont));
2595 else
2596 IM_ASSERT(Fonts.Size > 0 && "Cannot use MergeMode for the first font"); // When using MergeMode make sure that a font has already been added before. You can use ImGui::GetIO().Fonts->AddFontDefault() to add the default imgui font.
2597
2598 Sources.push_back(*font_cfg);
2599 ImFontConfig& new_font_cfg = Sources.back();
2600 if (new_font_cfg.DstFont == NULL)
2601 new_font_cfg.DstFont = Fonts.back();
2602 if (!new_font_cfg.FontDataOwnedByAtlas)
2603 {
2604 new_font_cfg.FontData = IM_ALLOC(new_font_cfg.FontDataSize);
2605 new_font_cfg.FontDataOwnedByAtlas = true;
2606 memcpy(new_font_cfg.FontData, font_cfg->FontData, (size_t)new_font_cfg.FontDataSize);
2607 }
2608
2609 // Round font size
2610 // - We started rounding in 1.90 WIP (18991) as our layout system currently doesn't support non-rounded font size well yet.
2611 // - Note that using io.FontGlobalScale or SetWindowFontScale(), with are legacy-ish, partially supported features, can still lead to unrounded sizes.
2612 // - We may support it better later and remove this rounding.
2613 new_font_cfg.SizePixels = ImTrunc(new_font_cfg.SizePixels);
2614
2615 // Pointers to Sources data are otherwise dangling
2616 ImFontAtlasUpdateSourcesPointers(this);
2617
2618 // Invalidate texture
2619 TexReady = false;
2620 ClearTexData();
2621 return new_font_cfg.DstFont;
2622}
2623
2624// Default font TTF is compressed with stb_compress then base85 encoded (see misc/fonts/binary_to_compressed_c.cpp for encoder)
2625static unsigned int stb_decompress_length(const unsigned char* input);
2626static unsigned int stb_decompress(unsigned char* output, const unsigned char* input, unsigned int length);
2627static unsigned int Decode85Byte(char c) { return c >= '\\' ? c-36 : c-35; }
2628static void Decode85(const unsigned char* src, unsigned char* dst)
2629{
2630 while (*src)
2631 {
2632 unsigned int tmp = Decode85Byte(src[0]) + 85 * (Decode85Byte(src[1]) + 85 * (Decode85Byte(src[2]) + 85 * (Decode85Byte(src[3]) + 85 * Decode85Byte(src[4]))));
2633 dst[0] = ((tmp >> 0) & 0xFF); dst[1] = ((tmp >> 8) & 0xFF); dst[2] = ((tmp >> 16) & 0xFF); dst[3] = ((tmp >> 24) & 0xFF); // We can't assume little-endianness.
2634 src += 5;
2635 dst += 4;
2636 }
2637}
2638#ifndef IMGUI_DISABLE_DEFAULT_FONT
2639static const char* GetDefaultCompressedFontDataTTF(int* out_size);
2640#endif
2641
2642// Load embedded ProggyClean.ttf at size 13, disable oversampling
2643ImFont* ImFontAtlas::AddFontDefault(const ImFontConfig* font_cfg_template)
2644{
2645#ifndef IMGUI_DISABLE_DEFAULT_FONT
2646 ImFontConfig font_cfg = font_cfg_template ? *font_cfg_template : ImFontConfig();
2647 if (!font_cfg_template)
2648 {
2649 font_cfg.OversampleH = font_cfg.OversampleV = 1;
2650 font_cfg.PixelSnapH = true;
2651 }
2652 if (font_cfg.SizePixels <= 0.0f)
2653 font_cfg.SizePixels = 13.0f * 1.0f;
2654 if (font_cfg.Name[0] == '\0')
2655 ImFormatString(font_cfg.Name, IM_ARRAYSIZE(font_cfg.Name), "ProggyClean.ttf, %dpx", (int)font_cfg.SizePixels);
2656 font_cfg.EllipsisChar = (ImWchar)0x0085;
2657 font_cfg.GlyphOffset.y = 1.0f * IM_TRUNC(font_cfg.SizePixels / 13.0f); // Add +1 offset per 13 units
2658
2659 int ttf_compressed_size = 0;
2660 const char* ttf_compressed = GetDefaultCompressedFontDataTTF(&ttf_compressed_size);
2661 const ImWchar* glyph_ranges = font_cfg.GlyphRanges != NULL ? font_cfg.GlyphRanges : GetGlyphRangesDefault();
2662 ImFont* font = AddFontFromMemoryCompressedTTF(ttf_compressed, ttf_compressed_size, font_cfg.SizePixels, &font_cfg, glyph_ranges);
2663 return font;
2664#else
2665 IM_ASSERT(0 && "AddFontDefault() disabled in this build.");
2666 IM_UNUSED(font_cfg_template);
2667 return NULL;
2668#endif // #ifndef IMGUI_DISABLE_DEFAULT_FONT
2669}
2670
2671ImFont* ImFontAtlas::AddFontFromFileTTF(const char* filename, float size_pixels, const ImFontConfig* font_cfg_template, const ImWchar* glyph_ranges)
2672{
2673 IM_ASSERT(!Locked && "Cannot modify a locked ImFontAtlas between NewFrame() and EndFrame/Render()!");
2674 size_t data_size = 0;
2675 void* data = ImFileLoadToMemory(filename, "rb", &data_size, 0);
2676 if (!data)
2677 {
2678 IM_ASSERT_USER_ERROR(0, "Could not load font file!");
2679 return NULL;
2680 }
2681 ImFontConfig font_cfg = font_cfg_template ? *font_cfg_template : ImFontConfig();
2682 if (font_cfg.Name[0] == '\0')
2683 {
2684 // Store a short copy of filename into into the font name for convenience
2685 const char* p;
2686 for (p = filename + ImStrlen(filename); p > filename && p[-1] != '/' && p[-1] != '\\'; p--) {}
2687 ImFormatString(font_cfg.Name, IM_ARRAYSIZE(font_cfg.Name), "%s, %.0fpx", p, size_pixels);
2688 }
2689 return AddFontFromMemoryTTF(data, (int)data_size, size_pixels, &font_cfg, glyph_ranges);
2690}
2691
2692// NB: Transfer ownership of 'ttf_data' to ImFontAtlas, unless font_cfg_template->FontDataOwnedByAtlas == false. Owned TTF buffer will be deleted after Build().
2693ImFont* ImFontAtlas::AddFontFromMemoryTTF(void* font_data, int font_data_size, float size_pixels, const ImFontConfig* font_cfg_template, const ImWchar* glyph_ranges)
2694{
2695 IM_ASSERT(!Locked && "Cannot modify a locked ImFontAtlas between NewFrame() and EndFrame/Render()!");
2696 ImFontConfig font_cfg = font_cfg_template ? *font_cfg_template : ImFontConfig();
2697 IM_ASSERT(font_cfg.FontData == NULL);
2698 IM_ASSERT(font_data_size > 100 && "Incorrect value for font_data_size!"); // Heuristic to prevent accidentally passing a wrong value to font_data_size.
2699 font_cfg.FontData = font_data;
2700 font_cfg.FontDataSize = font_data_size;
2701 font_cfg.SizePixels = size_pixels > 0.0f ? size_pixels : font_cfg.SizePixels;
2702 if (glyph_ranges)
2703 font_cfg.GlyphRanges = glyph_ranges;
2704 return AddFont(&font_cfg);
2705}
2706
2707ImFont* ImFontAtlas::AddFontFromMemoryCompressedTTF(const void* compressed_ttf_data, int compressed_ttf_size, float size_pixels, const ImFontConfig* font_cfg_template, const ImWchar* glyph_ranges)
2708{
2709 const unsigned int buf_decompressed_size = stb_decompress_length((const unsigned char*)compressed_ttf_data);
2710 unsigned char* buf_decompressed_data = (unsigned char*)IM_ALLOC(buf_decompressed_size);
2711 stb_decompress(buf_decompressed_data, (const unsigned char*)compressed_ttf_data, (unsigned int)compressed_ttf_size);
2712
2713 ImFontConfig font_cfg = font_cfg_template ? *font_cfg_template : ImFontConfig();
2714 IM_ASSERT(font_cfg.FontData == NULL);
2715 font_cfg.FontDataOwnedByAtlas = true;
2716 return AddFontFromMemoryTTF(buf_decompressed_data, (int)buf_decompressed_size, size_pixels, &font_cfg, glyph_ranges);
2717}
2718
2719ImFont* ImFontAtlas::AddFontFromMemoryCompressedBase85TTF(const char* compressed_ttf_data_base85, float size_pixels, const ImFontConfig* font_cfg, const ImWchar* glyph_ranges)
2720{
2721 int compressed_ttf_size = (((int)ImStrlen(compressed_ttf_data_base85) + 4) / 5) * 4;
2722 void* compressed_ttf = IM_ALLOC((size_t)compressed_ttf_size);
2723 Decode85((const unsigned char*)compressed_ttf_data_base85, (unsigned char*)compressed_ttf);
2724 ImFont* font = AddFontFromMemoryCompressedTTF(compressed_ttf, compressed_ttf_size, size_pixels, font_cfg, glyph_ranges);
2725 IM_FREE(compressed_ttf);
2726 return font;
2727}
2728
2729int ImFontAtlas::AddCustomRectRegular(int width, int height)
2730{
2731 IM_ASSERT(width > 0 && width <= 0xFFFF);
2732 IM_ASSERT(height > 0 && height <= 0xFFFF);
2733 ImFontAtlasCustomRect r;
2734 r.Width = (unsigned short)width;
2735 r.Height = (unsigned short)height;
2736 CustomRects.push_back(r);
2737 return CustomRects.Size - 1; // Return index
2738}
2739
2740int ImFontAtlas::AddCustomRectFontGlyph(ImFont* font, ImWchar id, int width, int height, float advance_x, const ImVec2& offset)
2741{
2742#ifdef IMGUI_USE_WCHAR32
2743 IM_ASSERT(id <= IM_UNICODE_CODEPOINT_MAX);
2744#endif
2745 IM_ASSERT(font != NULL);
2746 IM_ASSERT(width > 0 && width <= 0xFFFF);
2747 IM_ASSERT(height > 0 && height <= 0xFFFF);
2748 ImFontAtlasCustomRect r;
2749 r.Width = (unsigned short)width;
2750 r.Height = (unsigned short)height;
2751 r.GlyphID = id;
2752 r.GlyphColored = 0; // Set to 1 manually to mark glyph as colored // FIXME: No official API for that (#8133)
2753 r.GlyphAdvanceX = advance_x;
2754 r.GlyphOffset = offset;
2755 r.Font = font;
2756 CustomRects.push_back(r);
2757 return CustomRects.Size - 1; // Return index
2758}
2759
2760void ImFontAtlas::CalcCustomRectUV(const ImFontAtlasCustomRect* rect, ImVec2* out_uv_min, ImVec2* out_uv_max) const
2761{
2762 IM_ASSERT(TexWidth > 0 && TexHeight > 0); // Font atlas needs to be built before we can calculate UV coordinates
2763 IM_ASSERT(rect->IsPacked()); // Make sure the rectangle has been packed
2764 *out_uv_min = ImVec2((float)rect->X * TexUvScale.x, (float)rect->Y * TexUvScale.y);
2765 *out_uv_max = ImVec2((float)(rect->X + rect->Width) * TexUvScale.x, (float)(rect->Y + rect->Height) * TexUvScale.y);
2766}
2767
2768bool ImFontAtlasGetMouseCursorTexData(ImFontAtlas* atlas, ImGuiMouseCursor cursor_type, ImVec2* out_offset, ImVec2* out_size, ImVec2 out_uv_border[2], ImVec2 out_uv_fill[2])
2769{
2770 if (cursor_type <= ImGuiMouseCursor_None || cursor_type >= ImGuiMouseCursor_COUNT)
2771 return false;
2772 if (atlas->Flags & ImFontAtlasFlags_NoMouseCursors)
2773 return false;
2774
2775 IM_ASSERT(atlas->PackIdMouseCursors != -1);
2776 ImFontAtlasCustomRect* r = atlas->GetCustomRectByIndex(atlas->PackIdMouseCursors);
2777 ImVec2 pos = FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_CURSOR_DATA[cursor_type][0] + ImVec2((float)r->X, (float)r->Y);
2778 ImVec2 size = FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_CURSOR_DATA[cursor_type][1];
2779 *out_size = size;
2780 *out_offset = FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_CURSOR_DATA[cursor_type][2];
2781 out_uv_border[0] = (pos) * atlas->TexUvScale;
2782 out_uv_border[1] = (pos + size) * atlas->TexUvScale;
2783 pos.x += FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_W + 1;
2784 out_uv_fill[0] = (pos) * atlas->TexUvScale;
2785 out_uv_fill[1] = (pos + size) * atlas->TexUvScale;
2786 return true;
2787}
2788
2789bool ImFontAtlas::Build()
2790{
2791 IM_ASSERT(!Locked && "Cannot modify a locked ImFontAtlas between NewFrame() and EndFrame/Render()!");
2792
2793 // Default font is none are specified
2794 if (Sources.Size == 0)
2795 AddFontDefault();
2796
2797 // Select builder
2798 // - Note that we do not reassign to atlas->FontBuilderIO, since it is likely to point to static data which
2799 // may mess with some hot-reloading schemes. If you need to assign to this (for dynamic selection) AND are
2800 // using a hot-reloading scheme that messes up static data, store your own instance of ImFontBuilderIO somewhere
2801 // and point to it instead of pointing directly to return value of the GetBuilderXXX functions.
2802 const ImFontBuilderIO* builder_io = FontBuilderIO;
2803 if (builder_io == NULL)
2804 {
2805#ifdef IMGUI_ENABLE_FREETYPE
2806 builder_io = ImGuiFreeType::GetBuilderForFreeType();
2807#elif defined(IMGUI_ENABLE_STB_TRUETYPE)
2808 builder_io = ImFontAtlasGetBuilderForStbTruetype();
2809#else
2810 IM_ASSERT(0); // Invalid Build function
2811#endif
2812 }
2813
2814 // Build
2815 return builder_io->FontBuilder_Build(this);
2816}
2817
2818void ImFontAtlasBuildMultiplyCalcLookupTable(unsigned char out_table[256], float in_brighten_factor)
2819{
2820 for (unsigned int i = 0; i < 256; i++)
2821 {
2822 unsigned int value = (unsigned int)(i * in_brighten_factor);
2823 out_table[i] = value > 255 ? 255 : (value & 0xFF);
2824 }
2825}
2826
2827void ImFontAtlasBuildMultiplyRectAlpha8(const unsigned char table[256], unsigned char* pixels, int x, int y, int w, int h, int stride)
2828{
2829 IM_ASSERT_PARANOID(w <= stride);
2830 unsigned char* data = pixels + x + y * stride;
2831 for (int j = h; j > 0; j--, data += stride - w)
2832 for (int i = w; i > 0; i--, data++)
2833 *data = table[*data];
2834}
2835
2836void ImFontAtlasBuildGetOversampleFactors(const ImFontConfig* src, int* out_oversample_h, int* out_oversample_v)
2837{
2838 // Automatically disable horizontal oversampling over size 36
2839 *out_oversample_h = (src->OversampleH != 0) ? src->OversampleH : (src->SizePixels * src->RasterizerDensity > 36.0f || src->PixelSnapH) ? 1 : 2;
2840 *out_oversample_v = (src->OversampleV != 0) ? src->OversampleV : 1;
2841}
2842
2843#ifdef IMGUI_ENABLE_STB_TRUETYPE
2844// Temporary data for one source font (multiple source fonts can be merged into one destination ImFont)
2845// (C++03 doesn't allow instancing ImVector<> with function-local types so we declare the type here.)
2846struct ImFontBuildSrcData
2847{
2848 stbtt_fontinfo FontInfo;
2849 stbtt_pack_range PackRange; // Hold the list of codepoints to pack (essentially points to Codepoints.Data)
2850 stbrp_rect* Rects; // Rectangle to pack. We first fill in their size and the packer will give us their position.
2851 stbtt_packedchar* PackedChars; // Output glyphs
2852 const ImWchar* SrcRanges; // Ranges as requested by user (user is allowed to request too much, e.g. 0x0020..0xFFFF)
2853 int DstIndex; // Index into atlas->Fonts[] and dst_tmp_array[]
2854 int GlyphsHighest; // Highest requested codepoint
2855 int GlyphsCount; // Glyph count (excluding missing glyphs and glyphs already set by an earlier source font)
2856 ImBitVector GlyphsSet; // Glyph bit map (random access, 1-bit per codepoint. This will be a maximum of 8KB)
2857 ImVector<int> GlyphsList; // Glyph codepoints list (flattened version of GlyphsSet)
2858};
2859
2860// Temporary data for one destination ImFont* (multiple source fonts can be merged into one destination ImFont)
2861struct ImFontBuildDstData
2862{
2863 int SrcCount; // Number of source fonts targeting this destination font.
2864 int GlyphsHighest;
2865 int GlyphsCount;
2866 ImBitVector GlyphsSet; // This is used to resolve collision when multiple sources are merged into a same destination font.
2867};
2868
2869static void UnpackBitVectorToFlatIndexList(const ImBitVector* in, ImVector<int>* out)
2870{
2871 IM_ASSERT(sizeof(in->Storage.Data[0]) == sizeof(int));
2872 const ImU32* it_begin = in->Storage.begin();
2873 const ImU32* it_end = in->Storage.end();
2874 for (const ImU32* it = it_begin; it < it_end; it++)
2875 if (ImU32 entries_32 = *it)
2876 for (ImU32 bit_n = 0; bit_n < 32; bit_n++)
2877 if (entries_32 & ((ImU32)1 << bit_n))
2878 out->push_back((int)(((it - it_begin) << 5) + bit_n));
2879}
2880
2881static bool ImFontAtlasBuildWithStbTruetype(ImFontAtlas* atlas)
2882{
2883 IM_ASSERT(atlas->Sources.Size > 0);
2884
2885 ImFontAtlasBuildInit(atlas);
2886
2887 // Clear atlas
2888 atlas->TexID = (ImTextureID)NULL;
2889 atlas->TexWidth = atlas->TexHeight = 0;
2890 atlas->TexUvScale = ImVec2(0.0f, 0.0f);
2891 atlas->TexUvWhitePixel = ImVec2(0.0f, 0.0f);
2892 atlas->ClearTexData();
2893
2894 // Temporary storage for building
2895 ImVector<ImFontBuildSrcData> src_tmp_array;
2896 ImVector<ImFontBuildDstData> dst_tmp_array;
2897 src_tmp_array.resize(atlas->Sources.Size);
2898 dst_tmp_array.resize(atlas->Fonts.Size);
2899 memset(src_tmp_array.Data, 0, (size_t)src_tmp_array.size_in_bytes());
2900 memset(dst_tmp_array.Data, 0, (size_t)dst_tmp_array.size_in_bytes());
2901
2902 // 1. Initialize font loading structure, check font data validity
2903 for (int src_i = 0; src_i < atlas->Sources.Size; src_i++)
2904 {
2905 ImFontBuildSrcData& src_tmp = src_tmp_array[src_i];
2906 ImFontConfig& src = atlas->Sources[src_i];
2907 IM_ASSERT(src.DstFont && (!src.DstFont->IsLoaded() || src.DstFont->ContainerAtlas == atlas));
2908
2909 // Find index from src.DstFont (we allow the user to set cfg.DstFont. Also it makes casual debugging nicer than when storing indices)
2910 src_tmp.DstIndex = -1;
2911 for (int output_i = 0; output_i < atlas->Fonts.Size && src_tmp.DstIndex == -1; output_i++)
2912 if (src.DstFont == atlas->Fonts[output_i])
2913 src_tmp.DstIndex = output_i;
2914 if (src_tmp.DstIndex == -1)
2915 {
2916 IM_ASSERT(src_tmp.DstIndex != -1); // src.DstFont not pointing within atlas->Fonts[] array?
2917 return false;
2918 }
2919 // Initialize helper structure for font loading and verify that the TTF/OTF data is correct
2920 const int font_offset = stbtt_GetFontOffsetForIndex((unsigned char*)src.FontData, src.FontNo);
2921 IM_ASSERT(font_offset >= 0 && "FontData is incorrect, or FontNo cannot be found.");
2922 if (!stbtt_InitFont(&src_tmp.FontInfo, (unsigned char*)src.FontData, font_offset))
2923 {
2924 IM_ASSERT(0 && "stbtt_InitFont(): failed to parse FontData. It is correct and complete? Check FontDataSize.");
2925 return false;
2926 }
2927
2928 // Measure highest codepoints
2929 ImFontBuildDstData& dst_tmp = dst_tmp_array[src_tmp.DstIndex];
2930 src_tmp.SrcRanges = src.GlyphRanges ? src.GlyphRanges : atlas->GetGlyphRangesDefault();
2931 for (const ImWchar* src_range = src_tmp.SrcRanges; src_range[0] && src_range[1]; src_range += 2)
2932 {
2933 // Check for valid range. This may also help detect *some* dangling pointers, because a common
2934 // user error is to setup ImFontConfig::GlyphRanges with a pointer to data that isn't persistent,
2935 // or to forget to zero-terminate the glyph range array.
2936 IM_ASSERT(src_range[0] <= src_range[1] && "Invalid range: is your glyph range array persistent? it is zero-terminated?");
2937 src_tmp.GlyphsHighest = ImMax(src_tmp.GlyphsHighest, (int)src_range[1]);
2938 }
2939 dst_tmp.SrcCount++;
2940 dst_tmp.GlyphsHighest = ImMax(dst_tmp.GlyphsHighest, src_tmp.GlyphsHighest);
2941 }
2942
2943 // 2. For every requested codepoint, check for their presence in the font data, and handle redundancy or overlaps between source fonts to avoid unused glyphs.
2944 int total_glyphs_count = 0;
2945 for (int src_i = 0; src_i < src_tmp_array.Size; src_i++)
2946 {
2947 ImFontBuildSrcData& src_tmp = src_tmp_array[src_i];
2948 ImFontBuildDstData& dst_tmp = dst_tmp_array[src_tmp.DstIndex];
2949 src_tmp.GlyphsSet.Create(src_tmp.GlyphsHighest + 1);
2950 if (dst_tmp.GlyphsSet.Storage.empty())
2951 dst_tmp.GlyphsSet.Create(dst_tmp.GlyphsHighest + 1);
2952
2953 for (const ImWchar* src_range = src_tmp.SrcRanges; src_range[0] && src_range[1]; src_range += 2)
2954 for (unsigned int codepoint = src_range[0]; codepoint <= src_range[1]; codepoint++)
2955 {
2956 if (dst_tmp.GlyphsSet.TestBit(codepoint)) // Don't overwrite existing glyphs. We could make this an option for MergeMode (e.g. MergeOverwrite==true)
2957 continue;
2958 if (!stbtt_FindGlyphIndex(&src_tmp.FontInfo, codepoint)) // It is actually in the font?
2959 continue;
2960
2961 // Add to avail set/counters
2962 src_tmp.GlyphsCount++;
2963 dst_tmp.GlyphsCount++;
2964 src_tmp.GlyphsSet.SetBit(codepoint);
2965 dst_tmp.GlyphsSet.SetBit(codepoint);
2966 total_glyphs_count++;
2967 }
2968 }
2969
2970 // 3. Unpack our bit map into a flat list (we now have all the Unicode points that we know are requested _and_ available _and_ not overlapping another)
2971 for (int src_i = 0; src_i < src_tmp_array.Size; src_i++)
2972 {
2973 ImFontBuildSrcData& src_tmp = src_tmp_array[src_i];
2974 src_tmp.GlyphsList.reserve(src_tmp.GlyphsCount);
2975 UnpackBitVectorToFlatIndexList(&src_tmp.GlyphsSet, &src_tmp.GlyphsList);
2976 src_tmp.GlyphsSet.Clear();
2977 IM_ASSERT(src_tmp.GlyphsList.Size == src_tmp.GlyphsCount);
2978 }
2979 for (int dst_i = 0; dst_i < dst_tmp_array.Size; dst_i++)
2980 dst_tmp_array[dst_i].GlyphsSet.Clear();
2981 dst_tmp_array.clear();
2982
2983 // Allocate packing character data and flag packed characters buffer as non-packed (x0=y0=x1=y1=0)
2984 // (We technically don't need to zero-clear buf_rects, but let's do it for the sake of sanity)
2985 ImVector<stbrp_rect> buf_rects;
2986 ImVector<stbtt_packedchar> buf_packedchars;
2987 buf_rects.resize(total_glyphs_count);
2988 buf_packedchars.resize(total_glyphs_count);
2989 memset(buf_rects.Data, 0, (size_t)buf_rects.size_in_bytes());
2990 memset(buf_packedchars.Data, 0, (size_t)buf_packedchars.size_in_bytes());
2991
2992 // 4. Gather glyphs sizes so we can pack them in our virtual canvas.
2993 int total_surface = 0;
2994 int buf_rects_out_n = 0;
2995 int buf_packedchars_out_n = 0;
2996 const int pack_padding = atlas->TexGlyphPadding;
2997 for (int src_i = 0; src_i < src_tmp_array.Size; src_i++)
2998 {
2999 ImFontBuildSrcData& src_tmp = src_tmp_array[src_i];
3000 if (src_tmp.GlyphsCount == 0)
3001 continue;
3002
3003 src_tmp.Rects = &buf_rects[buf_rects_out_n];
3004 src_tmp.PackedChars = &buf_packedchars[buf_packedchars_out_n];
3005 buf_rects_out_n += src_tmp.GlyphsCount;
3006 buf_packedchars_out_n += src_tmp.GlyphsCount;
3007
3008 // Automatic selection of oversampling parameters
3009 ImFontConfig& src = atlas->Sources[src_i];
3010 int oversample_h, oversample_v;
3011 ImFontAtlasBuildGetOversampleFactors(&src, &oversample_h, &oversample_v);
3012
3013 // Convert our ranges in the format stb_truetype wants
3014 src_tmp.PackRange.font_size = src.SizePixels * src.RasterizerDensity;
3015 src_tmp.PackRange.first_unicode_codepoint_in_range = 0;
3016 src_tmp.PackRange.array_of_unicode_codepoints = src_tmp.GlyphsList.Data;
3017 src_tmp.PackRange.num_chars = src_tmp.GlyphsList.Size;
3018 src_tmp.PackRange.chardata_for_range = src_tmp.PackedChars;
3019 src_tmp.PackRange.h_oversample = (unsigned char)oversample_h;
3020 src_tmp.PackRange.v_oversample = (unsigned char)oversample_v;
3021
3022 // Gather the sizes of all rectangles we will need to pack (this loop is based on stbtt_PackFontRangesGatherRects)
3023 const float scale = (src.SizePixels > 0.0f) ? stbtt_ScaleForPixelHeight(&src_tmp.FontInfo, src.SizePixels * src.RasterizerDensity) : stbtt_ScaleForMappingEmToPixels(&src_tmp.FontInfo, -src.SizePixels * src.RasterizerDensity);
3024 for (int glyph_i = 0; glyph_i < src_tmp.GlyphsList.Size; glyph_i++)
3025 {
3026 int x0, y0, x1, y1;
3027 const int glyph_index_in_font = stbtt_FindGlyphIndex(&src_tmp.FontInfo, src_tmp.GlyphsList[glyph_i]);
3028 IM_ASSERT(glyph_index_in_font != 0);
3029 stbtt_GetGlyphBitmapBoxSubpixel(&src_tmp.FontInfo, glyph_index_in_font, scale * oversample_h, scale * oversample_v, 0, 0, &x0, &y0, &x1, &y1);
3030 src_tmp.Rects[glyph_i].w = (stbrp_coord)(x1 - x0 + pack_padding + oversample_h - 1);
3031 src_tmp.Rects[glyph_i].h = (stbrp_coord)(y1 - y0 + pack_padding + oversample_v - 1);
3032 total_surface += src_tmp.Rects[glyph_i].w * src_tmp.Rects[glyph_i].h;
3033 }
3034 }
3035 for (int i = 0; i < atlas->CustomRects.Size; i++)
3036 total_surface += (atlas->CustomRects[i].Width + pack_padding) * (atlas->CustomRects[i].Height + pack_padding);
3037
3038 // We need a width for the skyline algorithm, any width!
3039 // The exact width doesn't really matter much, but some API/GPU have texture size limitations and increasing width can decrease height.
3040 // User can override TexDesiredWidth and TexGlyphPadding if they wish, otherwise we use a simple heuristic to select the width based on expected surface.
3041 const int surface_sqrt = (int)ImSqrt((float)total_surface) + 1;
3042 atlas->TexHeight = 0;
3043 if (atlas->TexDesiredWidth > 0)
3044 atlas->TexWidth = atlas->TexDesiredWidth;
3045 else
3046 atlas->TexWidth = (surface_sqrt >= 4096 * 0.7f) ? 4096 : (surface_sqrt >= 2048 * 0.7f) ? 2048 : (surface_sqrt >= 1024 * 0.7f) ? 1024 : 512;
3047
3048 // 5. Start packing
3049 // Pack our extra data rectangles first, so it will be on the upper-left corner of our texture (UV will have small values).
3050 const int TEX_HEIGHT_MAX = 1024 * 32;
3051 stbtt_pack_context spc = {};
3052 stbtt_PackBegin(&spc, NULL, atlas->TexWidth, TEX_HEIGHT_MAX, 0, 0, NULL);
3053 spc.padding = atlas->TexGlyphPadding; // Because we mixup stbtt_PackXXX and stbrp_PackXXX there's a bit of a hack here, not passing the value to stbtt_PackBegin() allows us to still pack a TexWidth-1 wide item. (#8107)
3054 ImFontAtlasBuildPackCustomRects(atlas, spc.pack_info);
3055
3056 // 6. Pack each source font. No rendering yet, we are working with rectangles in an infinitely tall texture at this point.
3057 for (int src_i = 0; src_i < src_tmp_array.Size; src_i++)
3058 {
3059 ImFontBuildSrcData& src_tmp = src_tmp_array[src_i];
3060 if (src_tmp.GlyphsCount == 0)
3061 continue;
3062
3063 stbrp_pack_rects((stbrp_context*)spc.pack_info, src_tmp.Rects, src_tmp.GlyphsCount);
3064
3065 // Extend texture height and mark missing glyphs as non-packed so we won't render them.
3066 // FIXME: We are not handling packing failure here (would happen if we got off TEX_HEIGHT_MAX or if a single if larger than TexWidth?)
3067 for (int glyph_i = 0; glyph_i < src_tmp.GlyphsCount; glyph_i++)
3068 if (src_tmp.Rects[glyph_i].was_packed)
3069 atlas->TexHeight = ImMax(atlas->TexHeight, src_tmp.Rects[glyph_i].y + src_tmp.Rects[glyph_i].h);
3070 }
3071
3072 // 7. Allocate texture
3073 atlas->TexHeight = (atlas->Flags & ImFontAtlasFlags_NoPowerOfTwoHeight) ? (atlas->TexHeight + 1) : ImUpperPowerOfTwo(atlas->TexHeight);
3074 atlas->TexUvScale = ImVec2(1.0f / atlas->TexWidth, 1.0f / atlas->TexHeight);
3075 atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8 = (unsigned char*)IM_ALLOC(atlas->TexWidth * atlas->TexHeight);
3076 memset(atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8, 0, atlas->TexWidth * atlas->TexHeight);
3077 spc.pixels = atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8;
3078 spc.height = atlas->TexHeight;
3079
3080 // 8. Render/rasterize font characters into the texture
3081 for (int src_i = 0; src_i < src_tmp_array.Size; src_i++)
3082 {
3083 ImFontConfig& src = atlas->Sources[src_i];
3084 ImFontBuildSrcData& src_tmp = src_tmp_array[src_i];
3085 if (src_tmp.GlyphsCount == 0)
3086 continue;
3087
3088 stbtt_PackFontRangesRenderIntoRects(&spc, &src_tmp.FontInfo, &src_tmp.PackRange, 1, src_tmp.Rects);
3089
3090 // Apply multiply operator
3091 if (src.RasterizerMultiply != 1.0f)
3092 {
3093 unsigned char multiply_table[256];
3094 ImFontAtlasBuildMultiplyCalcLookupTable(multiply_table, src.RasterizerMultiply);
3095 stbrp_rect* r = &src_tmp.Rects[0];
3096 for (int glyph_i = 0; glyph_i < src_tmp.GlyphsCount; glyph_i++, r++)
3097 if (r->was_packed)
3098 ImFontAtlasBuildMultiplyRectAlpha8(multiply_table, atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8, r->x, r->y, r->w, r->h, atlas->TexWidth * 1);
3099 }
3100 src_tmp.Rects = NULL;
3101 }
3102
3103 // End packing
3104 stbtt_PackEnd(&spc);
3105 buf_rects.clear();
3106
3107 // 9. Setup ImFont and glyphs for runtime
3108 for (int src_i = 0; src_i < src_tmp_array.Size; src_i++)
3109 {
3110 // When merging fonts with MergeMode=true:
3111 // - We can have multiple input fonts writing into a same destination font.
3112 // - dst_font->Sources is != from src which is our source configuration.
3113 ImFontBuildSrcData& src_tmp = src_tmp_array[src_i];
3114 ImFontConfig& src = atlas->Sources[src_i];
3115 ImFont* dst_font = src.DstFont;
3116
3117 const float font_scale = stbtt_ScaleForPixelHeight(&src_tmp.FontInfo, src.SizePixels);
3118 int unscaled_ascent, unscaled_descent, unscaled_line_gap;
3119 stbtt_GetFontVMetrics(&src_tmp.FontInfo, &unscaled_ascent, &unscaled_descent, &unscaled_line_gap);
3120
3121 const float ascent = ImCeil(unscaled_ascent * font_scale);
3122 const float descent = ImFloor(unscaled_descent * font_scale);
3123 ImFontAtlasBuildSetupFont(atlas, dst_font, &src, ascent, descent);
3124 const float font_off_x = src.GlyphOffset.x;
3125 const float font_off_y = src.GlyphOffset.y + IM_ROUND(dst_font->Ascent);
3126
3127 const float inv_rasterization_scale = 1.0f / src.RasterizerDensity;
3128
3129 for (int glyph_i = 0; glyph_i < src_tmp.GlyphsCount; glyph_i++)
3130 {
3131 // Register glyph
3132 const int codepoint = src_tmp.GlyphsList[glyph_i];
3133 const stbtt_packedchar& pc = src_tmp.PackedChars[glyph_i];
3134 stbtt_aligned_quad q;
3135 float unused_x = 0.0f, unused_y = 0.0f;
3136 stbtt_GetPackedQuad(src_tmp.PackedChars, atlas->TexWidth, atlas->TexHeight, glyph_i, &unused_x, &unused_y, &q, 0);
3137 float x0 = q.x0 * inv_rasterization_scale + font_off_x;
3138 float y0 = q.y0 * inv_rasterization_scale + font_off_y;
3139 float x1 = q.x1 * inv_rasterization_scale + font_off_x;
3140 float y1 = q.y1 * inv_rasterization_scale + font_off_y;
3141 dst_font->AddGlyph(&src, (ImWchar)codepoint, x0, y0, x1, y1, q.s0, q.t0, q.s1, q.t1, pc.xadvance * inv_rasterization_scale);
3142 }
3143 }
3144
3145 // Cleanup
3146 src_tmp_array.clear_destruct();
3147
3148 ImFontAtlasBuildFinish(atlas);
3149 return true;
3150}
3151
3152const ImFontBuilderIO* ImFontAtlasGetBuilderForStbTruetype()
3153{
3154 static ImFontBuilderIO io;
3155 io.FontBuilder_Build = ImFontAtlasBuildWithStbTruetype;
3156 return &io;
3157}

3159#endif // IMGUI_ENABLE_STB_TRUETYPE
3160
3161void ImFontAtlasUpdateSourcesPointers(ImFontAtlas* atlas)
3162{
3163 for (ImFontConfig& src : atlas->Sources)
3164 {
3165 ImFont* font = src.DstFont;
3166 if (!src.MergeMode)
3167 {
3168 font->Sources = &src;
3169 font->SourcesCount = 0;
3170 }
3171 font->SourcesCount++;
3172 }
3173}
3174
3175void ImFontAtlasBuildSetupFont(ImFontAtlas* atlas, ImFont* font, ImFontConfig* font_config, float ascent, float descent)
3176{
3177 if (!font_config->MergeMode)
3178 {
3179 font->ClearOutputData();
3180 font->FontSize = font_config->SizePixels;
3181 IM_ASSERT(font->Sources == font_config);
3182 font->ContainerAtlas = atlas;
3183 font->Ascent = ascent;
3184 font->Descent = descent;
3185 }
3186}
3187
3188void ImFontAtlasBuildPackCustomRects(ImFontAtlas* atlas, void* stbrp_context_opaque)
3189{
3190 stbrp_context* pack_context = (stbrp_context*)stbrp_context_opaque;
3191 IM_ASSERT(pack_context != NULL);
3192
3193 ImVector<ImFontAtlasCustomRect>& user_rects = atlas->CustomRects;
3194 IM_ASSERT(user_rects.Size >= 1); // We expect at least the default custom rects to be registered, else something went wrong.
3195#ifdef __GNUC__
3196 if (user_rects.Size < 1) { __builtin_unreachable(); } // Workaround for GCC bug if IM_ASSERT() is defined to conditionally throw (see #5343)
3197#endif
3198
3199 const int pack_padding = atlas->TexGlyphPadding;
3200 ImVector<stbrp_rect> pack_rects;
3201 pack_rects.resize(user_rects.Size);
3202 memset(pack_rects.Data, 0, (size_t)pack_rects.size_in_bytes());
3203 for (int i = 0; i < user_rects.Size; i++)
3204 {
3205 pack_rects[i].w = user_rects[i].Width + pack_padding;
3206 pack_rects[i].h = user_rects[i].Height + pack_padding;
3207 }
3208 stbrp_pack_rects(pack_context, &pack_rects[0], pack_rects.Size);
3209 for (int i = 0; i < pack_rects.Size; i++)
3210 if (pack_rects[i].was_packed)
3211 {
3212 user_rects[i].X = (unsigned short)pack_rects[i].x;
3213 user_rects[i].Y = (unsigned short)pack_rects[i].y;
3214 IM_ASSERT(pack_rects[i].w == user_rects[i].Width + pack_padding && pack_rects[i].h == user_rects[i].Height + pack_padding);
3215 atlas->TexHeight = ImMax(atlas->TexHeight, pack_rects[i].y + pack_rects[i].h);
3216 }
3217}
3218
3219void ImFontAtlasBuildRender8bppRectFromString(ImFontAtlas* atlas, int x, int y, int w, int h, const char* in_str, char in_marker_char, unsigned char in_marker_pixel_value)
3220{
3221 IM_ASSERT(x >= 0 && x + w <= atlas->TexWidth);
3222 IM_ASSERT(y >= 0 && y + h <= atlas->TexHeight);
3223 unsigned char* out_pixel = atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8 + x + (y * atlas->TexWidth);
3224 for (int off_y = 0; off_y < h; off_y++, out_pixel += atlas->TexWidth, in_str += w)
3225 for (int off_x = 0; off_x < w; off_x++)
3226 out_pixel[off_x] = (in_str[off_x] == in_marker_char) ? in_marker_pixel_value : 0x00;
3227}
3228
3229void ImFontAtlasBuildRender32bppRectFromString(ImFontAtlas* atlas, int x, int y, int w, int h, const char* in_str, char in_marker_char, unsigned int in_marker_pixel_value)
3230{
3231 IM_ASSERT(x >= 0 && x + w <= atlas->TexWidth);
3232 IM_ASSERT(y >= 0 && y + h <= atlas->TexHeight);
3233 unsigned int* out_pixel = atlas->TexPixelsRGBA32 + x + (y * atlas->TexWidth);
3234 for (int off_y = 0; off_y < h; off_y++, out_pixel += atlas->TexWidth, in_str += w)
3235 for (int off_x = 0; off_x < w; off_x++)
3236 out_pixel[off_x] = (in_str[off_x] == in_marker_char) ? in_marker_pixel_value : IM_COL32_BLACK_TRANS;
3237}
3238
3239static void ImFontAtlasBuildRenderDefaultTexData(ImFontAtlas* atlas)
3240{
3241 ImFontAtlasCustomRect* r = atlas->GetCustomRectByIndex(atlas->PackIdMouseCursors);
3242 IM_ASSERT(r->IsPacked());
3243
3244 const int w = atlas->TexWidth;
3245 if (atlas->Flags & ImFontAtlasFlags_NoMouseCursors)
3246 {
3247 // White pixels only
3248 IM_ASSERT(r->Width == 2 && r->Height == 2);
3249 const int offset = (int)r->X + (int)r->Y * w;
3250 if (atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8 != NULL)
3251 {
3252 atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8[offset] = atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8[offset + 1] = atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8[offset + w] = atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8[offset + w + 1] = 0xFF;
3253 }
3254 else
3255 {
3256 atlas->TexPixelsRGBA32[offset] = atlas->TexPixelsRGBA32[offset + 1] = atlas->TexPixelsRGBA32[offset + w] = atlas->TexPixelsRGBA32[offset + w + 1] = IM_COL32_WHITE;
3257 }
3258 }
3259 else
3260 {
3261 // White pixels and mouse cursor
3262 IM_ASSERT(r->Width == FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_W * 2 + 1 && r->Height == FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_H);
3263 const int x_for_white = r->X;
3264 const int x_for_black = r->X + FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_W + 1;
3265 if (atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8 != NULL)
3266 {
3267 ImFontAtlasBuildRender8bppRectFromString(atlas, x_for_white, r->Y, FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_W, FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_H, FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_PIXELS, '.', 0xFF);
3268 ImFontAtlasBuildRender8bppRectFromString(atlas, x_for_black, r->Y, FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_W, FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_H, FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_PIXELS, 'X', 0xFF);
3269 }
3270 else
3271 {
3272 ImFontAtlasBuildRender32bppRectFromString(atlas, x_for_white, r->Y, FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_W, FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_H, FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_PIXELS, '.', IM_COL32_WHITE);
3273 ImFontAtlasBuildRender32bppRectFromString(atlas, x_for_black, r->Y, FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_W, FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_H, FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_PIXELS, 'X', IM_COL32_WHITE);
3274 }
3275 }
3276 atlas->TexUvWhitePixel = ImVec2((r->X + 0.5f) * atlas->TexUvScale.x, (r->Y + 0.5f) * atlas->TexUvScale.y);
3277}
3278
3279static void ImFontAtlasBuildRenderLinesTexData(ImFontAtlas* atlas)
3280{
3281 if (atlas->Flags & ImFontAtlasFlags_NoBakedLines)
3282 return;
3283
3284 // This generates a triangular shape in the texture, with the various line widths stacked on top of each other to allow interpolation between them
3285 ImFontAtlasCustomRect* r = atlas->GetCustomRectByIndex(atlas->PackIdLines);
3286 IM_ASSERT(r->IsPacked());
3287 for (int n = 0; n < IM_DRAWLIST_TEX_LINES_WIDTH_MAX + 1; n++) // +1 because of the zero-width row
3288 {
3289 // Each line consists of at least two empty pixels at the ends, with a line of solid pixels in the middle
3290 int y = n;
3291 int line_width = n;
3292 int pad_left = (r->Width - line_width) / 2;
3293 int pad_right = r->Width - (pad_left + line_width);
3294
3295 // Write each slice
3296 IM_ASSERT(pad_left + line_width + pad_right == r->Width && y < r->Height); // Make sure we're inside the texture bounds before we start writing pixels
3297 if (atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8 != NULL)
3298 {
3299 unsigned char* write_ptr = &atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8[r->X + ((r->Y + y) * atlas->TexWidth)];
3300 for (int i = 0; i < pad_left; i++)
3301 *(write_ptr + i) = 0x00;
3302
3303 for (int i = 0; i < line_width; i++)
3304 *(write_ptr + pad_left + i) = 0xFF;
3305
3306 for (int i = 0; i < pad_right; i++)
3307 *(write_ptr + pad_left + line_width + i) = 0x00;
3308 }
3309 else
3310 {
3311 unsigned int* write_ptr = &atlas->TexPixelsRGBA32[r->X + ((r->Y + y) * atlas->TexWidth)];
3312 for (int i = 0; i < pad_left; i++)
3313 *(write_ptr + i) = IM_COL32(255, 255, 255, 0);
3314
3315 for (int i = 0; i < line_width; i++)
3316 *(write_ptr + pad_left + i) = IM_COL32_WHITE;
3317
3318 for (int i = 0; i < pad_right; i++)
3319 *(write_ptr + pad_left + line_width + i) = IM_COL32(255, 255, 255, 0);
3320 }
3321
3322 // Calculate UVs for this line
3323 ImVec2 uv0 = ImVec2((float)(r->X + pad_left - 1), (float)(r->Y + y)) * atlas->TexUvScale;
3324 ImVec2 uv1 = ImVec2((float)(r->X + pad_left + line_width + 1), (float)(r->Y + y + 1)) * atlas->TexUvScale;
3325 float half_v = (uv0.y + uv1.y) * 0.5f; // Calculate a constant V in the middle of the row to avoid sampling artifacts
3326 atlas->TexUvLines[n] = ImVec4(uv0.x, half_v, uv1.x, half_v);
3327 }
3328}
3329
3330// Note: this is called / shared by both the stb_truetype and the FreeType builder
3331void ImFontAtlasBuildInit(ImFontAtlas* atlas)
3332{
3333 // Register texture region for mouse cursors or standard white pixels
3334 if (atlas->PackIdMouseCursors < 0)
3335 {
3336 if (!(atlas->Flags & ImFontAtlasFlags_NoMouseCursors))
3337 atlas->PackIdMouseCursors = atlas->AddCustomRectRegular(FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_W * 2 + 1, FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_H);
3338 else
3339 atlas->PackIdMouseCursors = atlas->AddCustomRectRegular(2, 2);
3340 }
3341
3342 // Register texture region for thick lines
3343 // The +2 here is to give space for the end caps, whilst height +1 is to accommodate the fact we have a zero-width row
3344 if (atlas->PackIdLines < 0)
3345 {
3346 if (!(atlas->Flags & ImFontAtlasFlags_NoBakedLines))
3347 atlas->PackIdLines = atlas->AddCustomRectRegular(IM_DRAWLIST_TEX_LINES_WIDTH_MAX + 2, IM_DRAWLIST_TEX_LINES_WIDTH_MAX + 1);
3348 }
3349}
3350
3351// This is called/shared by both the stb_truetype and the FreeType builder.
3352void ImFontAtlasBuildFinish(ImFontAtlas* atlas)
3353{
3354 // Render into our custom data blocks
3355 IM_ASSERT(atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8 != NULL || atlas->TexPixelsRGBA32 != NULL);
3356 ImFontAtlasBuildRenderDefaultTexData(atlas);
3357 ImFontAtlasBuildRenderLinesTexData(atlas);
3358
3359 // Register custom rectangle glyphs
3360 for (int i = 0; i < atlas->CustomRects.Size; i++)
3361 {
3362 const ImFontAtlasCustomRect* r = &atlas->CustomRects[i];
3363 if (r->Font == NULL || r->GlyphID == 0)
3364 continue;
3365
3366 // Will ignore ImFontConfig settings: GlyphMinAdvanceX, GlyphMinAdvanceY, PixelSnapH
3367 IM_ASSERT(r->Font->ContainerAtlas == atlas);
3368 ImVec2 uv0, uv1;
3369 atlas->CalcCustomRectUV(r, &uv0, &uv1);
3370 r->Font->AddGlyph(NULL, (ImWchar)r->GlyphID, r->GlyphOffset.x, r->GlyphOffset.y, r->GlyphOffset.x + r->Width, r->GlyphOffset.y + r->Height, uv0.x, uv0.y, uv1.x, uv1.y, r->GlyphAdvanceX);
3371 if (r->GlyphColored)
3372 r->Font->Glyphs.back().Colored = 1;
3373 }
3374
3375 // Build all fonts lookup tables
3376 for (ImFont* font : atlas->Fonts)
3377 if (font->DirtyLookupTables)
3378 font->BuildLookupTable();
3379
3380 atlas->TexReady = true;
3381}

3383//-------------------------------------------------------------------------
3384// [SECTION] ImFontAtlas: glyph ranges helpers
3385//-------------------------------------------------------------------------
3386// - GetGlyphRangesDefault()
3387// - GetGlyphRangesGreek()
3388// - GetGlyphRangesKorean()
3389// - GetGlyphRangesChineseFull()
3390// - GetGlyphRangesChineseSimplifiedCommon()
3391// - GetGlyphRangesJapanese()
3392// - GetGlyphRangesCyrillic()
3393// - GetGlyphRangesThai()
3394// - GetGlyphRangesVietnamese()
3395//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
3396
3397// Retrieve list of range (2 int per range, values are inclusive)
3398const ImWchar* ImFontAtlas::GetGlyphRangesDefault()
3399{
3400 static const ImWchar ranges[] =
3401 {
3402 0x0020, 0x00FF, // Basic Latin + Latin Supplement
3403 0,
3404 };
3405 return &ranges[0];
3406}
3407
3408const ImWchar* ImFontAtlas::GetGlyphRangesGreek()
3409{
3410 static const ImWchar ranges[] =
3411 {
3412 0x0020, 0x00FF, // Basic Latin + Latin Supplement
3413 0x0370, 0x03FF, // Greek and Coptic
3414 0,
3415 };
3416 return &ranges[0];
3417}
3418
3419const ImWchar* ImFontAtlas::GetGlyphRangesKorean()
3420{
3421 static const ImWchar ranges[] =
3422 {
3423 0x0020, 0x00FF, // Basic Latin + Latin Supplement
3424 0x3131, 0x3163, // Korean alphabets
3425 0xAC00, 0xD7A3, // Korean characters
3426 0xFFFD, 0xFFFD, // Invalid
3427 0,
3428 };
3429 return &ranges[0];
3430}
3431
3432const ImWchar* ImFontAtlas::GetGlyphRangesChineseFull()
3433{
3434 static const ImWchar ranges[] =
3435 {
3436 0x0020, 0x00FF, // Basic Latin + Latin Supplement
3437 0x2000, 0x206F, // General Punctuation
3438 0x3000, 0x30FF, // CJK Symbols and Punctuations, Hiragana, Katakana
3439 0x31F0, 0x31FF, // Katakana Phonetic Extensions
3440 0xFF00, 0xFFEF, // Half-width characters
3441 0xFFFD, 0xFFFD, // Invalid
3442 0x4e00, 0x9FAF, // CJK Ideograms
3443 0,
3444 };
3445 return &ranges[0];
3446}
3447
3448static void UnpackAccumulativeOffsetsIntoRanges(int base_codepoint, const short* accumulative_offsets, int accumulative_offsets_count, ImWchar* out_ranges)
3449{
3450 for (int n = 0; n < accumulative_offsets_count; n++, out_ranges += 2)
3451 {
3452 out_ranges[0] = out_ranges[1] = (ImWchar)(base_codepoint + accumulative_offsets[n]);
3453 base_codepoint += accumulative_offsets[n];
3454 }
3455 out_ranges[0] = 0;
3456}

3597 3,2,1,1,1,1,2,1,1,
3598 };
3599 static ImWchar base_ranges[] = // not zero-terminated
3600 {
3601 0x0020, 0x00FF, // Basic Latin + Latin Supplement
3602 0x3000, 0x30FF, // CJK Symbols and Punctuations, Hiragana, Katakana
3603 0x31F0, 0x31FF, // Katakana Phonetic Extensions
3604 0xFF00, 0xFFEF, // Half-width characters
3605 0xFFFD, 0xFFFD // Invalid
3606 };
3607 static ImWchar full_ranges[IM_ARRAYSIZE(base_ranges) + IM_ARRAYSIZE(accumulative_offsets_from_0x4E00)*2 + 1] = { 0 };
3608 if (!full_ranges[0])
3609 {
3610 memcpy(full_ranges, base_ranges, sizeof(base_ranges));
3611 UnpackAccumulativeOffsetsIntoRanges(0x4E00, accumulative_offsets_from_0x4E00, IM_ARRAYSIZE(accumulative_offsets_from_0x4E00), full_ranges + IM_ARRAYSIZE(base_ranges));
3612 }
3613 return &full_ranges[0];
3614}
