3657
3658//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
3659// [SECTION] ImFontGlyphRangesBuilder
3660//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
3661
3662void ImFontGlyphRangesBuilder::AddText(const char* text, const char* text_end)
3663{
3664 while (text_end ? (text < text_end) : *text)
3665 {
3666 unsigned int c = 0;
3667 int c_len = ImTextCharFromUtf8(&c, text, text_end);
3668 text += c_len;
3669 if (c_len == 0)
3670 break;
3671 AddChar((ImWchar)c);
3672 }
3673}
3674
3675void ImFontGlyphRangesBuilder::AddRanges(const ImWchar* ranges)
3676{
3677 for (; ranges[0]; ranges += 2)
3678 for (unsigned int c = ranges[0]; c <= ranges[1] && c <= IM_UNICODE_CODEPOINT_MAX; c++) //-V560
3679 AddChar((ImWchar)c);
3680}
3681
3682void ImFontGlyphRangesBuilder::BuildRanges(ImVector<ImWchar>* out_ranges)
3683{
3684 const int max_codepoint = IM_UNICODE_CODEPOINT_MAX;
3685 for (int n = 0; n <= max_codepoint; n++)
3686 if (GetBit(n))
3687 {
3688 out_ranges->push_back((ImWchar)n);
3689 while (n < max_codepoint && GetBit(n + 1))
3690 n++;
3691 out_ranges->push_back((ImWchar)n);
3692 }
3693 out_ranges->push_back(0);
3694}
3695
3696//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
3697// [SECTION] ImFont
3698//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
3699
3700ImFont::ImFont()
3701{
3702 memset(this, 0, sizeof(*this));
3703 Scale = 1.0f;
3704}
3705
3706ImFont::~ImFont()
3707{
3708 ClearOutputData();
3709}
3710
3711void ImFont::ClearOutputData()
3712{
3713 FontSize = 0.0f;
3714 FallbackAdvanceX = 0.0f;
3715 Glyphs.clear();
3716 IndexAdvanceX.clear();
3717 IndexLookup.clear();
3718 FallbackGlyph = NULL;
3719 ContainerAtlas = NULL;
3720 DirtyLookupTables = true;
3721 Ascent = Descent = 0.0f;
3722 MetricsTotalSurface = 0;
3723 memset(Used8kPagesMap, 0, sizeof(Used8kPagesMap));
3724}
3725
3726static ImWchar FindFirstExistingGlyph(ImFont* font, const ImWchar* candidate_chars, int candidate_chars_count)
3727{
3728 for (int n = 0; n < candidate_chars_count; n++)
3729 if (font->FindGlyphNoFallback(candidate_chars[n]) != NULL)
3730 return candidate_chars[n];
3731 return 0;
3732}
3733
3734void ImFont::BuildLookupTable()
3735{
3736 int max_codepoint = 0;
3737 for (int i = 0; i != Glyphs.Size; i++)
3738 max_codepoint = ImMax(max_codepoint, (int)Glyphs[i].Codepoint);
3739
3740 // Build lookup table
3741 IM_ASSERT(Glyphs.Size > 0 && "Font has not loaded glyph!");
3742 IM_ASSERT(Glyphs.Size < 0xFFFF); // -1 is reserved
3743 IndexAdvanceX.clear();
3744 IndexLookup.clear();
3745 DirtyLookupTables = false;
3746 memset(Used8kPagesMap, 0, sizeof(Used8kPagesMap));
3747 GrowIndex(max_codepoint + 1);
3748 for (int i = 0; i < Glyphs.Size; i++)
3749 {
3750 int codepoint = (int)Glyphs[i].Codepoint;
3751 IndexAdvanceX[codepoint] = Glyphs[i].AdvanceX;
3752 IndexLookup[codepoint] = (ImU16)i;
3753
3754 // Mark 4K page as used
3755 const int page_n = codepoint / 8192;
3756 Used8kPagesMap[page_n >> 3] |= 1 << (page_n & 7);
3757 }
3758
3759 // Create a glyph to handle TAB
3760 // FIXME: Needs proper TAB handling but it needs to be contextualized (or we could arbitrary say that each string starts at "column 0" ?)
3761 if (FindGlyph((ImWchar)' '))
3762 {
3763 if (Glyphs.back().Codepoint != '\t') // So we can call this function multiple times (FIXME: Flaky)
3764 Glyphs.resize(Glyphs.Size + 1);
3765 ImFontGlyph& tab_glyph = Glyphs.back();
3766 tab_glyph = *FindGlyph((ImWchar)' ');
3767 tab_glyph.Codepoint = '\t';
3768 tab_glyph.AdvanceX *= IM_TABSIZE;
3769 IndexAdvanceX[(int)tab_glyph.Codepoint] = (float)tab_glyph.AdvanceX;
3770 IndexLookup[(int)tab_glyph.Codepoint] = (ImU16)(Glyphs.Size - 1);
3771 }
3772
3773 // Mark special glyphs as not visible (note that AddGlyph already mark as non-visible glyphs with zero-size polygons)
3774 if (ImFontGlyph* glyph = (ImFontGlyph*)(void*)FindGlyph((ImWchar)' '))
3775 glyph->Visible = false;
3776 if (ImFontGlyph* glyph = (ImFontGlyph*)(void*)FindGlyph((ImWchar)'\t'))
3777 glyph->Visible = false;
3778
3779 // Setup Fallback character
3780 const ImWchar fallback_chars[] = { (ImWchar)IM_UNICODE_CODEPOINT_INVALID, (ImWchar)'?', (ImWchar)' ' };
3781 FallbackGlyph = FindGlyphNoFallback(FallbackChar);
3782 if (FallbackGlyph == NULL)
3783 {
3784 FallbackChar = FindFirstExistingGlyph(this, fallback_chars, IM_ARRAYSIZE(fallback_chars));
3785 FallbackGlyph = FindGlyphNoFallback(FallbackChar);
3786 if (FallbackGlyph == NULL)
3787 {
3788 FallbackGlyph = &Glyphs.back();
3789 FallbackChar = (ImWchar)FallbackGlyph->Codepoint;
3790 }
3791 }
3792 FallbackAdvanceX = FallbackGlyph->AdvanceX;
3793 for (int i = 0; i < max_codepoint + 1; i++)
3794 if (IndexAdvanceX[i] < 0.0f)
3795 IndexAdvanceX[i] = FallbackAdvanceX;
3796
3797 // Setup Ellipsis character. It is required for rendering elided text. We prefer using U+2026 (horizontal ellipsis).
3798 // However some old fonts may contain ellipsis at U+0085. Here we auto-detect most suitable ellipsis character.
3799 // FIXME: Note that 0x2026 is rarely included in our font ranges. Because of this we are more likely to use three individual dots.
3800 const ImWchar ellipsis_chars[] = { Sources->EllipsisChar, (ImWchar)0x2026, (ImWchar)0x0085 };
3801 const ImWchar dots_chars[] = { (ImWchar)'.', (ImWchar)0xFF0E };
3802 if (EllipsisChar == 0)
3803 EllipsisChar = FindFirstExistingGlyph(this, ellipsis_chars, IM_ARRAYSIZE(ellipsis_chars));
3804 const ImWchar dot_char = FindFirstExistingGlyph(this, dots_chars, IM_ARRAYSIZE(dots_chars));
3805 if (EllipsisChar != 0)
3806 {
3807 EllipsisCharCount = 1;
3808 EllipsisWidth = EllipsisCharStep = FindGlyph(EllipsisChar)->X1;
3809 }
3810 else if (dot_char != 0)
3811 {
3812 const ImFontGlyph* dot_glyph = FindGlyph(dot_char);
3813 EllipsisChar = dot_char;
3814 EllipsisCharCount = 3;
3815 EllipsisCharStep = (float)(int)(dot_glyph->X1 - dot_glyph->X0) + 1.0f;
3816 EllipsisWidth = ImMax(dot_glyph->AdvanceX, dot_glyph->X0 + EllipsisCharStep * 3.0f - 1.0f); // FIXME: Slightly odd for normally mono-space fonts but since this is used for trailing contents.
3817 }
3818}
3819
3820// API is designed this way to avoid exposing the 8K page size
3821// e.g. use with IsGlyphRangeUnused(0, 255)
3822bool ImFont::IsGlyphRangeUnused(unsigned int c_begin, unsigned int c_last)
3823{
3824 unsigned int page_begin = (c_begin / 8192);
3825 unsigned int page_last = (c_last / 8192);
3826 for (unsigned int page_n = page_begin; page_n <= page_last; page_n++)
3827 if ((page_n >> 3) < sizeof(Used8kPagesMap))
3828 if (Used8kPagesMap[page_n >> 3] & (1 << (page_n & 7)))
3829 return false;
3830 return true;
3831}
3832
3833void ImFont::GrowIndex(int new_size)
3834{
3835 IM_ASSERT(IndexAdvanceX.Size == IndexLookup.Size);
3836 if (new_size <= IndexLookup.Size)
3837 return;
3838 IndexAdvanceX.resize(new_size, -1.0f);
3839 IndexLookup.resize(new_size, (ImU16)-1);
3840}
3841
3842// x0/y0/x1/y1 are offset from the character upper-left layout position, in pixels. Therefore x0/y0 are often fairly close to zero.
3843// Not to be mistaken with texture coordinates, which are held by u0/v0/u1/v1 in normalized format (0.0..1.0 on each texture axis).
3844// 'src' is not necessarily == 'this->Sources' because multiple source fonts+configs can be used to build one target font.
3845void ImFont::AddGlyph(const ImFontConfig* src, ImWchar codepoint, float x0, float y0, float x1, float y1, float u0, float v0, float u1, float v1, float advance_x)
3846{
3847 if (src != NULL)
3848 {
3849 // Clamp & recenter if needed
3850 const float advance_x_original = advance_x;
3851 advance_x = ImClamp(advance_x, src->GlyphMinAdvanceX, src->GlyphMaxAdvanceX);
3852 if (advance_x != advance_x_original)
3853 {
3854 float char_off_x = src->PixelSnapH ? ImTrunc((advance_x - advance_x_original) * 0.5f) : (advance_x - advance_x_original) * 0.5f;
3855 x0 += char_off_x;
3856 x1 += char_off_x;
3857 }
3858
3859 // Snap to pixel
3860 if (src->PixelSnapH)
3861 advance_x = IM_ROUND(advance_x);
3862
3863 // Bake extra spacing
3864 advance_x += src->GlyphExtraAdvanceX;
3865 }
3866
3867 int glyph_idx = Glyphs.Size;
3868 Glyphs.resize(Glyphs.Size + 1);
3869 ImFontGlyph& glyph = Glyphs[glyph_idx];
3870 glyph.Codepoint = (unsigned int)codepoint;
3871 glyph.Visible = (x0 != x1) && (y0 != y1);
3872 glyph.Colored = false;
3873 glyph.X0 = x0;
3874 glyph.Y0 = y0;
3875 glyph.X1 = x1;
3876 glyph.Y1 = y1;
3877 glyph.U0 = u0;
3878 glyph.V0 = v0;
3879 glyph.U1 = u1;
3880 glyph.V1 = v1;
3881 glyph.AdvanceX = advance_x;
3882 IM_ASSERT(Glyphs.Size < 0xFFFF); // IndexLookup[] hold 16-bit values and -1 is reserved.
3883
3884 // Compute rough surface usage metrics (+1 to account for average padding, +0.99 to round)
3885 // We use (U1-U0)*TexWidth instead of X1-X0 to account for oversampling.
3886 float pad = ContainerAtlas->TexGlyphPadding + 0.99f;
3887 DirtyLookupTables = true;
3888 MetricsTotalSurface += (int)((glyph.U1 - glyph.U0) * ContainerAtlas->TexWidth + pad) * (int)((glyph.V1 - glyph.V0) * ContainerAtlas->TexHeight + pad);
3889}
3890
3891void ImFont::AddRemapChar(ImWchar dst, ImWchar src, bool overwrite_dst)
3892{
3893 IM_ASSERT(IndexLookup.Size > 0); // Currently this can only be called AFTER the font has been built, aka after calling ImFontAtlas::GetTexDataAs*() function.
3894 unsigned int index_size = (unsigned int)IndexLookup.Size;
3895
3896 if (dst < index_size && IndexLookup.Data[dst] == (ImU16)-1 && !overwrite_dst) // 'dst' already exists
3897 return;
3898 if (src >= index_size && dst >= index_size) // both 'dst' and 'src' don't exist -> no-op
3899 return;
3900
3901 GrowIndex(dst + 1);
3902 IndexLookup[dst] = (src < index_size) ? IndexLookup.Data[src] : (ImU16)-1;
3903 IndexAdvanceX[dst] = (src < index_size) ? IndexAdvanceX.Data[src] : 1.0f;
3904}
3905
3906// Find glyph, return fallback if missing
3907ImFontGlyph* ImFont::FindGlyph(ImWchar c)
3908{
3909 if (c >= (size_t)IndexLookup.Size)
3910 return FallbackGlyph;
3911 const ImU16 i = IndexLookup.Data[c];
3912 if (i == (ImU16)-1)
3913 return FallbackGlyph;
3914 return &Glyphs.Data[i];
3915}
3916
3917ImFontGlyph* ImFont::FindGlyphNoFallback(ImWchar c)
3918{
3919 if (c >= (size_t)IndexLookup.Size)
3920 return NULL;
3921 const ImU16 i = IndexLookup.Data[c];
3922 if (i == (ImU16)-1)
3923 return NULL;
3924 return &Glyphs.Data[i];
3925}
3926
3927// Trim trailing space and find beginning of next line
3928static inline const char* CalcWordWrapNextLineStartA(const char* text, const char* text_end)
3929{
3930 while (text < text_end && ImCharIsBlankA(*text))
3931 text++;
3932 if (*text == '\n')
3933 text++;
3934 return text;
3935}
3936
3937#define ImFontGetCharAdvanceX(_FONT, _CH) ((int)(_CH) < (_FONT)->IndexAdvanceX.Size ? (_FONT)->IndexAdvanceX.Data[_CH] : (_FONT)->FallbackAdvanceX)
3938
3939// Simple word-wrapping for English, not full-featured. Please submit failing cases!
3940// This will return the next location to wrap from. If no wrapping if necessary, this will fast-forward to e.g. text_end.
3941// FIXME: Much possible improvements (don't cut things like "word !", "word!!!" but cut within "word,,,,", more sensible support for punctuations, support for Unicode punctuations, etc.)
3942const char* ImFont::CalcWordWrapPositionA(float scale, const char* text, const char* text_end, float wrap_width)
3943{
3944 // For references, possible wrap point marked with ^
3945 // "aaa bbb, ccc,ddd. eee fff. ggg!"
3946 // ^ ^ ^ ^ ^__ ^ ^
3947
3948 // List of hardcoded separators: .,;!?'"
3949
3950 // Skip extra blanks after a line returns (that includes not counting them in width computation)
3951 // e.g. "Hello world" --> "Hello" "World"
3952
3953 // Cut words that cannot possibly fit within one line.
3954 // e.g.: "The tropical fish" with ~5 characters worth of width --> "The tr" "opical" "fish"
3955 float line_width = 0.0f;
3956 float word_width = 0.0f;
3957 float blank_width = 0.0f;
3958 wrap_width /= scale; // We work with unscaled widths to avoid scaling every characters
3959
3960 const char* word_end = text;
3961 const char* prev_word_end = NULL;
3962 bool inside_word = true;
3963
3964 const char* s = text;
3965 IM_ASSERT(text_end != NULL);
3966 while (s < text_end)
3967 {
3968 unsigned int c = (unsigned int)*s;
3969 const char* next_s;
3970 if (c < 0x80)
3971 next_s = s + 1;
3972 else
3973 next_s = s + ImTextCharFromUtf8(&c, s, text_end);
3974
3975 if (c < 32)
3976 {
3977 if (c == '\n')
3978 {
3979 line_width = word_width = blank_width = 0.0f;
3980 inside_word = true;
3981 s = next_s;
3982 continue;
3983 }
3984 if (c == '\r')
3985 {
3986 s = next_s;
3987 continue;
3988 }
3989 }
3990
3991 const float char_width = ImFontGetCharAdvanceX(this, c);
3992 if (ImCharIsBlankW(c))
3993 {
3994 if (inside_word)
3995 {
3996 line_width += blank_width;
3997 blank_width = 0.0f;
3998 word_end = s;
3999 }
4000 blank_width += char_width;
4001 inside_word = false;
4002 }
4003 else
4004 {
4005 word_width += char_width;
4006 if (inside_word)
4007 {
4008 word_end = next_s;
4009 }
4010 else
4011 {
4012 prev_word_end = word_end;
4013 line_width += word_width + blank_width;
4014 word_width = blank_width = 0.0f;
4015 }
4016
4017 // Allow wrapping after punctuation.
4018 inside_word = (c != '.' && c != ',' && c != ';' && c != '!' && c != '?' && c != '\"');
4019 }
4020
4021 // We ignore blank width at the end of the line (they can be skipped)
4022 if (line_width + word_width > wrap_width)
4023 {
4024 // Words that cannot possibly fit within an entire line will be cut anywhere.
4025 if (word_width < wrap_width)
4026 s = prev_word_end ? prev_word_end : word_end;
4027 break;
4028 }
4029
4030 s = next_s;
4031 }
4032
4033 // Wrap_width is too small to fit anything. Force displaying 1 character to minimize the height discontinuity.
4034 // +1 may not be a character start point in UTF-8 but it's ok because caller loops use (text >= word_wrap_eol).
4035 if (s == text && text < text_end)
4036 return s + 1;
4037 return s;
4038}
4039
4040ImVec2 ImFont::CalcTextSizeA(float size, float max_width, float wrap_width, const char* text_begin, const char* text_end, const char** remaining)
4041{
4042 if (!text_end)
4043 text_end = text_begin + ImStrlen(text_begin); // FIXME-OPT: Need to avoid this.
4044
4045 const float line_height = size;
4046 const float scale = size / FontSize;
4047
4048 ImVec2 text_size = ImVec2(0, 0);
4049 float line_width = 0.0f;
4050
4051 const bool word_wrap_enabled = (wrap_width > 0.0f);
4052 const char* word_wrap_eol = NULL;
4053
4054 const char* s = text_begin;
4055 while (s < text_end)
4056 {
4057 if (word_wrap_enabled)
4058 {
4059 // Calculate how far we can render. Requires two passes on the string data but keeps the code simple and not intrusive for what's essentially an uncommon feature.
4060 if (!word_wrap_eol)
4061 word_wrap_eol = CalcWordWrapPositionA(scale, s, text_end, wrap_width - line_width);
4062
4063 if (s >= word_wrap_eol)
4064 {
4065 if (text_size.x < line_width)
4066 text_size.x = line_width;
4067 text_size.y += line_height;
4068 line_width = 0.0f;
4069 word_wrap_eol = NULL;
4070 s = CalcWordWrapNextLineStartA(s, text_end); // Wrapping skips upcoming blanks
4071 continue;
4072 }
4073 }
4074
4075 // Decode and advance source
4076 const char* prev_s = s;
4077 unsigned int c = (unsigned int)*s;
4078 if (c < 0x80)
4079 s += 1;
4080 else
4081 s += ImTextCharFromUtf8(&c, s, text_end);
4082
4083 if (c < 32)
4084 {
4085 if (c == '\n')
4086 {
4087 text_size.x = ImMax(text_size.x, line_width);
4088 text_size.y += line_height;
4089 line_width = 0.0f;
4090 continue;
4091 }
4092 if (c == '\r')
4093 continue;
4094 }
4095
4096 const float char_width = ImFontGetCharAdvanceX(this, c) * scale;
4097 if (line_width + char_width >= max_width)
4098 {
4099 s = prev_s;
4100 break;
4101 }
4102
4103 line_width += char_width;
4104 }
4105
4106 if (text_size.x < line_width)
4107 text_size.x = line_width;
4108
4109 if (line_width > 0 || text_size.y == 0.0f)
4110 text_size.y += line_height;
4111
4112 if (remaining)
4113 *remaining = s;
4114
4115 return text_size;
4116}
4117
4118// Note: as with every ImDrawList drawing function, this expects that the font atlas texture is bound.
4119void ImFont::RenderChar(ImDrawList* draw_list, float size, const ImVec2& pos, ImU32 col, ImWchar c)
4120{
4121 const ImFontGlyph* glyph = FindGlyph(c);
4122 if (!glyph || !glyph->Visible)
4123 return;
4124 if (glyph->Colored)
4125 col |= ~IM_COL32_A_MASK;
4126 float scale = (size >= 0.0f) ? (size / FontSize) : 1.0f;
4127 float x = IM_TRUNC(pos.x);
4128 float y = IM_TRUNC(pos.y);
4129 draw_list->PrimReserve(6, 4);
4130 draw_list->PrimRectUV(ImVec2(x + glyph->X0 * scale, y + glyph->Y0 * scale), ImVec2(x + glyph->X1 * scale, y + glyph->Y1 * scale), ImVec2(glyph->U0, glyph->V0), ImVec2(glyph->U1, glyph->V1), col);
4131}
4132
4133// Note: as with every ImDrawList drawing function, this expects that the font atlas texture is bound.
4134void ImFont::RenderText(ImDrawList* draw_list, float size, const ImVec2& pos, ImU32 col, const ImVec4& clip_rect, const char* text_begin, const char* text_end, float wrap_width, bool cpu_fine_clip)
4135{
4136 // Align to be pixel perfect
4137 float x = IM_TRUNC(pos.x);
4138 float y = IM_TRUNC(pos.y);
4139 if (y > clip_rect.w)
4140 return;
4141
4142 if (!text_end)
4143 text_end = text_begin + ImStrlen(text_begin); // ImGui:: functions generally already provides a valid text_end, so this is merely to handle direct calls.
4144
4145 const float scale = size / FontSize;
4146 const float line_height = FontSize * scale;
4147 const float origin_x = x;
4148 const bool word_wrap_enabled = (wrap_width > 0.0f);
4149
4150 // Fast-forward to first visible line
4151 const char* s = text_begin;
4152 if (y + line_height < clip_rect.y)
4153 while (y + line_height < clip_rect.y && s < text_end)
4154 {
4155 const char* line_end = (const char*)ImMemchr(s, '\n', text_end - s);
4156 if (word_wrap_enabled)
4157 {
4158 // FIXME-OPT: This is not optimal as do first do a search for \n before calling CalcWordWrapPositionA().
4159 // If the specs for CalcWordWrapPositionA() were reworked to optionally return on \n we could combine both.
4160 // However it is still better than nothing performing the fast-forward!
4161 s = CalcWordWrapPositionA(scale, s, line_end ? line_end : text_end, wrap_width);
4162 s = CalcWordWrapNextLineStartA(s, text_end);
4163 }
4164 else
4165 {
4166 s = line_end ? line_end + 1 : text_end;
4167 }
4168 y += line_height;
4169 }
4170
4171 // For large text, scan for the last visible line in order to avoid over-reserving in the call to PrimReserve()
4172 // Note that very large horizontal line will still be affected by the issue (e.g. a one megabyte string buffer without a newline will likely crash atm)
4173 if (text_end - s > 10000 && !word_wrap_enabled)
4174 {
4175 const char* s_end = s;
4176 float y_end = y;
4177 while (y_end < clip_rect.w && s_end < text_end)
4178 {
4179 s_end = (const char*)ImMemchr(s_end, '\n', text_end - s_end);
4180 s_end = s_end ? s_end + 1 : text_end;
4181 y_end += line_height;
4182 }
4183 text_end = s_end;
4184 }
4185 if (s == text_end)
4186 return;
4187
4188 // Reserve vertices for remaining worse case (over-reserving is useful and easily amortized)
4189 const int vtx_count_max = (int)(text_end - s) * 4;
4190 const int idx_count_max = (int)(text_end - s) * 6;
4191 const int idx_expected_size = draw_list->IdxBuffer.Size + idx_count_max;
4192 draw_list->PrimReserve(idx_count_max, vtx_count_max);
4193 ImDrawVert* vtx_write = draw_list->_VtxWritePtr;
4194 ImDrawIdx* idx_write = draw_list->_IdxWritePtr;
4195 unsigned int vtx_index = draw_list->_VtxCurrentIdx;
4196
4197 const ImU32 col_untinted = col | ~IM_COL32_A_MASK;
4198 const char* word_wrap_eol = NULL;
4199
4200 while (s < text_end)
4201 {
4202 if (word_wrap_enabled)
4203 {
4204 // Calculate how far we can render. Requires two passes on the string data but keeps the code simple and not intrusive for what's essentially an uncommon feature.
4205 if (!word_wrap_eol)
4206 word_wrap_eol = CalcWordWrapPositionA(scale, s, text_end, wrap_width - (x - origin_x));
4207
4208 if (s >= word_wrap_eol)
4209 {
4210 x = origin_x;
4211 y += line_height;
4212 if (y > clip_rect.w)
4213 break; // break out of main loop
4214 word_wrap_eol = NULL;
4215 s = CalcWordWrapNextLineStartA(s, text_end); // Wrapping skips upcoming blanks
4216 continue;
4217 }
4218 }
4219
4220 // Decode and advance source
4221 unsigned int c = (unsigned int)*s;
4222 if (c < 0x80)
4223 s += 1;
4224 else
4225 s += ImTextCharFromUtf8(&c, s, text_end);
4226
4227 if (c < 32)
4228 {
4229 if (c == '\n')
4230 {
4231 x = origin_x;
4232 y += line_height;
4233 if (y > clip_rect.w)
4234 break; // break out of main loop
4235 continue;
4236 }
4237 if (c == '\r')
4238 continue;
4239 }
4240
4241 const ImFontGlyph* glyph = FindGlyph((ImWchar)c);
4242 if (glyph == NULL)
4243 continue;
4244
4245 float char_width = glyph->AdvanceX * scale;
4246 if (glyph->Visible)
4247 {
4248 // We don't do a second finer clipping test on the Y axis as we've already skipped anything before clip_rect.y and exit once we pass clip_rect.w
4249 float x1 = x + glyph->X0 * scale;
4250 float x2 = x + glyph->X1 * scale;
4251 float y1 = y + glyph->Y0 * scale;
4252 float y2 = y + glyph->Y1 * scale;
4253 if (x1 <= clip_rect.z && x2 >= clip_rect.x)
4254 {
4255 // Render a character
4256 float u1 = glyph->U0;
4257 float v1 = glyph->V0;
4258 float u2 = glyph->U1;
4259 float v2 = glyph->V1;
4260
4261 // CPU side clipping used to fit text in their frame when the frame is too small. Only does clipping for axis aligned quads.
4262 if (cpu_fine_clip)
4263 {
4264 if (x1 < clip_rect.x)
4265 {
4266 u1 = u1 + (1.0f - (x2 - clip_rect.x) / (x2 - x1)) * (u2 - u1);
4267 x1 = clip_rect.x;
4268 }
4269 if (y1 < clip_rect.y)
4270 {
4271 v1 = v1 + (1.0f - (y2 - clip_rect.y) / (y2 - y1)) * (v2 - v1);
4272 y1 = clip_rect.y;
4273 }
4274 if (x2 > clip_rect.z)
4275 {
4276 u2 = u1 + ((clip_rect.z - x1) / (x2 - x1)) * (u2 - u1);
4277 x2 = clip_rect.z;
4278 }
4279 if (y2 > clip_rect.w)
4280 {
4281 v2 = v1 + ((clip_rect.w - y1) / (y2 - y1)) * (v2 - v1);
4282 y2 = clip_rect.w;
4283 }
4284 if (y1 >= y2)
4285 {
4286 x += char_width;
4287 continue;
4288 }
4289 }
4290
4291 // Support for untinted glyphs
4292 ImU32 glyph_col = glyph->Colored ? col_untinted : col;
4293
4294 // We are NOT calling PrimRectUV() here because non-inlined causes too much overhead in a debug builds. Inlined here:
4295 {
4296 vtx_write[0].pos.x = x1; vtx_write[0].pos.y = y1; vtx_write[0].col = glyph_col; vtx_write[0].uv.x = u1; vtx_write[0].uv.y = v1;
4297 vtx_write[1].pos.x = x2; vtx_write[1].pos.y = y1; vtx_write[1].col = glyph_col; vtx_write[1].uv.x = u2; vtx_write[1].uv.y = v1;
4298 vtx_write[2].pos.x = x2; vtx_write[2].pos.y = y2; vtx_write[2].col = glyph_col; vtx_write[2].uv.x = u2; vtx_write[2].uv.y = v2;
4299 vtx_write[3].pos.x = x1; vtx_write[3].pos.y = y2; vtx_write[3].col = glyph_col; vtx_write[3].uv.x = u1; vtx_write[3].uv.y = v2;
4300 idx_write[0] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_index); idx_write[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_index + 1); idx_write[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_index + 2);
4301 idx_write[3] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_index); idx_write[4] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_index + 2); idx_write[5] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_index + 3);
4302 vtx_write += 4;
4303 vtx_index += 4;
4304 idx_write += 6;
4305 }
4306 }
4307 }
4308 x += char_width;
4309 }
4310
4311 // Give back unused vertices (clipped ones, blanks) ~ this is essentially a PrimUnreserve() action.
4312 draw_list->VtxBuffer.Size = (int)(vtx_write - draw_list->VtxBuffer.Data); // Same as calling shrink()
4313 draw_list->IdxBuffer.Size = (int)(idx_write - draw_list->IdxBuffer.Data);
4314 draw_list->CmdBuffer[draw_list->CmdBuffer.Size - 1].ElemCount -= (idx_expected_size - draw_list->IdxBuffer.Size);
4315 draw_list->_VtxWritePtr = vtx_write;
4316 draw_list->_IdxWritePtr = idx_write;
4317 draw_list->_VtxCurrentIdx = vtx_index;
4318}

4320//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
4321// [SECTION] ImGui Internal Render Helpers
4322//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
4323// Vaguely redesigned to stop accessing ImGui global state:
4324// - RenderArrow()
4325// - RenderBullet()
4326// - RenderCheckMark()
4327// - RenderArrowDockMenu()
4328// - RenderArrowPointingAt()
4329// - RenderRectFilledRangeH()
4330// - RenderRectFilledWithHole()
4331//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
4332// Function in need of a redesign (legacy mess)
4333// - RenderColorRectWithAlphaCheckerboard()
4334//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
4335
4336// Render an arrow aimed to be aligned with text (p_min is a position in the same space text would be positioned). To e.g. denote expanded/collapsed state
4337void ImGui::RenderArrow(ImDrawList* draw_list, ImVec2 pos, ImU32 col, ImGuiDir dir, float scale)
4338{
4339 const float h = draw_list->_Data->FontSize * 1.00f;
4340 float r = h * 0.40f * scale;
4341 ImVec2 center = pos + ImVec2(h * 0.50f, h * 0.50f * scale);
4342
4343 ImVec2 a, b, c;
4344 switch (dir)
4345 {
4346 case ImGuiDir_Up:
4347 case ImGuiDir_Down:
4348 if (dir == ImGuiDir_Up) r = -r;
4349 a = ImVec2(+0.000f, +0.750f) * r;
4350 b = ImVec2(-0.866f, -0.750f) * r;
4351 c = ImVec2(+0.866f, -0.750f) * r;
4352 break;
4353 case ImGuiDir_Left:
4354 case ImGuiDir_Right:
4355 if (dir == ImGuiDir_Left) r = -r;
4356 a = ImVec2(+0.750f, +0.000f) * r;
4357 b = ImVec2(-0.750f, +0.866f) * r;
4358 c = ImVec2(-0.750f, -0.866f) * r;
4359 break;
4360 case ImGuiDir_None:
4361 case ImGuiDir_COUNT:
4362 IM_ASSERT(0);
4363 break;
4364 }
4365 draw_list->AddTriangleFilled(center + a, center + b, center + c, col);
4366}
4367
4368void ImGui::RenderBullet(ImDrawList* draw_list, ImVec2 pos, ImU32 col)
4369{
4370 // FIXME-OPT: This should be baked in font.
4371 draw_list->AddCircleFilled(pos, draw_list->_Data->FontSize * 0.20f, col, 8);
4372}

4374void ImGui::RenderCheckMark(ImDrawList* draw_list, ImVec2 pos, ImU32 col, float sz)
4375{
4376 float thickness = ImMax(sz / 5.0f, 1.0f);
4377 sz -= thickness * 0.5f;
4378 pos += ImVec2(thickness * 0.25f, thickness * 0.25f);
4379
4380 float third = sz / 3.0f;
4381 float bx = pos.x + third;
4382 float by = pos.y + sz - third * 0.5f;
4383 draw_list->PathLineTo(ImVec2(bx - third, by - third));
4384 draw_list->PathLineTo(ImVec2(bx, by));
4385 draw_list->PathLineTo(ImVec2(bx + third * 2.0f, by - third * 2.0f));
4386 draw_list->PathStroke(col, 0, thickness);
4387}
4388
4389// Render an arrow. 'pos' is position of the arrow tip. half_sz.x is length from base to tip. half_sz.y is length on each side.
4390void ImGui::RenderArrowPointingAt(ImDrawList* draw_list, ImVec2 pos, ImVec2 half_sz, ImGuiDir direction, ImU32 col)
4391{
4392 switch (direction)
4393 {
4394 case ImGuiDir_Left: draw_list->AddTriangleFilled(ImVec2(pos.x + half_sz.x, pos.y - half_sz.y), ImVec2(pos.x + half_sz.x, pos.y + half_sz.y), pos, col); return;
4395 case ImGuiDir_Right: draw_list->AddTriangleFilled(ImVec2(pos.x - half_sz.x, pos.y + half_sz.y), ImVec2(pos.x - half_sz.x, pos.y - half_sz.y), pos, col); return;
4396 case ImGuiDir_Up: draw_list->AddTriangleFilled(ImVec2(pos.x + half_sz.x, pos.y + half_sz.y), ImVec2(pos.x - half_sz.x, pos.y + half_sz.y), pos, col); return;
4397 case ImGuiDir_Down: draw_list->AddTriangleFilled(ImVec2(pos.x - half_sz.x, pos.y - half_sz.y), ImVec2(pos.x + half_sz.x, pos.y - half_sz.y), pos, col); return;
4398 case ImGuiDir_None: case ImGuiDir_COUNT: break; // Fix warnings
4399 }
4400}

4402// This is less wide than RenderArrow() and we use in dock nodes instead of the regular RenderArrow() to denote a change of functionality,
4403// and because the saved space means that the left-most tab label can stay at exactly the same position as the label of a loose window.
4404void ImGui::RenderArrowDockMenu(ImDrawList* draw_list, ImVec2 p_min, float sz, ImU32 col)
4405{
4406 draw_list->AddRectFilled(p_min + ImVec2(sz * 0.20f, sz * 0.15f), p_min + ImVec2(sz * 0.80f, sz * 0.30f), col);
4407 RenderArrowPointingAt(draw_list, p_min + ImVec2(sz * 0.50f, sz * 0.85f), ImVec2(sz * 0.30f, sz * 0.40f), ImGuiDir_Down, col);
4408}
4409
4410static inline float ImAcos01(float x)
4411{
4412 if (x <= 0.0f) return IM_PI * 0.5f;
4413 if (x >= 1.0f) return 0.0f;
4414 return ImAcos(x);
4415 //return (-0.69813170079773212f * x * x - 0.87266462599716477f) * x + 1.5707963267948966f; // Cheap approximation, may be enough for what we do.
4416}
4417
4418// FIXME: Cleanup and move code to ImDrawList.
4419void ImGui::RenderRectFilledRangeH(ImDrawList* draw_list, const ImRect& rect, ImU32 col, float x_start_norm, float x_end_norm, float rounding)
4420{
4421 if (x_end_norm == x_start_norm)
4422 return;
4423 if (x_start_norm > x_end_norm)
4424 ImSwap(x_start_norm, x_end_norm);
4425
4426 ImVec2 p0 = ImVec2(ImLerp(rect.Min.x, rect.Max.x, x_start_norm), rect.Min.y);
4427 ImVec2 p1 = ImVec2(ImLerp(rect.Min.x, rect.Max.x, x_end_norm), rect.Max.y);
4428 if (rounding == 0.0f)
4429 {
4430 draw_list->AddRectFilled(p0, p1, col, 0.0f);
4431 return;
4432 }
4433
4434 rounding = ImClamp(ImMin((rect.Max.x - rect.Min.x) * 0.5f, (rect.Max.y - rect.Min.y) * 0.5f) - 1.0f, 0.0f, rounding);
4435 const float inv_rounding = 1.0f / rounding;
4436 const float arc0_b = ImAcos01(1.0f - (p0.x - rect.Min.x) * inv_rounding);
4437 const float arc0_e = ImAcos01(1.0f - (p1.x - rect.Min.x) * inv_rounding);
4438 const float half_pi = IM_PI * 0.5f; // We will == compare to this because we know this is the exact value ImAcos01 can return.
4439 const float x0 = ImMax(p0.x, rect.Min.x + rounding);
4440 if (arc0_b == arc0_e)
4441 {
4442 draw_list->PathLineTo(ImVec2(x0, p1.y));
4443 draw_list->PathLineTo(ImVec2(x0, p0.y));
4444 }
4445 else if (arc0_b == 0.0f && arc0_e == half_pi)
4446 {
4447 draw_list->PathArcToFast(ImVec2(x0, p1.y - rounding), rounding, 3, 6); // BL
4448 draw_list->PathArcToFast(ImVec2(x0, p0.y + rounding), rounding, 6, 9); // TR
4449 }
4450 else
4451 {
4452 draw_list->PathArcTo(ImVec2(x0, p1.y - rounding), rounding, IM_PI - arc0_e, IM_PI - arc0_b); // BL
4453 draw_list->PathArcTo(ImVec2(x0, p0.y + rounding), rounding, IM_PI + arc0_b, IM_PI + arc0_e); // TR
4454 }
4455 if (p1.x > rect.Min.x + rounding)
4456 {
4457 const float arc1_b = ImAcos01(1.0f - (rect.Max.x - p1.x) * inv_rounding);
4458 const float arc1_e = ImAcos01(1.0f - (rect.Max.x - p0.x) * inv_rounding);
4459 const float x1 = ImMin(p1.x, rect.Max.x - rounding);
4460 if (arc1_b == arc1_e)
4461 {
4462 draw_list->PathLineTo(ImVec2(x1, p0.y));
4463 draw_list->PathLineTo(ImVec2(x1, p1.y));
4464 }
4465 else if (arc1_b == 0.0f && arc1_e == half_pi)
4466 {
4467 draw_list->PathArcToFast(ImVec2(x1, p0.y + rounding), rounding, 9, 12); // TR
4468 draw_list->PathArcToFast(ImVec2(x1, p1.y - rounding), rounding, 0, 3); // BR
4469 }
4470 else
4471 {
4472 draw_list->PathArcTo(ImVec2(x1, p0.y + rounding), rounding, -arc1_e, -arc1_b); // TR
4473 draw_list->PathArcTo(ImVec2(x1, p1.y - rounding), rounding, +arc1_b, +arc1_e); // BR
4474 }
4475 }
4476 draw_list->PathFillConvex(col);
4477}
4478
4479void ImGui::RenderRectFilledWithHole(ImDrawList* draw_list, const ImRect& outer, const ImRect& inner, ImU32 col, float rounding)
4480{
4481 const bool fill_L = (inner.Min.x > outer.Min.x);
4482 const bool fill_R = (inner.Max.x < outer.Max.x);
4483 const bool fill_U = (inner.Min.y > outer.Min.y);
4484 const bool fill_D = (inner.Max.y < outer.Max.y);
4485 if (fill_L) draw_list->AddRectFilled(ImVec2(outer.Min.x, inner.Min.y), ImVec2(inner.Min.x, inner.Max.y), col, rounding, ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersNone | (fill_U ? 0 : ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopLeft) | (fill_D ? 0 : ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBottomLeft));
4486 if (fill_R) draw_list->AddRectFilled(ImVec2(inner.Max.x, inner.Min.y), ImVec2(outer.Max.x, inner.Max.y), col, rounding, ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersNone | (fill_U ? 0 : ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopRight) | (fill_D ? 0 : ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBottomRight));
4487 if (fill_U) draw_list->AddRectFilled(ImVec2(inner.Min.x, outer.Min.y), ImVec2(inner.Max.x, inner.Min.y), col, rounding, ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersNone | (fill_L ? 0 : ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopLeft) | (fill_R ? 0 : ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopRight));
4488 if (fill_D) draw_list->AddRectFilled(ImVec2(inner.Min.x, inner.Max.y), ImVec2(inner.Max.x, outer.Max.y), col, rounding, ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersNone | (fill_L ? 0 : ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBottomLeft) | (fill_R ? 0 : ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBottomRight));
4489 if (fill_L && fill_U) draw_list->AddRectFilled(ImVec2(outer.Min.x, outer.Min.y), ImVec2(inner.Min.x, inner.Min.y), col, rounding, ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopLeft);
4490 if (fill_R && fill_U) draw_list->AddRectFilled(ImVec2(inner.Max.x, outer.Min.y), ImVec2(outer.Max.x, inner.Min.y), col, rounding, ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopRight);
4491 if (fill_L && fill_D) draw_list->AddRectFilled(ImVec2(outer.Min.x, inner.Max.y), ImVec2(inner.Min.x, outer.Max.y), col, rounding, ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBottomLeft);
4492 if (fill_R && fill_D) draw_list->AddRectFilled(ImVec2(inner.Max.x, inner.Max.y), ImVec2(outer.Max.x, outer.Max.y), col, rounding, ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBottomRight);
4493}
4494
4495ImDrawFlags ImGui::CalcRoundingFlagsForRectInRect(const ImRect& r_in, const ImRect& r_outer, float threshold)
4496{
4497 bool round_l = r_in.Min.x <= r_outer.Min.x + threshold;
4498 bool round_r = r_in.Max.x >= r_outer.Max.x - threshold;
4499 bool round_t = r_in.Min.y <= r_outer.Min.y + threshold;
4500 bool round_b = r_in.Max.y >= r_outer.Max.y - threshold;
4501 return ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersNone
4502 | ((round_t && round_l) ? ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopLeft : 0) | ((round_t && round_r) ? ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopRight : 0)
4503 | ((round_b && round_l) ? ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBottomLeft : 0) | ((round_b && round_r) ? ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBottomRight : 0);
4504}
4505
4506// Helper for ColorPicker4()
4507// NB: This is rather brittle and will show artifact when rounding this enabled if rounded corners overlap multiple cells. Caller currently responsible for avoiding that.
4508// Spent a non reasonable amount of time trying to getting this right for ColorButton with rounding+anti-aliasing+ImGuiColorEditFlags_HalfAlphaPreview flag + various grid sizes and offsets, and eventually gave up... probably more reasonable to disable rounding altogether.
4509// FIXME: uses ImGui::GetColorU32
4510void ImGui::RenderColorRectWithAlphaCheckerboard(ImDrawList* draw_list, ImVec2 p_min, ImVec2 p_max, ImU32 col, float grid_step, ImVec2 grid_off, float rounding, ImDrawFlags flags)
4511{
4512 if ((flags & ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersMask_) == 0)
4513 flags = ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersDefault_;
4514 if (((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) >> IM_COL32_A_SHIFT) < 0xFF)
4515 {
4516 ImU32 col_bg1 = GetColorU32(ImAlphaBlendColors(IM_COL32(204, 204, 204, 255), col));
4517 ImU32 col_bg2 = GetColorU32(ImAlphaBlendColors(IM_COL32(128, 128, 128, 255), col));
4518 draw_list->AddRectFilled(p_min, p_max, col_bg1, rounding, flags);
4519
4520 int yi = 0;
4521 for (float y = p_min.y + grid_off.y; y < p_max.y; y += grid_step, yi++)
4522 {
4523 float y1 = ImClamp(y, p_min.y, p_max.y), y2 = ImMin(y + grid_step, p_max.y);
4524 if (y2 <= y1)
4525 continue;
4526 for (float x = p_min.x + grid_off.x + (yi & 1) * grid_step; x < p_max.x; x += grid_step * 2.0f)
4527 {
4528 float x1 = ImClamp(x, p_min.x, p_max.x), x2 = ImMin(x + grid_step, p_max.x);
4529 if (x2 <= x1)
4530 continue;
4531 ImDrawFlags cell_flags = ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersNone;
4532 if (y1 <= p_min.y) { if (x1 <= p_min.x) cell_flags |= ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopLeft; if (x2 >= p_max.x) cell_flags |= ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopRight; }
4533 if (y2 >= p_max.y) { if (x1 <= p_min.x) cell_flags |= ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBottomLeft; if (x2 >= p_max.x) cell_flags |= ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBottomRight; }
4534
4535 // Combine flags
4536 cell_flags = (flags == ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersNone || cell_flags == ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersNone) ? ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersNone : (cell_flags & flags);
4537 draw_list->AddRectFilled(ImVec2(x1, y1), ImVec2(x2, y2), col_bg2, rounding, cell_flags);
4538 }
4539 }
4540 }
4541 else
4542 {
4543 draw_list->AddRectFilled(p_min, p_max, col, rounding, flags);
4544 }
4545}
4546
4547//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
4548// [SECTION] Decompression code
4549//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
4550// Compressed with stb_compress() then converted to a C array and encoded as base85.
4551// Use the program in misc/fonts/binary_to_compressed_c.cpp to create the array from a TTF file.
4552// The purpose of encoding as base85 instead of "0x00,0x01,..." style is only save on _source code_ size.
4553// Decompression from stb.h (public domain) by Sean Barrett https://github.com/nothings/stb/blob/master/stb.h
4554//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
4555
4556static unsigned int stb_decompress_length(const unsigned char *input)
4557{
4558 return (input[8] << 24) + (input[9] << 16) + (input[10] << 8) + input[11];
4559}
4560
4561static unsigned char *stb__barrier_out_e, *stb__barrier_out_b;
4562static const unsigned char *stb__barrier_in_b;
4563static unsigned char *stb__dout;
4564static void stb__match(const unsigned char *data, unsigned int length)
4565{
4566 // INVERSE of memmove... write each byte before copying the next...
4567 IM_ASSERT(stb__dout + length <= stb__barrier_out_e);
4568 if (stb__dout + length > stb__barrier_out_e) { stb__dout += length; return; }
4569 if (data < stb__barrier_out_b) { stb__dout = stb__barrier_out_e+1; return; }
4570 while (length--) *stb__dout++ = *data++;
4571}
4572
4573static void stb__lit(const unsigned char *data, unsigned int length)
4574{
4575 IM_ASSERT(stb__dout + length <= stb__barrier_out_e);
4576 if (stb__dout + length > stb__barrier_out_e) { stb__dout += length; return; }
4577 if (data < stb__barrier_in_b) { stb__dout = stb__barrier_out_e+1; return; }
4578 memcpy(stb__dout, data, length);
4579 stb__dout += length;
4580}
4581
4582#define stb__in2(x) ((i[x] << 8) + i[(x)+1])
4583#define stb__in3(x) ((i[x] << 16) + stb__in2((x)+1))
4584#define stb__in4(x) ((i[x] << 24) + stb__in3((x)+1))
4585
4586static const unsigned char *stb_decompress_token(const unsigned char *i)
4587{
4588 if (*i >= 0x20) { // use fewer if's for cases that expand small
4589 if (*i >= 0x80) stb__match(stb__dout-i[1]-1, i[0] - 0x80 + 1), i += 2;
4590 else if (*i >= 0x40) stb__match(stb__dout-(stb__in2(0) - 0x4000 + 1), i[2]+1), i += 3;
4591 else /* *i >= 0x20 */ stb__lit(i+1, i[0] - 0x20 + 1), i += 1 + (i[0] - 0x20 + 1);
4592 } else { // more ifs for cases that expand large, since overhead is amortized
4593 if (*i >= 0x18) stb__match(stb__dout-(stb__in3(0) - 0x180000 + 1), i[3]+1), i += 4;
4594 else if (*i >= 0x10) stb__match(stb__dout-(stb__in3(0) - 0x100000 + 1), stb__in2(3)+1), i += 5;
4595 else if (*i >= 0x08) stb__lit(i+2, stb__in2(0) - 0x0800 + 1), i += 2 + (stb__in2(0) - 0x0800 + 1);
4596 else if (*i == 0x07) stb__lit(i+3, stb__in2(1) + 1), i += 3 + (stb__in2(1) + 1);
4597 else if (*i == 0x06) stb__match(stb__dout-(stb__in3(1)+1), i[4]+1), i += 5;
4598 else if (*i == 0x04) stb__match(stb__dout-(stb__in3(1)+1), stb__in2(4)+1), i += 6;
4599 }
4600 return i;
4601}
4602
4603static unsigned int stb_adler32(unsigned int adler32, unsigned char *buffer, unsigned int buflen)
4604{
4605 const unsigned long ADLER_MOD = 65521;
4606 unsigned long s1 = adler32 & 0xffff, s2 = adler32 >> 16;
4607 unsigned long blocklen = buflen % 5552;
4608
4609 unsigned long i;
4610 while (buflen) {
4611 for (i=0; i + 7 < blocklen; i += 8) {
4612 s1 += buffer[0], s2 += s1;
4613 s1 += buffer[1], s2 += s1;
4614 s1 += buffer[2], s2 += s1;
4615 s1 += buffer[3], s2 += s1;
4616 s1 += buffer[4], s2 += s1;
4617 s1 += buffer[5], s2 += s1;
4618 s1 += buffer[6], s2 += s1;
4619 s1 += buffer[7], s2 += s1;
4620
4621 buffer += 8;
4622 }
4623
4624 for (; i < blocklen; ++i)
4625 s1 += *buffer++, s2 += s1;
4626
4627 s1 %= ADLER_MOD, s2 %= ADLER_MOD;
4628 buflen -= blocklen;
4629 blocklen = 5552;
4630 }
4631 return (unsigned int)(s2 << 16) + (unsigned int)s1;
4632}
4633
4634static unsigned int stb_decompress(unsigned char *output, const unsigned char *i, unsigned int /*length*/)
4635{
4636 if (stb__in4(0) != 0x57bC0000) return 0;
4637 if (stb__in4(4) != 0) return 0; // error! stream is > 4GB
4638 const unsigned int olen = stb_decompress_length(i);
4639 stb__barrier_in_b = i;
4640 stb__barrier_out_e = output + olen;
4641 stb__barrier_out_b = output;
4642 i += 16;
4643
4644 stb__dout = output;
4645 for (;;) {
4646 const unsigned char *old_i = i;
4647 i = stb_decompress_token(i);
4648 if (i == old_i) {
4649 if (*i == 0x05 && i[1] == 0xfa) {
4650 IM_ASSERT(stb__dout == output + olen);
4651 if (stb__dout != output + olen) return 0;
4652 if (stb_adler32(1, output, olen) != (unsigned int) stb__in4(2))
4653 return 0;
4654 return olen;
4655 } else {
4656 IM_ASSERT(0); /* NOTREACHED */
4657 return 0;
4658 }
4659 }
4660 IM_ASSERT(stb__dout <= output + olen);
4661 if (stb__dout > output + olen)
4662 return 0;
4663 }
4664}
